# Wiki Index

The catalog of all pages in this wiki. Each entry: a wikilink to the page and a one-line summary. The LLM reads this first when answering queries to identify candidate pages.

Keep summaries tight ‚Äî one line each. The index is engineered to be cheap to read; a fat index defeats its purpose.

When this file exceeds ~300 lines or the wiki passes ~150 pages, shard into `wiki/indexes/<type>.md` and replace this file with a directory of shards. See the `scaling-playbook.md` reference in the `llm-wiki` skill for the migration procedure.

---

- [[mcp-plan]] ‚Äî the SUPERSEDED (2026-07-01) MCP design doc (sibling of the checklist): v3‚Üív4 rationale, full 241-tool inventory across 12 servers, and the still-valid standards (naming, JSON-Schema 2020-12, error ranges, SemVer, 2-tests-per-tool, doc contract).
- [[mcp-prompt]] ‚Äî the CURRENT one-tool-per-session MCP-completion subagent prompt: names the real 11 servers (server‚Üíproject‚Üífile), the 3-part tool DoD (binding+tests+docs), and reverses the old no-business-asserts test policy. Ground truth: `docs/mcp/MCP_STATUS.md`.

- [[findings-register]] ‚Äî the validation-campaign disposition ledger: every note across all 86 per-unit reports triaged into fixed-now / feasible / not-possible / by-design; green-washing detection; a 2026-06-12 snapshot superseded by the 2026-06-24 re-validation reset.

- [[validation-protocol]] ‚Äî the validation *methodology* (VALIDATION_PROTOCOL.md): one fresh session per unit in a context separate from the implementer's, Stage A (validate the description vs external primary sources) before Stage B (validate the code), ending in exactly one of ‚úÖ CLEAN / üîß LIMITED; the per-session prompt, checklists, verdict legend, and report template the ledger operationalizes.

- [[chrom-aneu-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-ANEU-001 (aneuploidy detection): first Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Aneuploidy/CNV + Griffiths + Santaguida-Amon + McCarroll-Altshuler sources; log2 depth-ratio ‚Üí CN=round(2^logRatio√ó2) clamped [0,10], ‚â•80%-bin whole-chromosome call, confidence=1‚àímin(1,|CN/2‚àí2^logRatio|); Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosome + partial-aneuploidy limitations.

- [[chrom-synt-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-SYNT-001 (synteny analysis): fourth Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Synteny/Comparative-genomics/Rearrangement + MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer sources; `FindSyntenyBlocks` (ortholog pairs grouped by chr pair ‚Üí collinear runs merged under maxGap, ‚â•minGenes; I1‚ÄìI5 incl. SequenceIdentity=NaN per MCScanX) + `DetectRearrangements` (adjacent-block signals ‚Üí Translocation/Inversion/Deletion/Duplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation/inversion oracles; ¬ß7 coverage-strengthen (M16 maxGap gap closed); deviations None.
- [[chrom-telo-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-TELO-001 (telomere analysis): fifth Chromosome-analysis file; Wikipedia Telomere + Meyne 1989 (TTAGGG conserved) + Cawthon 2002 (T/S ratio) + Blackburn-Gall 1978 sources; 3‚Ä≤ TTAGGG / 5‚Ä≤ CCCTAA end detection, 70%-per-window purity (5/6 or 5/7 match), T/S linearity length=refLen√ó(tsRatio/refRatio), IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&len<criticalLen)OR empty; 1200-bp/purity-0.833/12000/searchLen-truncation + T/S oracles; criticalLength/minTelomereLength/searchLength/referenceLength are configurable defaults not biological constants; deviations None.
- [[chrom-cent-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CHROM-CENT-001 (centromere analysis): second Chromosome-analysis file; layered multi-session record; Wikipedia + Levan 1964 + Hartley/McNulty/Masumoto/Rosandiƒá/Alkan/Shepelev + Dfam/T2T (CC0) sources; Levan q/p arm-ratio classes (1.7/3.0/7.0 boundaries), additive alpha-satellite/CENP-B/HOR/SF detectors (171-bp monomer, 17-bp box, <5% inter-HOR); AlphaSatelliteContent-is-density + SF1/SF2-unresolved limitations.
- [[codon-cai-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-CAI-001 (Codon Adaptation Index): Wikipedia + Sharp & Li 1987 + Jansen 2003 (verbatim single-codon exclusion) + Kazusa sources; geometric-mean-of-w=f/maxf formula, dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode, E. coli oracles (CUA-CCA-ACA‚Üí0.1980); one deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (not the RSCU page's 0.5 pseudocount).
- [[codon-enc-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-ENC-001 (Effective Number of Codons, ENC/Nc, Wright 1990): Fuglsang 2004/2006 (verbatim Wright equations) + NCBI degeneracy partition sources; codon-homozygosity FÃÇ=(n¬∑Œ£p¬≤‚àí1)/(n‚àí1), Nc=2+9/FÃÇ‚ÇÇ+1/FÃÇ‚ÇÉ+5/FÃÇ‚ÇÑ+3/FÃÇ‚ÇÜ, unbiased‚Üí61 / max-bias‚Üí20 / no-bias-sim‚Üí40.5 oracles, Ile (FÃÇ‚ÇÇ+FÃÇ‚ÇÑ)/2 fallback; one assumption = non-source lower clamp at 20.
- [[codon-opt-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-OPT-001 (codon optimization / OptimizeSequence): Wikipedia codon-usage-bias + CAI + Plotkin-Kudla 2011 + Mignon 2018 + Kazusa sources; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondary), protein-preservation + Met/Trp-fixed + CAI‚àà(0,1] invariants, E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon tables; RNA-notation + T‚ÜíU + trim-to-codon + 1e-6 CAI clamp implementation notes; no source contradictions.
- [[codon-rscu-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-RSCU-001 (RSCU + `CountCodons`): second RSCU unit; Sharp/Tuohy/Mosurski 1986 + LIRMM + GenomicSig + seqinr `uco` + cubar `est_rscu` sources, n_i¬∑x/Œ£x formula, Leu CTGCTGCTGCTA‚Üí4.5/1.5/0 + Phe TTTTTTTTC‚Üí4/3,2/3 examples, CountCodons non-overlapping-triplet/non-ACGT-exclusion contract; stop-codons-as-degeneracy-3-family framing (cross-page nuance vs the concept's forward_table exclusion), cubar pseudocount vs repo-returns-0 for absent families.
- [[codon-stats-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-STATS-001 (Codon Usage Statistics, GetStatistics + CalculateCai): the codon-family aggregation/reporting view; bundles RSCU + ENC + CAI + positional GC (GC1/GC2/GC3, GC3s=synonymous-3rd-position GC excluding Met/Trp/stop, Peden 1999) + E. coli/human reference tables; Sharp & Li 1987 + Biopython + Kazusa + CodonW/EMBOSS sources; ATGGCA‚ÜíGC3s 0/GC3 50 + GCTGCC‚ÜíCAI ‚àö0.122 oracles; deviations = GC3s-as-percentage + skip-zero-w (not 0.01 floor); reuses existing codon concepts, no new concept.
- [[codon-usage-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-USAGE-001 (raw codon usage table + TVD comparison, CalculateCodonUsage + CompareCodonUsage): Wikipedia codon-usage-bias + Kazusa + Sharp & Li 1987 sources; unnormalized Dictionary<codon,int> counts (T‚ÜíU, drop partial codon), Similarity=1‚àíŒ£|f‚ÇÅ‚àíf‚ÇÇ|/2 TVD in [0,1] with proven identity/symmetry/range/disjoint‚Üí0 properties, AUGGCUGCU‚Üí{AUG:1,GCU:2} + sim oracles (2/3, 0.5, 0.75, 0.25, disjoint‚Üí0); TVD-not-cosine + empty‚Üí0 deviations; new codon-usage-comparison concept, reuses RSCU counting.
- [[seq-codon-freq-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-CODON-FREQ-001 (Codon Frequencies, SequenceStatistics.CalculateCodonFrequencies(seq, frame)): the normalized, frame-aware frequency view of the codon-usage family; returns count/total fractions (double), DNA-native (no T‚ÜíU), non-ACGT/ambiguous triplets excluded (Kazusa CUTG), reading-frame offset 0/1/2 changes the multiset; Kazusa CUTG + EMBOSS cusp (Fraction=per-AA‚âÝthis / Frequency=count/total) + Wikipedia + Nakamura-Gojobori-Ikemura 2000 sources; ATGATGAAA f0‚ÜíATG 2/3,AAA 1/3 / f1‚ÜíTGA 1.0, ATGNNNAAA‚ÜíATG 1/2,AAA 1/2, cusp 22/386=56.995/1000 oracles; single assumption = empty table when total=0; distinct method from CalculateCodonUsage (CODON-USAGE-001, raw int counts + T‚ÜíU + frame-0), enriches codon-usage-comparison, no new concept.
- [[codon-rare-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit CODON-RARE-001 (rare codon detection, FindRareCodons + %MinMax/Sherlocc cluster addendum): Wikipedia + GenScript GenRCA (Fan 2024) + Kazusa + Shu 2006 (5√óCUA ~3-fold inhibition) + Sharp & Li 1987 sources; freq<threshold (default 0.15) per-family rule, E. coli AGA/AGG/CGA/CUA rare set; Clarke&Clark 2008 %MinMax 18-codon window (%Min/%Max signed, ¬±100%) + Chartier 2012 Sherlocc 7-codon ‚â•4-slow cluster rule; Arg-family %MinMax oracles (‚àí86.36/+100/+36.47) + Sherlocc 7√óAGA/4+3/3+4 oracles; single-codon-AA no-NaN + overlapping-window-merge corner cases; no contradictions.
- [[trans-codon-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-CODON-001 (codon ‚Üí amino-acid translation, `GeneticCode.Translate`, area Translation): NCBI Genetic Codes (`transl_table` 1/2/3/11 `AAs`+`Starts` strings, 2024-09-23) + Wikipedia Genetic/Start/Stop codon sources; complete 64-codon Standard table oracle + table-2 (AGA/AGG‚Üí`*`, AUA‚ÜíM, UGA‚ÜíW) / table-3 (CUN‚ÜíT, AUA‚ÜíM, UGA‚ÜíW) diff oracles; DNA‚ÜîRNA T‚ÜîU + case-insensitive + stop‚Üí`*` + len‚âÝ3‚ÜíArgumentException contract; mappings match NCBI exactly (Deviations: None), BUT one flagged source-vs-impl discrepancy ‚Äî IUPAC ambiguity codon (NNN) returns `'X'` not the doc's promised exception (only non-IUPAC like Z throws). New concept [[genetic-code-translation]].
- [[trans-prot-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-PROT-001 (**whole-sequence protein translation** ‚Äî the `Translator` class, area Translation): the sequence-level layer **above** the TRANS-CODON-001 codon table. Framed translation (`frame` 0/1/2, else throws), **six-frame** translation (dict keyed ‚àí3‚Ä¶+3 excluding 0; 3 forward + 3 reverse-complement, each 5'‚Üí3'), optional `toFirstStop`, and genetic-code-parameterized `Translator.FindOrfs` (min-length + both-strand). Composes [[genetic-code-translation]] via a `GeneticCode` parameter (all 4 tables flow through); DNA‚ÜîRNA T‚ÜíU + case-insensitive + trailing partial codon untranslated. Oracle: insulin B chain (UniProt P01308 pos 25‚Äì54) `TTCGTG‚Ä¶AAGACC` 90 nt ‚Üí `FVNQHLCGSHLVEALYLVCGERGFFYTPKT` 30 aa; 4 tables verified codon-by-codon vs NCBI (2024-09-23), Deviations None. Sources: Wikipedia Translation-biology / Reading-frame / ORF + NCBI Genetic Codes + UniProt P01308. Its ORF finder is deliberately **not** contract-equivalent to the ATG-only [[open-reading-frame-detection]]. **Enriched** [[genetic-code-translation]] (no new concept).
- [[trans-sixframe-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-SIXFRAME-001 (**six-frame translation** + **START‚ÜíSTOP ORF finding**, the same `Translator` surface as TRANS-PROT-001, from the reference-implementation angle): **Biopython `six_frame_translations`** (governing algorithm) + **EMBOSS `transeq`** (frame values 1/2/3/F/‚àí1/‚àí2/‚àí3/R/6) + **EMBOSS `getorf`** (`-find 1` START‚ÜíSTOP model) + **NCBI transl_table=1** + **Wikipedia Reading-frame** sources. Key distinctive detail: the **reverse-frame numbering convention** ‚Äî this repo uses the **Biopython independent-offset** rule (frame ‚àík = reverse-complement translated 5'‚Üí3' at offset k‚àí1, no correspondence to +1), the documented "alternative" to EMBOSS's phase-locked default (hence `ACTGG` frame ‚àí1 = `P` here vs `S` in EMBOSS ‚Äî a labelling convention, not a bug). ORF `FindOrfs` = START‚ÜíSTOP, start-residue included / stop excluded, `minLength` in **amino acids** (getorf's `-minsize` is nucleotides). Oracles: 39-nt full six-frame table; `GGGATGAAACCCTAAGGG` ‚Üí `MKP` (start 3, end 14 incl.). **Enriched** [[genetic-code-translation]] (no new concept); genetic-code-parameterized sibling of ATG-only [[open-reading-frame-detection]].
- [[compgen-ani-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-ANI-001 (Average Nucleotide Identity, ANIb; first Comparative-genomics file): Goris 2007 + Konstantinidis & Tiedje 2005 + pyani sources; 1020 nt query fragmentation, best-match placement, >30% identity / ‚â•70% alignable cut-offs recalculated over query-fragment length, mean of qualifying fragments; ANI‚âà95%‚Üî70% DDH species boundary; gapped Smith-Waterman recovers indels (AAAACCCC/AAAATCCCC 0.875‚Üí1.0), reciprocal ANI = mean of both directions; exact-arithmetic oracles (1.0/0.9375/0.875, cut-off/short‚Üíexclude‚Üí0); engine decision = LocalAlign not NCBI-BLASTN; deviations None.
- [[compgen-cluster-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-CLUSTER-001 (Conserved Gene Clusters / common intervals of permutations; Comparative-genomics): Uno & Yagiura 2000 + Heber & Stoye 2001 + Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 + Didier et al. 2013 sources; cluster = gene-label set contiguous in EVERY genome (order/strand-free), size ‚â•2, whole set trivial, K‚â•2; golden vector Id‚Çá vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) ‚Üí {1,2}{1,2,3}{3,4,5,6}{4,5}{4,5,6}{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, sequence-with-duplicates {1,2,3,4}; strict gap-free model (maxGap inert, API back-compat only; gene-teams not implemented); deviations None.
- [[compgen-dotplot-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001 (Dot Plot Generation, word-match / k-tuple dot matrix; Comparative-genomics): Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 + EMBOSS `dottup` + Wikipedia + Huttley sources; dot at (x,y) iff length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences), `wordSize` (default 10) noise/sensitivity trade-off, `stepSize` x-subsampling; AGCGT/AT k=1‚Üí{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4‚Üí7-dot overlapping set, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjoint‚Üíno dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[compgen-ortho-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-ORTHO-001 (ortholog detection by Reciprocal Best Hits + in-paralog within-genome best hits; Comparative-genomics): Fitch 1970 (orthology=speciation / paralogy=duplication) + Tatusov 1997 (COG symmetrical best hits) + Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 (operational RBH, best hit=max similarity, ‚â•50% coverage, E‚â§1e-6) + Remm 2001 (InParanoid RBH seed + in-paralog rule) sources; RBH reciprocity guard (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog), within-genome mutual best hits = recent paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog/empty oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking; deviations None. Shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, sub-unit of genome-comparison-core-dispensable.
- [[compgen-compare-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-COMPARE-001 (end-to-end genome comparison `CompareGenomes`; Comparative-genomics orchestrating pipeline): Tettelin 2005 (pan-genome core/dispensable) + Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008/Tatusov 1997 (RBH = shared gene) + fraction-of-syntenic-genes metric + MCScanX (Wang 2012) sources; core=RBH ortholog pairs, dispensable=rest, outputs Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped ‚â§1; oracles one-shared‚Üí1/1/1, disjoint‚Üí0/2/2, identical 5-collinear+1‚Üí5/1/1 & 0.8333; symmetric partition; empty‚Üíall-0; two assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate inherited from COMPGEN-RBH-001, MCScanX ‚â•5-anchor block threshold ‚Üí OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[compgen-rearr-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REARR-001 (genome rearrangement detection by breakpoints, signed gene-order comparison; Comparative-genomics): Hunter Lecture 16 (Hannenhalli‚ÄìPevzner/Bafna‚ÄìPevzner) + Tannier PMC3887456 + Bafna‚ÄìPevzner 1998 sources; signed permutation `Œ±(i)=¬±a`, extended `(0,‚Ä¶,n+1)`, breakpoint = pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(‚àíy,‚àíx)` in Œ≤, `b(Œ±)` count + `d_BP=n‚àísim` + reversal lower bound `d‚â•b/2`; Inversion (sign-flip reversal) vs Transposition (orientation-preserving block move); Hunter `Œ±=(‚àí2,‚àí3,+1,+6,‚àí5,‚àí4)`‚Üíb=6, identity‚Üí0, single-inversion‚Üí2 oracles; three scoping assumptions (orthologMap-supplied anchors, strand=sign, only Inversion/Transposition classified ‚Äî Translocation/indel/dup "Not implemented"); the signed-permutation alternative to block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]]; deviations None.
- [[compgen-reversal-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001 (Reversal/inversion distance as the breakpoint lower bound ‚åàb/2‚åâ; Comparative-genomics): NOT a new algorithm ‚Äî the UNSIGNED specialization of [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]'s reversal-distance bound (Bafna‚ÄìPevzner 1998 + Hunter Lecture 16 + H√ºbotter 2020 + Bergeron‚ÄìMixtacki‚ÄìStoye 2009); `CalculateReversalDistance` counts unsigned breakpoints `|Œî|‚âÝ1` on the extended perm and returns `‚åàb/2‚åâ=(b+1)/2`; [2,3,1,6,5,4]‚Üí2, [4,3,2,1]‚Üí1, identity‚Üí0 oracles; lower-bound-not-exact (no HP cycle/hurdle refinement); two assumptions (integer ‚åàb/2‚åâ rounding, unequal-length‚ÜíArgumentException); deviations None.

- [[protmotif-domain-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-DOMAIN-001 (protein domain prediction & signal-peptide prediction; ProteinMotif family): `FindDomains` deterministic PROSITE-**pattern** domain scan (PS00028 C2H2 zinc finger `C-x(2,4)-C-x(3)-[LIVMFYWC]-x(8)-H-x(3,5)-H`/PF00096, PS00017 P-loop `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`/PF00069, PS00678 WD40 15-residue signature/PF00400; ScanProsite‚Üíregex rules; GBB1_HUMAN P62873 WD40 positive at 69/156/284) ‚Äî SH3/PDZ are PROSITE **PROFILEs** with no deterministic pattern (honest residual, unsourced regexes removed); opt-in `FindDomainsByHmm`/`Plan7ProfileHmm` reproduces HMMER3 over 3 bundled CC0 Pfam HMMs (PF00018 SH3/PF00595 PDZ/PF00400 WD40) ‚Äî Viterbi/Forward log-odds (1e-9 hand-HMM pin), local-multihit `pre_score` vs Swiss-Prot `bg->f` (~1e-5-bit hmmsearch parity), null2 bias, Gumbel/exp E-values (`E=P¬∑Z`), `p7_domaindef` envelope decomposition (GBB1‚Üí7 blades exact) + stochastic-traceback clustering (Easel LCG seed 42), all verified vs pyhmmer 0.12.1; `PredictSignalPeptide` von Heijne tripartite n/h/c + ‚àí1,‚àí3 rule {A,G,S}, weights (n+2h+c)/4, evidence-based constraints (nScore>0 & hScore‚â•0.5, no arbitrary threshold), Probability=Score (**this tripartite signal-peptide model is superseded** ‚Äî see [[protmotif-sp-001-evidence]]); C2H2 4..24 / P-loop 4..11 oracles; six resolved design decisions; MSV/bias prefilters + exact-RNG parity + full-Pfam out of scope; new concept [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]].
- [[protmotif-sp-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-SP-001 (signal-peptide cleavage-site prediction, `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictSignalPeptide`; ProteinMotif family): **redesign of the SAME method** ‚Äî **replaces** the fabricated tripartite n/h/c model of [[protmotif-domain-001-evidence|DOMAIN-001]] with the **von Heijne (1986) log-odds weight matrix** = EMBOSS 6.6.0 `sigcleave` (doc + `sigcleave.c` + `data/Esig.euk`/`Esig.pro`). Score = argmax over sites of `Œ£ ln(count/expect)` across positions ‚àí13..+2 (natural log; zero counts ‚Üí `1.0e-10` at conserved cols ‚àí3/‚àí1, else `1.0`); cleavage between ‚àí1/+1, `CleavagePosition` = 1-based mature start; `IsLikelySignalPeptide ‚áî Score ‚â• 3.5` (`minWeight` default 3.5, ~95% sens/spec, cleavage 75‚Äì80% correct); eukaryotic matrix (161 seqs) default, prokaryotic (36 seqs) via `prokaryote:true`. Worked oracle **ACH2_DROME (UniProt P17644)** ‚Üí Score **13.739**, mature start **42**, window `LLVLLLLCETVQA` (re-derived exactly in Python). Corner cases: best site always reported (`minWeight` only flags likelihood); < 15-aa window ‚Üí null; non-standard residues contribute 0; case-insensitive. One assumption (min length = 15-aa window); pitfalls log10-vs-ln and missing ‚àí3/‚àí1 penalty. Enriches [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] (no new concept).
- [[protmotif-find-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-FIND-001 (Protein Motif Search, Pattern-based; ProteinMotif family general engine): `ProteinMotifFinder.FindMotifByPattern` ‚Äî the **general, arbitrary caller-supplied PROSITE-pattern** protein motif finder that [[common-protein-motifs|`FindCommonMotifs`]] is a fixed-dictionary application of. Three primitives: `ConvertPrositeToRegex` (PROSITE‚Üíregex: `x`‚Üí`.`, `[ABC]`‚Üí`[ABC]`, `{ABC}`‚Üí`[^ABC]`, `x(n)`‚Üí`.{n}`, `x(n,m)`‚Üí`.{n,m}`, `<`‚Üí`^`, `>`‚Üí`$`); `FindMotifByPattern` (overlapping matches via regex lookahead `(?=(pattern))`, ScanProsite-consistent, 0-based Start/End, case-insensitive, empty/null‚Üíempty, invalid regex handled gracefully); information-content scoring `CalculateMotifScore` IC=Œ£log‚ÇÇ(20/allowed_count) over constrained positions + `CalculateEValue` E=(N‚àíL+1)¬∑2^(‚àíIC) (Schneider & Stephens 1990 ‚Äî BLAST citation explicitly removed). Verified PROSITE patterns PS00001/00004‚Äì00009/00016‚Äì00018/00028/00029 and **fixed two impl bugs**: PS00007 `[RK].{2}[DE].{3}Y` (was loosened `.{2,3}`) and PS00018 EF-hand (`{W}` not `x` at pos 2 + restored trailing `[LIVMFYW]`); five non-PROSITE patterns literature-verified (NLS1/NES1/SIM1/WW1/SH3_1). Datasets: Human Insulin P01308 + constructed pattern fixtures; all assumptions eliminated (0-vs-1-based coord convention only); new concept [[protein-motif-pattern-search]].
- [[protmotif-pattern-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-PATTERN-001 (Protein Pattern Matching Methods: `FindMotifByPattern`, `FindMotifByProsite`, `ConvertPrositeToRegex`, `FindDomains`). **Second Evidence over the same PROSITE‚Üíregex engine as PROTMOTIF-FIND-001** ‚Äî NO new concept; enriches [[protein-motif-pattern-search]] (and touches [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] for `FindDomains`). Two ASSUMPTIONs (lookahead overlap enumeration; combinatorial E=(N‚àíL+1)¬∑2^(‚àíIC) not ScanProsite Swiss-Prot E-value); no contradictions with FIND-001.

- [[protmotif-lc-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-LC-001 (protein low-complexity region detection, SEG; ProteinMotif-family registration of the SEG method). **Same algorithm as DISORDER-LC-001** ‚Äî NO new concept; enriches/cross-links the existing [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] anchor. - [[protmotif-tm-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROTMOTIF-TM-001 (Transmembrane helix prediction, Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy sliding window; ProteinMotif family, genuinely distinct hydrophobicity-based unit): slide a window of length **19** along the protein, score each window as the **arithmetic mean** of its per-residue Kyte-Doolittle (1982) hydropathy values, emit contiguous runs with window mean **> threshold 1.6** as membrane-spanning segments. Sources ‚Äî Kyte & Doolittle 1982 (rank 1) + Davidson DGPB background (window 19 + threshold 1.6 + mean-windowing rule, verbatim) + QIAGEN CLC + Davidson per-AA scores (the 20 scale values I 4.5‚Ä¶R ‚àí4.5, D/E/N/Q ‚àí3.5) + Biopython ProtParam `protein_scale(edge=1.0)`=mean/`gravy` + TM Œ±-helix length ~18‚Äì21 residues to span the ~3‚Äì4 nm bilayer. Oracles `D√ó10+L√ó20+D√ó10`‚Üíone segment (5,34) peak 3.8 / `D√ó40`‚Üínone / `L√ó19`‚Üí(0,18,3.8). Corner cases: <windowSize/null/empty‚Üíempty; non-standard residues (X,B,Z,`*`) excluded from the window mean. One assumption = segment `End=lastPassingProfileIndex+windowSize‚àí1` clamped (2026-06-16 off-by-one correction), no deviations; new concept [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]].

- [[meta-func-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit META-FUNC-001 (Functional prediction, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`; fifth Metagenomics family Evidence): Altschul NCBI BLAST-statistics tutorial + NCBI `blast_stat.c` (ungapped BLOSUM62 Œª=0.3176/K=0.134/H=0.4012) + NCBI BLOSUM62 diagonals (W11‚Ä¶) + PNNL ORA ¬ß8.2 sources; homology transfer = exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S ‚Üí bit `S'=(ŒªS‚àílnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=K¬∑m¬∑n¬∑e^(‚àíŒªS)=m¬∑n¬∑2^(‚àíS')`, best hit = lowest E-value (INV-01..03,06); hypergeometric right-tail ORA `P(X‚â•x)=1‚àíŒ£_{i=0}^{x‚àí1}C(M,i)C(N‚àíM,n‚àíi)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, p‚àà[0,1], x=0/M=0/n=0‚Üíp=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWW‚ÜíS33/S'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546e‚àí5 (both forms agree) + ORA N8000/M400/n100/x20‚Üí7.88e‚àí8; one assumption ASM-01 = ungapped exact-match model (affects which hits found, not the formulas); no contradictions. - [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit META-PATHWAY-001 (Pathway enrichment / over-representation analysis, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`; the DEDICATED unit for the ORA machinery that META-FUNC-001 exercises as component B): Boyle et al. 2004 GO::TermFinder (PMC3037731) + PNNL Proteomics ORA ¬ß8.2 (`phyper` reference) sources; hypergeometric right-tail `P(X‚â•x)=1‚àíŒ£_{i=0}^{x‚àí1}C(M,i)C(N‚àíM,n‚àíi)/C(N,n)` (N=background/M=pathway size/n=query/x=overlap), `phyper(x‚àí1,M,N‚àíM,n,lower.tail=FALSE)`, log-Gamma summation, p‚àà[0,1], sorted ascending; x=0/M=0/n=0‚Üíp=1 corner cases, M‚Üîn symmetry; oracles PNNL N8000/M100/n400/x20‚Üí7.88e‚àí8 + exact rational 1/252 (all overlap) / 5/6 (partial) / 1 (no overlap) / 251/252 (at-least-one); one assumption = background defaults to union-of-pathway-members when caller supplies none (formula-preserving, caller-overridable); no FDR correction; no contradictions. - [[rep-str-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit REP-STR-001 (Microsatellite / Short Tandem Repeat (STR) detection ‚Äî perfect default `FindMicrosatellites` **plus** the opt-in approximate/imperfect/interrupted `FindApproximateTandemRepeats` + `ComputeBernoulliStatistics`, Benson **Tandem Repeats Finder** 1999 model): Benson 1999 *Nucleic Acids Research* 27(2):573 (approximate-repeat definition, seven TRF statistics, wraparound-DP alignment, majority-rule consensus) + TRF definitions/desc pages (Bernoulli adjacent-copy model, PM matching / PI indel probability, defaults PM .80/PI .10) + TRF reference impl (recommended weights `(+2,‚àí7,‚àí7)`, Minscore 50) + Wikipedia Microsatellite (1‚Äì6 bp unit, 5‚Äì50 copies) sources; the opt-in approximate detector **closes the exact-copies-only gap** ‚Äî reports an interrupted tract as ONE repeat with percent-matches/percent-indels/score while the perfect detector fragments it; oracles `CAGCAGCAGTAGCAGCAG`‚Üíperiod 3 `CAG`√ó6 17match/1mismatch score 27 94.4%, single-base-deletion 29-bp‚Üíscore 51 clears default gate, Bernoulli adjacent PM 13/15 distinct from consensus 17/18, `CACACATACACA`‚ÜíPM 0.80 on-threshold; three assumptions (deterministic exhaustive (start,period) scan vs TRF probabilistic k-tuple seeding ‚Äî the genome-scale residual; percentage denominator = total alignment columns; adjacent-copy segmentation for Bernoulli PM/PI, exact for substitution-only); no contradictions. **No new concept** ‚Äî enriches the repeats family anchor [[repetitive-element-detection]] (Approximate STR detection section).
- [[restr-filter-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RESTR-FILTER-001 (Restriction Enzyme Filtering ‚Äî the first RESTR-* / MolTools reagent-selection unit): filter the enzyme library by end type (`GetBluntCutters()` / `GetStickyCutters()`) and by recognition-site length (`GetEnzymesByCutLength(min, max)` + single-length overload). Sources: Wikipedia *Sticky and blunt ends* (blunt = both strands terminate in a base pair, sticky = 5'/3' overhang, **blunt & sticky are the only two categories ‚Üí total, disjoint partition**, blunt-blunt always compatible) + Wikipedia *Restriction enzyme* (Type II undivided palindromes **4‚Äì8 nt**; center cut‚Üíblunt / staggered‚Üísticky; EcoRI `G^AATTC` / SmaI `CCC^GGG` / KpnI `GGTAC^C` / PstI `CTGCA^G` examples) + Wikipedia *List of restriction enzyme cutting sites* (4/6/8-bp categories) + NEB/REBASE (KpnI 3' overhang, EcoRI 5' overhang) + PMC/REBASE (SfiI interrupted palindrome `GGCCNNNN^NGGCC`, 13 nt, outside 4‚Äì8). Dataset oracle: SmaI/EcoRV/AluI/HaeIII blunt vs EcoRI(5')/KpnI(3')/PstI(3')/NotI/TaqI sticky + SfiI 13-nt interrupted. Contract: blunt ‚à™ sticky = full library & disjoint; `[min,max]` **inclusive** (`6‚Üí6` all 6-cutters, `9‚Üí10` none, `[4,8]` whole undivided library **except** 13-nt SfiI); single-length overload agrees at `min==max`; `min>max`/negative/zero ‚Üí empty. One API-shape assumption (inclusive range bounds; recognition-length values source-backed). No contradictions. New concept [[restriction-enzyme-filtering]].
- [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-DOTBRACKET-001 (Dot-Bracket / extended WUSS notation ‚Äî **parse & validate** a structure string; the notation/representation layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.ParseDotBracket` (structure string ‚Üí base pairs) + `ValidateDotBracket` (well-formedness). Sources: ViennaRNA *RNA Structure Notations* / *Dot-Bracket Notation* (rank 3 ‚Äî base pairs = matching `()`, unpaired = `.`; extended notation adds `<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase/lowercase letter pairs; **families are not required to nest ‚Üí pseudoknots**; uppercase = 5' opener / lowercase = 3' closer) + ViennaRNA WUSS / `vrna_db_from_WUSS()` + Infernal Nawrocki & Eddy 2013 (rank 3 ‚Äî **any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning if partners match**; flatten treats letter-pair pseudoknots as unpaired ‚Üí each family an **independent pairing system**) + Rfam glossary (rank 5 ‚Äî `<>`/`()`/`[]`/`{}` all pair; non-bracket `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` all single-stranded). Algorithm: **one balanced-bracket stack per family** (shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`); a closer must match a same-family opener. Oracles ‚Äî parse `((((....))))`‚Üí(0,11),(1,10),(2,9),(3,8), `([)]`‚Üí`(`:(0,2)+`[`:(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]` / `((((AAAA....))))aaaa`‚Üítwo 4-bp crossing helices; validate `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`‚Üí**true**, `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`‚Üí**false**. Two API-contract assumptions (malformed input ‚Üí best-effort parse dropping unmatched closers, gate with `ValidateDotBracket`; empty/null ‚Üí valid pair-free). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]].
- [[rna-energy-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-ENERGY-001 (**Free Energy Calculation**; the thermodynamic/energy layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`, the **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor** free-energy terms summed into a fold's ŒîG¬∞ at 37 ¬∞C. Sources: **NNDB (Nearest Neighbor Database) Turner04** (definitive parameter tables ‚Äî WC/GU stacking, hairpin `loop.txt`, terminal-mismatch, tri/tetra/hexaloop totals, hairpin bonuses/penalties) + Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004 (PNAS 101:7287) + Xia 1998 + SantaLucia 1998 + Heus & Pardi 1991; reference impls ViennaRNA / MFOLD / RNAstructure. Model `ŒîG¬∞total = init + Œ£stacking + Œ£loops`. Key parameters ‚Äî WC stacking **all negative** (GC-rich most stable, `GC/CG` ‚àí3.42, `GG/CC` ‚àí3.26; `AA/UU` ‚àí0.93); **G-U wobble variable, two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=‚àí0.5, note-b `5'GGUC/3'CUGG` special 3-stack total ‚àí4.12 (vs ‚àí1.77); **hairpin-loop init positive & non-monotonic** (3‚Üí5.4, 4‚Üí5.6, 6‚Üí5.4, 9‚Üí6.4, Jacobson-Stockmayer beyond 9); special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloop total energies; all-C loop penalty (3-nt +1.5 / >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); terminal mismatch (96); +0.45 per AU/GU end. Oracles GC 3-bp stem ‚àí5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` ‚àí3.42, GGUC/CUGG ‚àí4.12; single base pair / empty / poly-A ‚Üí **ŒîG¬∞=0** (stacking needs ‚â•2 adjacent pairs). No assumptions remain (all params = exact NNDB match); three **defined conditions** (37 ¬∞C, 2-dp precision, unknown stacks‚Üí0.0). No contradictions. New concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-HAIRPIN-001 (**Hairpin Loop and Stem Free-Energy Calculation**, Turner 2004 NN model): a focused deep-dive on `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy` + `CalculateStemEnergy`, **not** a stem-loop enumerator and **not** miRNA-specific ‚Äî it enriches the energy-layer concept [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (sibling of [[rna-energy-001-evidence]]) rather than defining a new one; distinct from the miRNA hairpin *finder* [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Source: **NNDB Turner 2004** hairpin pages (via Wayback) + **Mathews et al. 2004** PNAS 101:7287. Hairpin ŒîG¬∞ = init(n) + terminal mismatch + first-mismatch bonuses (UU/GA ‚àí0.9, GG ‚àí0.8) + special-GU-closure ‚àí2.2 (**G-U only, not U-G** ‚Äî documented asymmetry) + all-C penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6); **3-nt loops get no first-mismatch term**; loops < 3 nt prohibited; special tri/tetra/hexaloop totals override the model (`CAACG` 6.8, `CCUCGG` 2.5). Stem = per-stack stacking + **+0.45/AU-end**, P pairs ‚Üí **P‚àí1 stacks** (P ‚â§ 1 ‚áí 0). Oracles NNDB Example 1 (A-U closing, 6-nt loop A‚Ä¶A) loop +4.6 + helix ‚àí6.01 = **‚àí1.4**; Example 2 (5-nt loop G‚Ä¶G, GG bonus) loop +4.1 + helix ‚àí6.01 = **‚àí1.9**; all-C 3-nt loop 6.9, 4-nt 7.7. One display-precision item (2-dp intermediate rounding, tests assert `.Within(1e-9)`); no contradictions. **No new concept** ‚Äî enriches [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]].
- [[rna-invert-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-INVERT-001 (RNA inverted repeats / potential stem regions ‚Äî antiparallel **reverse-complement arms** that form a stem-loop; RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): IUPACpal (Alamro 2021, PMC7866733) `W G WÃÑ·¥ø` gapped model + *k*-Hamming mismatch (perfect = k=0) + Watson-Crick RNA complement (A‚ü∑U, C‚ü∑G) + Wikipedia/Ussery 2008 (`5'---TTACGnnnnnnCGTAA---3'`, zero-gap ‚áí palindrome) + EMBOSS `einverted` (inverted repeat = stem-loop = local alignment of a sequence vs its reverse complement) sources; oracles `UUACGAAAAAACGUAA` (arm `UUACG` 0‚Äì4 / loop 5‚Äì10 / arm `CGUAA` 11‚Äì15) and palindromic `GGCCAAAGGCC` (left 0‚Äì3 / right 7‚Äì10 / len 4); MUST antiparallel-not-parallel + no-IR‚Üíempty; scope restriction = **perfect ungapped `k=0`** arms only (einverted scored mismatch/gap DP Not Implemented), loop bounds via minSpacing/maxSpacing, maximal-arm non-overlapping greedy reporting; no contradictions. **No new concept** ‚Äî reuses [[repetitive-element-detection]] (same IUPACpal IR model) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (antiparallel RNA complement) + [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]/[[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] (stem-loop framing).
- [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-MFE-001 (**Minimum Free Energy (MFE) RNA secondary-structure prediction** ‚Äî the Zuker‚ÄìStiegler dynamic-programming folder; the folding/search layer of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Sources: **Zuker & Stiegler 1981** *NAR* 9(1):133 (rank 1 ‚Äî original MFE DP, loop decomposition hairpin/stacking/bulge-interior/multibranch, polynomial) + **Lorenz 2011** ViennaRNA 2.0 (rank 3 ‚Äî MFE fold "derived from the Zuker‚ÄìStiegler decomposition", **O(n¬≥)**) + **Ward 2017** *NAR* 45(14):8541 (rank 1 ‚Äî C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge, multiloop) + multiloop M/M1 + exterior F matrices, **standard affine multiloop ‚Üí O(n¬≥) time / O(n¬≤) space**, "simplest model is best") + **NNDB Turner 2004** worked examples + **Mathews 2004** PNAS 101:7287. The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner terms and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure. Oracles `CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy("CACAAAAAAAUGUG")`=‚àí1.41 (NNDB Example 1, structure `((((......))))`), `CACAGAAAGUGUG`=‚àí1.91 (Example 2, GG first mismatch). Invariants INV-01 MFE ‚â§ 0, INV-02 suffix-monotone `MFE(s) ‚â§ MFE(prefix)`, INV-03 optimized DP == classic O(n¬≥) baseline; empty/null / homopolymer `AAAAAAAA` / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` (`GCGC`) ‚Üí 0 (min hairpin loop 3 nt); intramolecular ‚áí no helix-init constant. Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0` with `a=9.25`/helix `c=‚àí0.63`; 2-dp rounding, tests `.Within(1e-9)` + `Round(mfe,1)`==NNDB), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]]; the folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] `AssessHairpinByMfe` path (prior pages' generic *RNA-STRUCT-001*) uses.
- [[rna-pair-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PAIR-001 (**RNA Base Pairing** ‚Äî the RNA-secondary-structure family's own base-pairing primitive): `RnaSecondaryStructure.CanPair` / `GetBasePairType` (typed `WatsonCrick`/`Wobble`/`null` classifier) / `GetComplement`. Sources: **Crick 1966** *J Mol Biol* 19:548 (wobble hypothesis ‚Äî G pairs C(WC)+U(wobble), U pairs A(WC)+G(wobble); G-U the only standard wobble, distinct from WC) + Wikipedia *Base pair* (canonical A‚Ä¢U 2 H-bonds / G‚Ä¢C 3 H-bonds, pairing reciprocal) + Wikipedia *Wobble base pair* + IUPAC-IUB 1970 *Biochemistry* 9(20):4022 (complement table) + Biopython `complement_rna("CGAUT")`‚Üí`"GCUAA"`. Rule {A-U, U-A, G-C, C-G}=WatsonCrick, {G-U, U-G}=Wobble, all else false/null; complement A‚ÜíU/U‚ÜíA/G‚ÜíC/C‚ÜíG/**T‚ÜíA**(DNA T=U)/N‚ÜíN/R‚ÜíY; symmetry `f(x,y)==f(y,x)`; non-alphabet‚Üífalse/null no exception. One non-correctness normalization (case-insensitive upper-casing). No contradictions. **No new concept** ‚Äî enriches the shared [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive (the MIRNA-PAIR-001 sibling), adding the typed `GetBasePairType` classifier surface.
- [[rna-partition-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PARTITION-001 (**RNA partition function (McCaskill) and Boltzmann structure probability** ‚Äî the probabilistic/ensemble layer of the RNA secondary-structure family): the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium partition function `Z`, per-base-pair binding probabilities, and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure. Sources: **McCaskill 1990** *Biopolymers* 29(6-7):1105 (rank 1, PMID 1695107 ‚Äî full equilibrium partition function + substructure probabilities, **O(n¬≥) recursion**) + **S. Will MIT 18.417 (2011)** slides (rank 1 ‚Äî inside `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + Œ£_k Q_{i,k-1}¬∑Q^b_{kj}`, `Z = Q_{1n}`, base case `Q_ij=1` for i‚â•j‚àím; outside base-pair-probability recursion; `Pr[P|S]=Z‚Åª¬πexp(‚àíŒ≤E(P))`) + **Freiburg McCaskill tool** (rank 3 ‚Äî simplified fixed-per-pair `E_bp` model, WC+GU pairing) + **ViennaRNA pf_fold** (rank 3 ‚Äî `p(s)=e^(‚àíŒ≤E(s))/Z`, default 37 ¬∞C = 310.15 K, RT = 0.61626805). **Correction (2026-06-16):** base-pair probability requires the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_kl¬∑O_kl/Z`; the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not external 1/20; verified to 3.3e-16 vs Boltzmann brute force). Oracles (E_bp=0 ‚áí Z counts structures): `AAAA`‚Üí1, `GC`‚Üí1, `GGGGCCCC`‚Üí16, `GGGAAACCC`‚Üí20 (two independent derivations). Invariants Z ‚â• 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) ‚àà [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum ‚â§ 1 (300 random seqs, max 0.983), monotone in E_bp; min-loop m forbids j‚àík ‚â§ m pairs, WC+GU only. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN ‚Äî energy model only; recurrence + probabilities + invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] ‚Äî the ensemble/`alternative_to` counterpart of [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]].
- [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKPREDICT-001 (**Pseudoknot structure prediction ‚Äî canonical H-type, pknotsRG class**; the **crossing-helix layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single simple recursive pseudoknot (two **crossing** helices, `i<k<j<l` Antczak 2018) ‚Äî the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill]] predictors cannot represent. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (rank 1, PMC514697 ‚Äî pknotsRG "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", grammar `a~~~u~~~b~~~v~~~a'~~~w~~~b'`, **O(n‚Å¥)/O(n¬≤)**, canonization rules, penalties) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** source (rank 3 ‚Äî verbatim penalties + same-NN-model helices, no extra per-pair penalty) + **Wikipedia/Rivas & Eddy 1999** (H-type 5'‚Üí3' stem1-5'‚Üíloop1‚Üístem2-5'‚Üíloop2‚Üístem1-3'‚Üíloop3‚Üístem2-3', two-layer `()`/`[]`) + **PDB 437D / Su 1999** (BWYV real H-type, tertiary-stabilized) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Energy = Turner NN stacking both helices + penalties **pseudoknot initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** (kcal/mol). Canonization: equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`‚Üí`HasPseudoknot==true`, stems (0,15)‚Ä¶(3,12)+(6,21)‚Ä¶(9,18), two-layer `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`, ŒîG<MFE; plain hairpin `GGGGAAAACCCC`‚Üí`HasPseudoknot==false` = MFE `((((....))))`; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG`‚ÜíNN optimum is the stem-1 hairpin **not** the knot (documented NN-only limit). Invariants `FreeEnergy ‚â§ CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` (MFE fallback), no spurious knot, each position paired ‚â§1√ó + ‚â•1 genuine crossing; empty/null/too-short‚Üíempty pair-free ŒîG 0. One documented scope note (PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage ‚Äî single canonical H-type only; recursively-nested / over-arching / multiple knots **not** implemented; loops fold with the existing MFE). No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] ‚Äî the crossing-structure complement of the nested MFE folder + McCaskill ensemble.
- [[rna-pkrecursive-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PKRECURSIVE-001 (**Recursive pknotsRG pseudoknot prediction ‚Äî nested / multiple / over-arching H-type knots**; the **recursive-grammar extension** of the single-knot RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain **several** pseudoknots and knots **nested inside loops / over-arched by an enclosing helix**, filling exactly the PARTIAL-coverage gap the single-knot unit recorded. **Same pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004/2007) ‚Äî same Turner-NN energy on both helices, same penalties **initiation 9.0 / unpaired loop nt 0.3 / pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol, same canonization rules ‚Äî but the three loops *u*/*v*/*w* now fold by the **same recursive folder** (a loop may contain a further knot), the top level **chains multiple knots**, and an enclosing helix may **over-arch** a knot. Sources: **Reeder & Giegerich 2004** *BMC Bioinformatics* 5:104 (loops "fold internally ‚Ä¶ **including simple recursive pseudoknots**", **O(n‚Å¥)/O(n¬≤)**, canonization 8‚Üí4 boundaries vs Rivas & Eddy O(n‚Å∂)/O(n‚Å¥)) + **Reeder, Steffen & Giegerich 2007** *NAR* 35:W320 (per-interval **competition** with unknotted foldings ‚Äî the whole-sequence mechanism enabling multiple/nested knots) + **pknotsRG `Energy.lhs`** (verbatim 9.0/0.3/0.0) + **Antczak 2018** (crossing `i<k<j<l`). Constructed fully-derivable oracles: over-arching `AAAAAAAAGGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGGUUUUUUUU` (38 nt)‚Üí`((((((((((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]))))))))` **ŒîG ‚àí14.37** (single-knot/MFE both ‚àí13.05, no combined structure); two-knot 80-nt‚Üí**two** crossing knots (crossing-count 32) **ŒîG ‚àí28.74** (single/MFE ‚àí27.14, none); plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`‚Üí no knot = MFE; single-knot parity `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`‚Üíidentical ‚àí8.76. Invariants recursive ŒîG ‚â§ MFE (0 violations, 150-seq random sweep), no spurious knots, each position paired ‚â§1√ó + ‚â•1 crossing; empty/null/too-short‚Üíempty pair-free. **Excluded** (verbatim): triple-crossing helices, kissing hairpins, bulged/unequal-length helices. Two scope notes: PARTIAL recursion (realizes the recursive *class* via maximal-extent helix scan, not bit-identical to the reference 4-boundary ADP parser) + two-simultaneous-knot cases are **engineered** (isolated A¬∑U clamps ‚Äî two strong G¬∑C knots are the genuine MFE only when the cross-region nested alternative is suppressed). No contradictions. **Enriches** [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] (¬ß6, the recursive extension of the single-knot concept ‚Äî no new concept).
- [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001 (**Pseudoknot detection** ‚Äî identify **crossing** base pairs in a **given** structure; the detection/analysis facet of the RNA crossing-helix family, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a base-pair **set** (not a sequence), a pure **O(n¬≤) combinatorial scan** reports every crossing pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l`. Sources: **Antczak et al. 2018** *Bioinformatics* 34(8):1304 (rank 1 ‚Äî crossing/conflict `i<j<i'<j'`, pseudoknot **order** = min base-pair-set decompositions to nested, DBL notation order 0 `()`/1 `[]`/2 `{}`/3 `<>`/4‚Äì8 letters, H-type `([)]`) + **Smit, Rother, Heringa & Knight 2008** *RNA* 14(3):410 (rank 1 ‚Äî pseudoknot presence *requires* crossing pairs; order-assignment / pseudoknot-removal family) + **biotite.structure.pseudoknots** (rank 3 ‚Äî crossing = not purely nestable; nested order 0 / knotted order 1+) + **Wikipedia Pseudoknot** (rank 4, cites Rivas & Eddy 1999). Crossing `i<k<j<l` = pseudoknot; two exhaustive negatives **nested** `i<k<l<j` + **disjoint** `j<k`. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)‚Üí`0<1<2<3`‚Üíone pseudoknot, nested (0,5)+(1,4)‚Üínone, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)‚Üínone. Invariants ‚â•2 pairs required / endpoints normalized min-max to open<close / deterministic / every reported knot satisfies `i<k<j<l`. **Distinct** from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (pair set vs sequence, O(n¬≤) scan vs O(n‚Å¥) energy DP) ‚Äî it *is* the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** grouping (DBL layering) Not Implemented (reports the binary crossing relations); no contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] ‚Äî the analysis-side sibling of the crossing-helix predictor.
- [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STEMLOOP-001 (**Stem-Loop (Hairpin) Detection**, area `RnaStructure`): the **enumeration layer** of the RNA secondary-structure family ‚Äî `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins` **scan a sequence for every stem-loop** it can form (stem of antiparallel WC/wobble pairs + apical loop), an **O(n¬≤¬∑L)** scan distinct from the single-optimal [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]], the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]]. Sources: Wikipedia (Stem-loop / Tetraloop / Pseudoknot ‚Äî loop **‚â•3 nt** steric floor, optimal **4-8 nt**; UUCG+GNRA **~70%** of 16S-rRNA tetraloops) + Woese 1990 (PNAS 87:8467) + Antao 1991 (NAR 19:5901, **UUCG most stable**) + Heus & Pardi 1991 (Science 253:191) + Rivas & Eddy 1999 (pseudoknot alg) + NNDB Turner 2004 (tetraloop energetics). Tetraloop families **GNRA** (GAAA/GCAA/GGAA/GUAA) / **UNCG** (UACG/UCCG/UGCG/UUCG) / **CUUG**, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus; `FindPseudoknots` flags crossing pairs `i<k<j<l` (same primitive as [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]). Oracles `GGGAAAACCC`‚Üí`(((....)))` (3-bp stem + AAAA loop), `GGGCGAAAGCCC`‚ÜíGNRA tetraloop, `AAAA‚Ä¶`/`GC`/`GCAUC`‚Üínone. Invariants non-overlap / ‚â§1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; defaults wobble-on, minLoop 3, minStem 3. Limitations: no PK prediction from sequence, simplified energy, no internal loops/bulges, single structure. No contradictions. **New concept** [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]].
- [[rna-struct-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit RNA-STRUCT-001 (**Secondary Structure Prediction**, area `RnaStructure`): the **top-level structure-prediction umbrella** on `RnaSecondaryStructure` ‚Äî `Predict(sequence)` (a **Nussinov & Jacobson 1980** O(n¬≥)/O(n¬≤) base-pair-**maximizing** DP), `PredictWithConstraints` (forced base pairs, Mathews 2004), `ToDotBracket`/`FromDotBracket` (notation round-trip). Headline objective = maximize the **(weighted) base-pair count** (WC ‚àí2.0 / wobble ‚àí1.0), "**relative stability, not physical energy units**" ‚Äî a **distinct sibling** of the physical-kcal/mol [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|RNA-MFE-001]], **not an alias**: both live on `RnaSecondaryStructure` and share its Zuker MFE machinery (this unit's **deviation D5** added `CalculateMfeStructure`/`PredictStructureMfe`, the Zuker‚ÄìStiegler traceback partner of RNA-MFE-001's `PredictStructure`). Stem-loop energy model uses Turner 2004 / NNDB terms ([[rna-free-energy-turner-model]]). Sources: Nussinov & Jacobson 1980 (*PNAS* 77:6309) + Zuker & Stiegler 1981 (*NAR* 9:133) + MIT 6.047 Lec 08 (Washietl 2012, explicit F/C/M/M¬π recurrences) + Turner 2004/NNDB + Mathews 2004 (*PNAS* 101:7287) + Wikipedia. Oracles simple hairpin `GGGGAAAACCCC`‚Üí`((((....))))`, GNRA `GCGCGAAACGCGC`‚ÜíGA first-mismatch ‚àí0.9, tRNA-like 72-nt cloverleaf, poly-A `AAAAAAAAAAAA`‚Üíno pairs/MFE 0. Invariants dot-bracket balance / MFE sign ‚â§ 0 / WC stacking negative / loop init positive / non-overlap / ‚â§1 pair per base; empty/null‚ÜíMFE 0, min hairpin 3-bp stem + 3-nt loop, case-insensitive. **Pseudoknots detected (not predicted)** via the `i<k<j<l` crossing test ([[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]); D1/D2/D5 resolved, D3 int21 (2,304) / D4 int22 (36,864) internal-loop lookup tables BLOCKED (too large for inline static data). No source contradictions; one wiki reconciliation (RNA-STRUCT-001 ‚âÝ RNA-MFE-001, superseding the earlier alias assumption). **New concept** [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]].
- [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-BOOT-001 (Phylogenetic Bootstrap Analysis ‚Äî Felsenstein's bootstrap proportions; first phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Felsenstein 1985 *Evolution* 39(4):783 (origin ‚Äî resample characters with replacement, same sample size, keep species; *P* = fraction of bootstrap samples a group appears in; 95%‚Üísignificant) + Lemoine 2018 *Nature* 556:452 PMC6030568 (same-length pseudo-alignments; support = proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch; branch = bipartition; binary per-replicate) + Biopython `Bio.Phylo.Consensus` (`bootstrap`/`bootstrap_trees`/`get_support` ‚Äî column resample `randint(0,length-1)`, clades matched **by terminal leaf-name set**, only `find_clades(terminal=False)` scored, `(t+1)*100/size`) sources; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor 100 reps seed 42 ‚Üí support{A,B}=support{C,D}=1.0 (saturated JC distances ‚Üí identical topology every replicate), all-identical `ACGTACGT`‚Üíevery clade 1.0; MUST-test support‚àà[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / support=k/replicates, input validation null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage √ó100); no contradictions. Own concept [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]].
- [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PHYLO-COMP-001 (Tree Comparison ‚Äî Robinson‚ÄìFoulds distance, MRCA, patristic distance; second phylogenetics PHYLO-* unit): Wikipedia Robinson‚ÄìFoulds metric / MRCA / Phylogenetic tree + Robinson & Foulds 1981 (doi:10.1016/0025-5564(81)90043-2, RF proper metric via splits) + Smith 2020 (generalized RF) + Day 1985 (linear-time) sources; RF = symmetric difference `A+B` of canonical split sets (raw count, even, rooted-clade = dummy-leaf), **max RF = 2(n‚àí2) rooted vs 2(n‚àí3) unrooted** reconciled by dummy-leaf equivalence; MRCA O(n) recursive leaf-name traversal (not-in-tree‚Üínull), patristic = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` (not-in-tree‚ÜíNaN, zero-branches‚Üí0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/‚â•0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/‚â•0; two source-backed scope decisions (binary-only via `PhyloNode` Left/Right, rooted-only via UPGMA/NJ); no deviations, no contradictions. Own concept [[tree-comparison-metrics]].

- [[pop-freq-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit POP-FREQ-001 (Allele & genotype frequencies ‚Äî major/minor frequencies, MAF, MAF filtering; foundational population-genetics POP-\* primitive): Wikipedia *Allele frequency* / *Genotype frequency* (biallelic `p = f(AA) + ¬Ωf(AB)`, `q = f(BB) + ¬Ωf(AB)`, **`p + q = 1`**; allele-counting `total = 2¬∑(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major = 2¬∑n_AA+n_AB`, `minor = 2¬∑n_BB+n_AB`; four-o'clock oracle 49/42/9 ‚Üí freq(a)=0.30/freq(A)=0.70) + Wikipedia *Minor allele frequency* (`MAF = min(alt_freq, 1‚àíalt_freq)`, **`0 ‚â§ MAF ‚â§ 0.5`**; HapMap MAF ‚â• 0.05, common>0.05 vs rare<0.05) + VCF/PLINK dosage encoding (0=hom-ref/1=het/2=hom-alt, `alt_freq = Œ£g/(2n)`) + Gillespie 2004 / NDSU PopGen sources; oracles AF-1‚Ä¶AF-6, MAF-1‚Ä¶MAF-6 (alt_freq 0.7 ‚Üí MAF 0.3 symmetry; monomorphic ‚Üí 0; 50/50 ‚Üí 0.5), FLT-1‚Ä¶FLT-6 (MAF<0.01 / <0.05 / >0.4, empty/all/none); invariants p+q=1, major+minor=total, MAF symmetric 0‚Ä¶0.5; edge cases zero samples‚Üí(0,0), empty vector‚ÜíMAF 0, **negative count ‚Üí `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); all exact-match, no deviations/contradictions. - [[probe-design-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-DESIGN-001 (**TaqMan 5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe design rules**, opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer; **first PROBE-\* unit**): Applied Biosystems / Thermo Fisher (rank 2, chemistry manufacturer) + PREMIER Biosoft (rank 3) + ScienceDirect "TaqMan" (5'-G quenching rationale) + IDT (corroborating) sources; the TaqMan-specific hard rules ‚Äî **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter *even after cleavage* ‚Üí hard rule, not a soft penalty; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves to the antisense strand when unavoidable), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of ‚â•4 consecutive Gs** (separate from the generic homopolymer cap), **GC 30‚Äì80%**, **length 18‚Äì22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised), **probe Tm ‚â• primer Tm + 10 ¬∞C** (caller-supplied primer Tm; probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6¬∑log‚ÇÅ‚ÇÄ[Na‚Å∫]+41¬∑GC‚àí600/N` formula, not a TaqMan-specific NN calc); oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm ‚â§ 39.35), GCATCACCCTACATCACC fails 5'-G, ACCCCGGGGACCCTACAT fails GGGG-run, C=1/G=9 fails more-G-than-C, 16-nt fails len<18, GC 100% fails, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG ‚Üí RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand-selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18‚Äì22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions. Own concept [[taqman-probe-design-rules]].

Oracle CCATTGCTACC (LNA@4) ‚Üí ŒîH¬∞ ‚àí80.014 / ŒîS¬∞ ‚àí216.6 ‚Üí LNA Tm **63.528 ¬∞C** vs all-DNA 59.692 (**ŒîTm +3.84 ¬∞C**), agreeing with MELTING `mct04` 63.614 to 0.086 ¬∞C (documented base-NN-set residual; increments applied exactly). Enriches [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (LNA section).
- [[probe-valid-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit PROBE-VALID-001 (**hybridization-probe validation / off-target specificity scan** ‚Äî a **gapped Smith‚ÄìWaterman local alignment** of the candidate probe against a pooled reference, replacing an earlier ungapped Hamming scan; the **specificity-checking sibling** of PROBE-DESIGN-001, a genuinely distinct algorithm): Smith & Waterman 1981 (local-alignment recurrence with the **zero floor** ‚Üí local, indel-aware; traceback stops at 0 so a mismatched tail is trimmed), Altschul et al. 1990/1997 BLAST (the **gapped-vs-ungapped** improvement ‚Äî a single gapped alignment finds indel off-targets the ungapped HSPs miss; the unit realizes the *gapped local alignment* property, an **exact** full SW scan, not seed-and-extend or a genome-scale index), Karlin & Altschul 1990 / Altschul 1990 statistics (opt-in `ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`: `E=K¬∑m¬∑n¬∑e^(‚àíŒªS)`, Œª = root of `Œ£ p_i p_j e^(Œª s_ij)=1`, bit score `S'=(ŒªS‚àíln K)/ln 2`, `E=m¬∑n¬∑2^(‚àíS')`; preconditions expected-score<0 **and** a positive score; K caller-supplied), Kane et al. 2000 (empirical **>75% identity** cross-hybridization threshold, `minIdentity` default 0.75, caller-configurable; <14‚Äì15 contiguous-complement caveat); oracles ‚Äî probe `ACGTACGTACGT` vs an indel copy `ACGTACTGTACGT` aligns `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12 identity 1.0 `HasGaps=true` (**found by gapped, missed by ungapped Hamming maxMismatches=3**); indel+mismatch `ACGTACTGTACTT` ‚Üí SW trims `TT` tail ‚Üí 10/12 = 0.8333 (admitted @0.75, rejected @0.90); Œª for +1/‚àí3 uniform-0.25 = **1.3740631** (‚âà blastn 1.37, expected score ‚àí2.0<0), K=0.711/S=30/m=20/n=1000 ‚Üí bit **59.9627**, **E=1.7802e‚àí14**, E‚Üì in S and linear in m¬∑n; BLAST DNA scoring +2/‚àí3 gap ‚àí2. ASSUMPTION: on-target = first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match (API/labelling, not a sourced constant); no source contradictions. Own concept [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]].

- [[seq-complex-dust-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPLEX-DUST-001 (**DUST triplet-frequency low-complexity score**, `score = ‚àë_t c(c‚àí1)/2 / (L‚àí2)` over nucleotide triplet counts; the DNA-sequence low-complexity **masker**): Morgulis, Gertz, Sch√§ffer & Agarwala 2006 *J Comput Biol* 13(5):1028 (PMID 16796549, primary ‚Äî "triplet frequencies in 64-base windows", SDUST rewrite = same score, symmetric/context-insensitive masking) + Li 2025 longdust arXiv:2509.07357 (verbatim score formula, `k=3` hardcoded, `L‚àí2` = number of triplets, default window 64 / threshold 2.0 = level 20, **HIGH score ‚áí LOW complexity**) + lh3/sdust `sdust.c` (incremental `rw += cw[t]++` = closed-form `c(c‚àí1)/2` sum, `if (rw*10 > L*T)` with `W=64`/`T=20` ‚áí score>2.0); hand-derived oracles `ATGC`‚Üí0.0 (all-distinct triplets) / `ACGTACGT`‚Üí0.333‚Ä¶ / `AAAAAA`‚Üí1.5 / `ACACACAC`‚Üí1.0 / `AAAAAAAAAA`‚Üí3.5, homopolymer max `(L‚àí3)/2`, `L<3` undefined; two ASSUMPTIONs (general `wordSize` normalization `L‚àíw+1` ‚Äî only k=3 source-backed; `L<wordSize`‚Üí0), no source contradictions. - [[seq-complex-kmer-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPLEX-KMER-001 (**k-mer entropy** ‚Äî Shannon entropy `H = ‚àíŒ£ p·µ¢ log‚ÇÇ p·µ¢` of the overlapping k-mer frequency distribution, `p·µ¢ = n·µ¢/(L‚àík+1)`, bits; the **entropy member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` family**, `SequenceComplexity.CalculateKmerEntropy`): Li 2025 longdust arXiv:2509.07357 (overlapping `L‚àík+1` k-mers, `H=‚àíŒ£p·µ¢log‚ÇÇp·µ¢`, skewed‚áílow / uniform‚áíhigh) + √áakƒ±r 2025 Entropy‚ÄìRank Ratio arXiv:2511.05300 (same formula, base-2‚áíbits, single-nt max log‚ÇÇ4=2) + Shannon 1948 (bounds `0‚â§H‚â§log(k)`, deterministic‚áí0 / uniform‚áílog_b n); hand-derived oracles `ACGT` k=1‚Üí2.0 / `ACGT` k=2‚Üílog‚ÇÇ3‚âà1.5849625 / `ATATAT` k=2‚Üí0.9709505945 / `AAAA` k=2‚Üí0.0 / `AAACGT` k=2‚Üí1.9219280949 (=log‚ÇÇ5‚àí0.4) / `AC` k=5‚Üí0.0 (L<k); homopolymer‚áíH0, all-distinct‚áíH log‚ÇÇN; two API-shape ASSUMPTIONs (L<k‚Üí0; k<1‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException, null DnaSequence‚ÜíArgumentNullException, null/empty string‚Üí0), no source contradictions. **Same formula as [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `Entropy` field** (a second entry point, not a new measure) ‚Äî enriches that concept rather than adding a new one.
- [[seq-complex-window-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-COMPLEX-WINDOW-001 (**windowed sequence complexity** ‚Äî a **sliding-window** scan emitting a per-position `ComplexityPoint` *profile*, each window carrying a **Shannon entropy** of base composition and a **linguistic complexity** value; the **profiling / scanning** member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` family, distinct from the whole-sequence scalars LZ / DUST / k-entropy): Troyanskaya et al. 2002 *Bioinformatics* 18(5):679 (PMID 12050064, primary ‚Äî **complexity profiles** as a function of position; linguistic complexity = distinct-subword counts, suffix-tree linear-time) + Wikipedia "Linguistic sequence complexity" (Gabrielian & Bolshoy 1999 / Trifonov 1990 ‚Äî `U·µ¢ = V·µ¢ / min(4^i, N‚àíi+1)`, summation `LC = Œ£ V·µ¢ / Œ£ Vmax,i`, range 0<C<1) + Wikipedia "Shannon entropy" (Shannon 1948 ‚Äî `H = ‚àíŒ£ p log‚ÇÇ p` bits, uniform DNA max log‚ÇÇ4 = 2, deterministic ‚áí 0); hand-derived oracles `ACGTACGT` window ‚Üí Shannon **2.0** / LC **23/29 = 0.7931‚Ä¶**, `AAAAAAAA` poly-A window ‚Üí Shannon **0.0** / LC **6/29 = 0.2069‚Ä¶**, geometry L=24/w=8/s=8 ‚Üí **3** windows ([0,7]c4 / [8,15]c12 / [16,23]c20); window count `floor((L‚àíw)/s)+1` for L‚â•w else 0, only fully-contained windows emitted (no trailing partial), Position = `WindowStart + w/2`, bounds 0‚â§H‚â§2 / 0‚â§LC‚â§1; three ASSUMPTIONs (center-position label, default w=64/s=10, maxWordLength = min(6,w)), null‚ÜíArgumentNullException / w<1¬∑s<1‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException, no source contradictions. - [[seq-entropy-profile-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-ENTROPY-PROFILE-001 (**sliding-window Shannon entropy profile** ‚Äî per fixed-width window, `H = ‚àíŒ£ p·µ¢ log‚ÇÇ p·µ¢` bits over the window's **single-base (k=1) composition**; emitted as a standalone entropy profile). Enriches [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]].
- [[seq-gc-analysis-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001 (**Comprehensive GC analysis** ‚Äî the composite `GcAnalysisResult` bundling whole-sequence scalars OverallGcContent `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)√ó100` + OverallGcSkew `(G‚àíC)/(G+C)` + OverallAtSkew `(A‚àíT)/(A+T)` with a **sliding-window** GC%/GC-skew profile and the **population variance** `œÉ¬≤=Œ£(x·µ¢‚àíŒº)¬≤/N` of each windowed series). The overall scalars are already covered ‚Äî GC content on [[base-composition]], GC/AT skew on [[nucleotide-composition-skew]]; the genuinely-distinct windowed profile + compositional variance ‚Üí NEW concept [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]]. Oracles `GGGCCAT`‚ÜíGC% 71.428‚Ä¶/GC-skew 0.2/AT-skew 0.0; windowed `GGCC` w2s2‚Üíwindows GG(+1,100)/CC(‚àí1,100)‚Üí`GcSkewVariance` 1.0 / `GcContentVariance` 0.0; shorter-than-window ‚áí empty lists + variances 0, scalars still computed; no-G/C ‚áí skew 0/GC% 0. Two labelling/estimator ASSUMPTIONs (GC% √ó100 vs Biopython `[0,1]` fraction; window "variability" = population variance √∑N, not sample √∑N‚àí1), no source contradictions.
- [[seq-gc-profile-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-GC-PROFILE-001 (**sliding-window GC-content profile** ‚Äî per fully-contained window, `GC% = (G+C)/(A+T+G+C)√ó100`, GC% only, no skew profile and no variance). The **same windowed GC-content measure and window geometry** as the composite `GcAnalysisResult`'s GC-content channel (SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001) ‚Üí a **standalone entry point**, enriches [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] rather than adding a new concept. Sources: Wikipedia "GC-content" (`GC%=(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)√ó100%`, four-base denominator, undefined at A+T+G+C=0) + Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.gc_fraction` (`[0,1]` √ó100 = percentage, default `ambiguous="remove"` drops N from the length, doctests `ACTGN` remove‚Üí0.50 / ignore‚Üí0.40, RNA `GGAUCUUCGGAUCU`‚Üí0.50). Hand-derived window oracles (√ó100) `GGGG`‚Üí100.0 / `AAAA`‚Üí0.0 / `ATGC`‚Üí50.0 / `GGGA`‚Üí75.0 / `GCAT`‚Üí50.0 / `GGAN` (N excluded)‚Üí66.66666666666666; window count `‚åä(n‚àíw)/step‚åã+1`, offsets 0/step/2¬∑step, RNA U = non-GC, every window bounded `[0,100]`, `windowSize>length`/null/empty‚Üíempty profile, case-insensitive. One open ASSUMPTION (all-N window ‚áí A+T+G+C=0 division by zero ‚Üí GC% **0**, mirroring sibling `GcSkewCalculator`; not dictated by the external sources) ‚Äî the N-exclusion denominator is source-backed (`remove` mode), not assumed; no source contradictions. Enriches [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]].
- [[seq-hydro-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-HYDRO-001 (**hydrophobicity analysis** ‚Äî the whole-sequence **Kyte-Doolittle GRAVY index** `Œ£(kd value)/length` and the **sliding-window hydropathy profile**, exactly `N‚àíW+1` unweighted window means). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property unit ‚Üí NEW concept [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] (the whole-sequence-scalar + raw-profile sibling that the segment-calling [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] thresholds). Sources: Biopython `ProtParamData.py` kd scale (20 residues I 4.5‚Ä¶R ‚àí4.5, Kyte & Doolittle 1982) + `ProtParam.py` (`gravy()` = total/length, `protein_scale` loop `range(N‚àíW+1)`, default `edge=1.0` = unweighted mean) + Expasy ProtParam (GRAVY = Œ£ hydropathy √∑ residues; positive ‚áí hydrophobic) + GCAT/Davidson (window 9 surface, window 19 transmembrane peaks > 1.6) + alakazam (CRAN) `gravy`. Hand-derived oracles `A`‚Üí1.8 / `AG`‚Üí0.7 / `FLIV`‚Üí3.825 / `RKDE`‚Üí‚àí3.85; window-3 `FLIV`‚Üí[3.7, 4.1666666667], `AG` (W>N)‚Üíempty; case-insensitive, empty/null ‚Üí 0/empty. One documented deviation (unknown residues **skipped** ‚Äî GRAVY √∑ recognized count, profile treats as 0 ‚Äî vs Biopython `gravy()` `KeyError`; neither mandated by the kd sources, in-alphabet values stay exactly source-conformant, algorithm doc ¬ß5.4); no source contradictions.

- [[seq-mw-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-MW-001 (**molecular weight calculation** ‚Äî the average-isotopic **molecular mass in Daltons** of a **protein, DNA or RNA** sequence via one shared polymerization formula). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* whole-sequence-scalar unit (mass, spanning all three molecule types) ‚Üí NEW concept [[molecular-weight]], the mass-weighted sibling of the [[base-composition]] tally and of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] GRAVY scalar. Formula fully sourced: Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.molecular_weight` (`weight = Œ£ weight_table[x] ‚àí (len‚àí1)¬∑water`, one water removed per bond ‚Äî peptide for protein, phosphodiester for nucleic acid; `water = 18.0153` avg / `18.010565` monoisotopic; single monomer ‚áí free-monomer mass, circular ‚áí ‚àíone more water, double-strand adds the complement strand, **error for protein**; "only unambiguous letters", nucleotides assumed 5'-phosphate) + Biopython `IUPACData` average tables ("from PubChem": protein *free-amino-acid* A 89.0932‚Ä¶G 75.0666‚Ä¶W 204.2252; DNA *monophosphate* A 331.2218/C 307.1971/G 347.2212/T 322.2085; RNA A 347.2212/C 323.1965/G 363.2206/U 324.1813) + Expasy Compute pI/Mw (protein Mw = "addition of average isotopic masses of amino acids ... and ... one water molecule", Da ‚Äî algebraically = `Œ£ free-amino-acid ‚àí (len‚àí1)¬∑water`) + Expasy ProtParam (delegates to Compute pI/Mw) + Expasy FindMod (residue-mass table + H‚ÇÇO 18.01524). Re-derived oracles (avg tables, water 18.0153) `AGC`‚Üíprotein **249.29** / DNA **949.61** / RNA **997.61** (Biopython docstring), single monomer (zero bonds ‚áí free-monomer mass) `G`‚Üí**75.0666** / `A` DNA‚Üí**331.2218** / `A` RNA‚Üí**347.2212**; empty/null‚Üí0. One documented deviation (unknown/ambiguous symbols **skipped** ‚Äî contribute no mass and no bond, reflecting only recognized monomers, no invented average ‚Äî whereas Biopython *rejects* them; the SEQ-\* skip-unknown convention, an API-shape choice, in-alphabet values stay exactly source-conformant) + two API-shape assumptions (ToUpperInvariant case-fold; the skip resolution); no source contradictions (Expasy/Biopython agree on formula and average-mass tables to rounding). Note MW pairs with pI in the Expasy source but **pI/charge is a separate calculation not in this unit**.
- [[seq-pi-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-PI-001 (**isoelectric point (pI)** ‚Äî the **pH at which a protein's net charge is zero**, found by bisecting the Henderson‚ÄìHasselbalch net-charge function over [0,14]). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property scalar (a charge/pH calculation, not mass or hydropathy) ‚Üí NEW concept [[isoelectric-point]], the ExPASy Compute pI/Mw partner of [[molecular-weight]]. Charge model fully sourced: Osorio et al. 2015 Peptides `charge_pI.cpp` (net charge `Œ£_basic +1/(1+10^(pH‚àípKa)) + Œ£_acidic ‚àí1/(1+10^(pKa‚àípH))`, Moore 1985; basic {R,K,H,N-term} / acidic {D,E,C,Y,C-term}, both termini once) + EMBOSS `iep` (pI = net-charge-zero pH, `Epk.dat` scale N-term 8.6/C-term 3.6/C 8.5/D 3.9/E 4.1/H 6.5/K 10.8/R 12.5/Y 10.1, [0,14] bracket, "no electrostatic interactions" ‚áí composition-only/order-independent) + Peptides `charge()` (nine pKa scales; EMBOSS worked example `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC` net charge 3.037398/2.914112/0.7184524 @ pH 5/7/9) + seqinr `computePI` + ExPASy Compute pI/Mw (Bjellqvist 1993 scale; small/highly-basic-protein accuracy caveat; pairs pI with Mw). Derived-pI oracles (EMBOSS, bisection ¬±0.01): `A`/`AG`‚Üí6.10 (termini-only midpoint), `D`‚Üí3.75, `K`‚Üí9.70, `DDDD`‚Üí3.23, `KKKK`‚Üí11.27, `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC`‚Üí9.67 (basic), `ACDEFGHIKLMNPQRSTVWY`‚Üí7.36 (EMBOSS ‚âÝ seqinr Bjellqvist 6.78454 ‚Äî scale-dependent). Two assumptions (empty/null‚Üí7.0 input-guard; pKa scale = EMBOSS, a parameter choice not a deviation), pI‚àà[0,14] invariant, no source contradictions.
- [[seq-secstruct-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-SECSTRUCT-001 (**protein secondary structure prediction** ‚Äî the **Chou-Fasman (1974/1978) PŒ±/PŒ≤/Pt conformational propensities** evaluated as a generic **sliding-window mean-propensity profile**: for a window `W`, the arithmetic mean of each of the Œ±-helix/Œ≤-sheet/Œ≤-turn propensities over each window). Genuinely distinct SEQ-\* protein-property unit ‚Üí NEW concept [[protein-secondary-structure-chou-fasman]] (the conformational-propensity analogue of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] hydropathy profile, sharing the exact `N‚àíW+1` unweighted window-mean mechanism). Sources: Wikipedia Chou‚ÄìFasman (rank 4; nucleation rules 4-of-6-helix threshold 1.03 / 3-of-5-sheet 1.00 / turn ‚àèp_t cutoff 7.5e-3; ~50‚Äì60% Q3 / 29-protein caveat) + Kelley bioinfo lecture (rank 4; helix STEP 1‚Äì4 state machine, worked A 142/83 E 151/37) + CSB|SJU Jakubowski (rank 4; **Lys PŒ± 1.16**) + Przytycka NCBI lecture (rank 4; **Lys 1.14 0.74 1.01**) + ravihansa3000/ChouFasman reference impl (rank 3; full 20-residue Pa/Pb/Pt integer table, **Lys 114**) + BMC Bioinformatics PMC1780123 (rank 1, peer-reviewed; restates rules, helix ‚ü®PŒ±‚ü©>1.03 & >‚ü®PŒ≤‚ü©). Hand-derived oracles: single-residue window = that residue's tuple (A 1.42/0.83/0.66, E 1.51/0.37/0.74, V 1.06/1.70/0.50, N 0.67/0.89/1.56, K 1.14/0.74/1.01); `AE` W2 ‚Üí helix 1.465 / sheet 0.60 / turn 0.70; `AEV` W3 ‚Üí helix 1.330 / sheet 0.9666‚Ä¶ / turn 0.6333‚Ä¶; `AXE` W3 averages only A+E; N‚àíW+1 windows in N-terminus order, case-insensitive, W>N/non-positive/null/empty ‚Üí empty. Three assumptions (the method under test is the generic **profile not** the nucleation/extension state machine, so default `W=7` is an API convenience not a CF constant; unknown residues **skip-and-excluded**; the **only contested value Lys PŒ± resolved to 1.14** ‚Äî two independent sources incl. the reference impl vs a single 1.16), no contradictions on the 19 uncontested residues.
- [[seq-stats-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-STATS-001 (**the ORIGINAL sequence-composition umbrella** ‚Äî nucleotide composition A/T/G/C/U/N/Other + Length, **GC content** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)`, **GC skew** `(G‚àíC)/(G+C)` and **AT skew** `(A‚àíT)/(A+T)`; also `SummarizeNucleotideSequence` aggregator + `CalculateAminoAcidComposition`). - [[seq-summary-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-SUMMARY-001 (**`SummarizeNucleotideSequence` ‚Äî the per-sequence summary record**: bundles Length, nucleotide Composition (A/T/G/C/U/N), **GcContent** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)`, **Shannon Entropy** `‚àíŒ£p·µ¢log‚ÇÇp·µ¢` bits, **linguistic Complexity**, and **MeltingTemperature** (Wallace len<14 / GC-Marmur-Doty len‚â•14) into one object). - [[seq-thermo-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-THERMO-001 (**DNA duplex thermodynamics** ‚Äî the full nearest-neighbor **ŒîH¬∞/ŒîS¬∞/ŒîG¬∞/Tm** 4-tuple of a Watson-Crick DNA duplex, a port of Biopython `Tm_NN` over the **DNA_NN3 / Allawi & SantaLucia 1997** table). - [[seq-tm-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-TM-001 (**`CalculateMeltingTemperature` ‚Äî the standalone scalar melting temperature**, length-dispatched at `ThermoConstants.WallaceMaxLength = 14` between the **Wallace rule** `4(G+C)+2(A+T)` for short oligos and the **Marmur-Doty GC formula** `64.9+41¬∑(GC‚àí16.4)/N` for len‚â•14). One ASSUMPTION (14-nt dispatch boundary, non-correctness-affecting under explicit flag) + NN-facet default C_T assumption + repo-vs-Biopython Marmur-Doty constant variant (64.9/‚àí672.4 vs 69.3/‚àí650); no source contradictions. Resolves the "SEQ-TM-001 remains un-ingested / natural home for Wallace/Marmur" follow-up flagged by the SEQ-SUMMARY-001 and SEQ-THERMO-001 ingests.
- [[seq-replication-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-REPLICATION-001 (**replication origin prediction via the cumulative GC-skew minimum** ‚Äî the classic ori-finder: integrate an *integer* running skew (G:+1, C:‚àí1, A/T:0, `Skew_0=0`, prefix indices `[0,n]`) and read origin off the global **minimum**, terminus off the **maximum**): Rosalind BA1F Minimum Skew Problem (rank 3, canonical worked example ‚Äî 100-nt sample min ‚àí4 @ positions **53, 97**, re-derived in-session exactly) + Grigoriev 1998 *Nucleic Acids Res* 26(10):2286 (rank 1 ‚Äî cumulative diagram min=origin/max=terminus, extrema ‚âà half chromosome apart, leading strand G-rich) + Lobry 1996 (PMID 8676740 ‚Äî skew sign flips at origin/terminus) + Wikipedia "GC skew" (max=terminal/min=origin); diagram oracles `CCGGGG`‚Üí`0,‚àí1,‚àí2,‚àí1,0,+1,+2` (min ‚àí2 @2/max +2 @6), `GGGCCC`‚Üí`0,+1,+2,+3,+2,+1,0`, `AATT`‚Üíflat; `PredictedOrigin=53` first-minimizer tie-break; one documented ASSUMPTION ‚Äî `IsSignificant` redefined threshold-free as `max>min` (invented `amplitude>count√ó0.01` constant **removed**), flat diagram ‚áí origin=terminus=0/false; no source contradictions. - [[seq-rnacomp-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SEQ-RNACOMP-001 (**RNA-specific per-base complement** ‚Äî `GetRnaComplementBase`, the IUPAC-complete RNA complement map; **RNACOMP ‚âÝ composition**, this is complement chemistry, not the [[base-composition]] tally). **No new concept** ‚Äî enriched [[rna-base-pairing]] (which already owns the RNA base complement `GetComplement`, RNA-PAIR-001): added a *SEQ-family full-IUPAC RNA complement* subsection. Same chemistry as `RnaSecondaryStructure.GetComplement` but IUPAC-complete (A‚ÜíU/U‚ÜíA/G‚ÜíC/C‚ÜíG, **T‚ÜíA** treating DNA T as U; reciprocal R‚ÜîY/M‚ÜîK/D‚ÜîH/B‚ÜîV; self-complementary W/S/X/N; non-IUPAC pass-through). One deviation: recognized bases returned **uppercase** (repo convention vs Biopython case-preserving) ‚Äî casing only, complement identity unchanged; no source contradictions.
- [[splice-acceptor-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-ACCEPTOR-001 (**acceptor / 3' splice site detection** ‚Äî score candidate `AG` dinucleotides for the three cis-elements of a real 3'ss under the canonical **GU-AG rule**). First ingested member of the **splicing** family ‚Üí NEW concept [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]. Three scoring surfaces: default `FindAcceptorSites` (**AcceptorPwm** PWM + PPT-quality, `(score/(count+1)+2)/4` [0,1] heuristic; weights from Shapiro & Senapathy 1987), opt-in `FindAcceptorBranchPoint` (18‚Äì40 nt window for the human **`yUnAy`** consensus, Gao 2008 conservation y@‚àí3 0.790/U@‚àí2 0.746/A@0 0.923/y@+1 0.751, found ‚â• 0.8¬∑3.210; Mercer 2015 corroboration), opt-in **MaxEntScan score3ss** `ScoreAcceptorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 23-nt max-entropy model; MIT-licensed maxentpy 82,560-record tables `Data/maxent_score3.txt`; canonical `ttccaaacgaacttttgtAGgga`‚Üí**2.89** cross-check, +8.19/‚àí0.08); U12 **YCCAC** non-canonical scoring (Hall & Padgett 1994). Corner cases: < 20 nt ‚Üí empty guard, no-AG ‚Üí empty, cryptic intronic AG decoys, weak PPT skipped. All prior assumptions RESOLVED (PWM weights verified, normalization = design choice, branch-point constants source-traceable). Licence flag: bundled MaxEntScan table is the MIT port, not the academic-terms Burge-lab Perl. No source contradictions.
- [[splice-donor-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-DONOR-001 (**donor / 5' splice site detection** ‚Äî score candidate `GT/GU` dinucleotides for the almost-invariant `GU` intron start under the canonical **GU-AG rule**). Donor member of the **splicing** family ‚Üí NEW concept [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] (5' partner of [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]). Single contiguous **`MAG|GURAGU`** consensus (‚àí3..+6; 0-G/+1-U ~100%, ‚àí1-G ~80% for U1 snRNP; **no branch point / PPT** ‚Äî asymmetric with the acceptor). Two surfaces only: default **IUPAC consensus match-fraction** `FindDonorSites`/`ScoreDonorSite` (plainer than the acceptor PWM+PPT; GC donors self-penalize via the +1-U mismatch 8/9<9/9, old 0.7 penalty removed), opt-in **MaxEntScan score5ss** `ScoreDonorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 9-nt window, **single 16,384-entry table, no overlapping sub-windows** vs score3's 82,560 records; canonical `cagGTAAGT`‚Üí**10.86**, +11.08/‚àí0.12). GC-AG (~0.5‚Äì1%) + U12 **AT-AC**/`ATATCC` non-canonical donors. Corner cases: < 9 nt ‚Üí empty, no GT/GU ‚Üí empty, cryptic donors. All prior assumptions RESOLVED (PWM‚ÜíIUPAC binary weights, normalization‚Üímatch fraction, GC penalty removed). Licence flag: bundled MaxEntScan table is the MIT port, not the academic-terms Burge-lab Perl. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-breakpoint-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SV-BREAKPOINT-001 (**breakpoint detection from split / soft-clipped reads**). First ingested member of the **germline structural-variant (SV)** family ‚Üí NEW concept [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]]. Localize an SV breakpoint to a single base at the aligned/clipped **junction** of a split read: the SAM/BAM CIGAR **soft clip `S` consumes the read (SEQ) but not the reference** and sits only at a read end ‚Üí **leading `S` = left / trailing `S` = right breakpoint** (ClipCrop "marginal point between clipped and matched sequence"; L/R-breakpoints; a no-`S` read = no signal). **Cluster** per-read junctions under three source-backed constraints ‚Äî positional **tolerance** (ClipCrop "clustered within 5-base differences", 5 b), **minimum support** (SoftSearch ‚â• x soft-clipped reads at a position, default 5 / configurable 2; support = # clipped reads in cluster), and **same clip-side + same chromosome** ‚Äî with a **min clip length** filter (‚â§ 5 clipped bases dropped) and `RefineBreakpoint`. Repository `SplitRead` record: `PrimaryPosition` = anchored SAM POS / `SupplementaryPosition` = junction coordinate / `ClipLength`. Oracles: 3 reads @ 5000 ¬± ‚â§ 5 b, same chr, support ‚â• 2 ‚Üí one breakpoint ~5000; 1 isolated read ‚Üí none; 5000 vs 5100 (gap > tolerance) ‚Üí two below-support groups ‚Üí none. Sources: SAM/BAM spec (samtools/hts-specs, rank 2 ‚Äî CIGAR consume table / POS / S-at-ends) + Tattini-Magi 2015 review (rank 1 ‚Äî anchored+imprecise split read, single-base resolution, clustering) + ClipCrop Suzuki 2011 (rank 1 ‚Äî junction=breakpoint, 5-b clustering, L/R) + SoftSearch Hart 2013 (rank 1 ‚Äî ‚â• x clipped reads, orientation combining, min clip > 5). One ASSUMPTION (cluster reported coordinate = rounded **mean** of member junctions, sub-tolerance only, mirroring sibling `ClusterSplitReads`); operates on already-extracted `SplitRead` records, not raw BAM. Orthogonal to the oncology read-evidence [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] / [[chromothripsis-inference]]. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-cnv-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SV-CNV-001 (**read-depth copy-number variation detection**).
