The **read-depth-segmentation member of the germline structural-variant (SV) family** ‚Üí NEW concept [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]] (a distinct method from the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] ‚Äî aggregate **read depth of coverage**, not per-read junctions). Pipeline: **read depth ‚àù copy number** (Yoon 2009) ‚Üí **windowed counting** (non-overlapping fixed-size windows, one read per start position, per-window mean RD) ‚Üí optional **GC correction** `r_i' = r_i¬∑m/m_GC` ‚Üí **log2 ratio** `log2(observed depth / reference depth)` (reference = overall median of window means when no baseline given) ‚Üí **integer CN = round(2¬∑2^log2)** (CNVkit "round" method, diploid ploidy 2) ‚Üí **del/dup call** + segment merge (`DetectCNV`/`SegmentCopyNumber`). Diploid anchors (verbatim CNVkit): 0.5√ó‚Üílog2 ‚àí1.0‚ÜíCN 1 (Deletion), 1.0√ó‚Üí0‚ÜíCN 2 (Neutral), 1.5√ó‚Üí+0.585‚ÜíCN 3 (Duplication/gain), 2.0√ó‚Üí+1.0‚ÜíCN 4 (amp). Corner cases: **zero-depth window ‚Üí no-call** (log2(0)=‚àí‚àû undefined, homozygous-deletion candidate, not ‚àí‚àû); **NaN log2 ‚Üí Neutral (CN 2)**; CN clamped **‚â• 0**. Sources: Yoon 2009 (Genome Res, rank 1 ‚Äî RD‚àùCN, windowed counting, GC formula) + CNVkit `call.py` + calling docs (rank 3 ‚Äî `n=ref_copies¬∑2^log2`, anchors log2(1/2)=‚àí1 / log2(3/2)=0.585, `max(0,ncopies)` clamp, `nan`‚Üíneutral). Two ASSUMPTIONs (reference baseline = overall median of non-zero window means; diploid ploidy 2), both source-supported. The oncology [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) is the classification layer *on top of* this same log2 ratio (swaps `round` for hard-threshold binning into 5 CNA states). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[sv-detect-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SV-DETECT-001 (**structural-variant detection from paired-end mapping (PEM) signatures** ‚Äî discordant read pairs). The **discordant-read-pair member of the germline structural-variant (SV) family** ‚Üí NEW concept [[discordant-pair-sv-detection]] (a third read-evidence channel, orthogonal to the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] and the depth-based [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]]). Read how a mate pair's mapped **span + orientation** deviate from the concordant **FR** proper pair (SAM FLAG 0x02; **RF is everted/discordant**, not proper) and classify the SV type: span `> Œº+c¬∑œÉ` (FR, same chr) ‚Üí **Deletion**, span `< Œº‚àíc¬∑œÉ` ‚Üí **Insertion**, **FF/RR** ‚Üí **Inversion**, everted **RF** ‚Üí **tandem Duplication**, mates on **different chromosomes** ‚Üí **Translocation**. Span cutoff = `c` s.d. of the empirical insert-size distribution (BreakDancer `-c`, default 3 ‚áí mean=400/sd=50 ‚áí bounds [250,550]); **signature-then-cluster** with **min support** ‚â• `-r` pairs (default 2). Corner cases: an insertion larger than the insert size is invisible to PEM span and its sequence is not recovered (split-read channel's job); below-support clusters dropped; cutoff bounds exact. One ASSUMPTION ‚Äî inter-chromosomal (translocation) precedence evaluated **before** orientation (inversion defined only for intra-chromosomal flipped pairs). Sources: Medvedev/Stanciu/Brudno 2009 (Nat Methods, rank 1 ‚Äî signature catalogue) + BreakDancer README + protocol (Chen 2009 / Fan 2014 ‚Äî s.d. cutoff, min support, DEL/INS/INV/ITX/CTX codes) + SAM/BWA proper-pair FR convention (cureffi/FLAG 0x02) + DELLY 2012 / SVXplorer 2020 (orientation‚Üítype: RF=dup, FF/RR=inv). Consumes already-mapped read-pair records, not raw BAM; research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-diff-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-DIFF-001 (**two-group RNA-seq differential expression** ‚Äî log2 fold change + Welch's t-test + Benjamini-Hochberg FDR). **First ingested unit of the Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** ‚Üí NEW concept [[differential-expression]]. `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateFoldChange` / `FindDifferentiallyExpressed`: **log2FC** `log2((mean(treatment)+c)/(mean(control)+c))` (pseudocount c=1, positive = up in treatment, DESeq2 Love 2014 + Science Park lesson) + a **Welch unequal-variance t-test** raw p `t=(XÃÑ‚ÇÇ‚àíXÃÑ‚ÇÅ)/‚àö(s‚ÇÅ¬≤/N‚ÇÅ+s‚ÇÇ¬≤/N‚ÇÇ)`, unbiased (N‚àí1) variances, Welch-Satterthwaite df, exact Student-t tail `p=I_{ŒΩ/(ŒΩ+t¬≤)}(ŒΩ/2,¬Ω)` via regularized incomplete beta (Welch 1947) + **Benjamini-Hochberg FDR** reproducing R `p.adjust(method="BH")` `pmin(1,cummin(n/i¬∑p[o]))[ro]` (BH 1995). DE ‚áî **two-criterion gate** `|log2FC| ‚â• threshold (default 1.0) AND adjusted p < alpha (default 0.05)`. Oracles: UP `log2(41/11)=+1.8981204‚Ä¶` / DOWN ‚àí1.8981204‚Ä¶ / FLAT 0; Welch {1,2,3} vs {7,8,9} ‚Üí t=7.348469, ŒΩ=4, p=0.0018262607 (SciPy cross-check); BH raw (0.001,0.4,0.5,0.9) ‚Üí adj (0.004,0.6667,0.6667,0.9). Corner cases: <2 replicates ‚Üí p=1; se=0 ‚Üí p=1 (equal means)/p=0 (unequal); zero mean ‚Üí pseudocount. Three source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (pseudocount 1, <2-replicate p=1, se=0 conventions). A **simple two-group** estimator, **not** the full DESeq2 negative-binomial GLM. `alternative_to` the rank-sum [[significant-taxa-detection]] (no built-in FDR); DE gene lists feed [[pathway-enrichment-ora]]. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-expr-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-EXPR-001 (**RNA-seq expression quantification** ‚Äî TPM / FPKM / RPKM + quantile normalization). **Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** sibling of the anchor [[differential-expression]] ‚Üí NEW concept [[expression-quantification]] (a distinct quantification/normalization method, upstream of the DE test). `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateTPM` / `CalculateFPKM` / `QuantileNormalize`: **TPM** `(X_i/l_i)/Œ£(X_j/l_j)¬∑10‚Å∂` (length-normalize into RPK **then** rescale so each sample **sums to exactly 10‚Å∂** ‚Äî the invariant RPKM lacks; Wagner 2012, Zhao/Ye/Stanton 2020); **FPKM/RPKM** `X_i¬∑10‚Åπ/(l_i¬∑N)` (per-kb + per-million-reads; RPKM‚â°FPKM formula; `TPM=FPKM/Œ£ FPKM¬∑10‚Å∂`); **quantile normalization** (Bolstad 2003 ‚Äî sort each column, set each rank to the cross-column rank mean, re-place; **tied values get the mean of the rank means they'd span**). Oracles: TPM A(10,2000)/B(20,4000)/C(30,1000) ‚Üí **(125000,125000,750000)** sum 10‚Å∂; FPKM X=1000,l=2000,N=10‚Å∂ ‚Üí **500**; quantile C1=(5,2,3,4)/C2=(4,1,4,2)/C3=(3,4,6,8) ‚Üí C2's two tied `4`s ‚Üí **5.166‚Ä¶** (mean of top-two rank means 4.666‚Ä¶/5.666‚Ä¶). Corner cases: all-zero counts ‚Üí TPM 0/0 undefined ‚Üí emit 0; non-positive length/N ‚Üí FPKM 0; empty ‚Üí empty. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (all-zero TPM ‚Üí 0; effective length = annotated length). Classic count-normalization, **not** an effective-length fragment model (kallisto/salmon) or TMM/median-of-ratios size factors (edgeR/DESeq2). TPM/RPKM are within-sample relative measures ‚Äî misused across samples (Zhao 2020). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[trans-splice-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit TRANS-SPLICE-001 (**RNA-seq alternative / differential splicing** ‚Äî event classification + Percent-Spliced-In / PSI). **Transcriptome / RNA-seq family** sibling of the anchor [[differential-expression]] ‚Üí NEW concept [[alternative-splicing-psi]] (read-quantification of splicing usage ‚Äî **distinct from** the genomic splice-site motif predictors [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] / [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] / [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]]). `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculatePSI` / `DetectAlternativeSplicing`: **PSI** `Œ® = I/(I+S)` (inclusion / (inclusion+exclusion) reads; Wang 2008, PMC3330053, SUPPA2) with opt-in **rMATS length-normalized** `œàÃÇ = (I/l·µ¢)/(I/l·µ¢ + S/l‚Çõ)` (Shen 2014, effective isoform lengths) ‚Üí default unnormalized, switches to rMATS when both lengths > 0; **ŒîPSI** = splicing-level differential readout. **Five canonical AS classes** (Wang 2008 = rMATS codes): SkippedExon (SE), RetainedIntron (RI), AlternativeFivePrimeSS (A5SS, alternative **donor** = moving 3‚Ä≤/END boundary of upstream exon), AlternativeThreePrimeSS (A3SS, alternative **acceptor** = moving 5‚Ä≤/START boundary of downstream exon), MutuallyExclusiveExons (MXE); an event needs **‚â•2 isoforms** of one gene. Oracles: (I=80,S=20) ‚Üí **0.80**; (80,20,l·µ¢=200,l‚Çõ=100) ‚Üí **0.6666‚Ä¶**. Corner cases: **0/0 ‚Üí NaN**, S=0 ‚Üí PSI 1, I=0 ‚Üí PSI 0, `0 ‚â§ PSI ‚â§ 1`, <2 isoforms ‚Üí no event. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (length normalization opt-in; forward strand / ascending coords). The splicing-level counterpart to the gene-level [[differential-expression]] ‚Äî a gene can be differentially spliced without changing total expression. Read-count ratio + coordinate comparison, **not** the full rMATS/SUPPA2 replicate statistics. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[splice-predict-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit SPLICE-PREDICT-001 (**gene structure prediction ‚Äî intron/exon**), the **composite / umbrella** of the **splicing** family ‚Üí NEW concept [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]]. Assembles the two boundary detectors into a whole split-gene model: find donors (`GT/GU`) + acceptors (`AG`) ‚Üí **pair** into introns under the **GT-AG rule** (Breathnach & Chambon 1981 `MAG|GURAGU` / `(Y)nNCAG|G`; Burge 1999 "each donor pairs with exactly one acceptor") bounded by `minIntronLength` (default 60) / `maxIntronLength` ‚Üí **greedy non-overlapping** selection ‚Üí exons = the gaps ‚Üí **type** each exon (Initial/Internal/Terminal/Single, Gilbert 1978) + **phase** = `(Œ£ preceding exon lengths) mod 3` (Alberts 2002) ‚Üí emit **spliced sequence** + **overall score** = mean of per-intron `(donor+acceptor)/2`, [0,1]. Datasets: D1 two-exon 153 nt ‚Üí 1 intron/2 exons/70-nt spliced, D2 single-exon 50 nt ‚Üí Single, D3 empty ‚Üí 0/0. Corner cases: 30-bp introns excluded by default min=60, no sites ‚Üí single-exon, DNA T‚â°U. All 4 assumptions RESOLVED (greedy=design decision, phase=trivial, overall-score=definition, **default branch-point 0.3 constant removed**). No source contradictions.
- [[variant-annot-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-ANNOT-001 (**variant annotation** ‚Äî VEP-style functional consequence + Sequence-Ontology IMPACT). The **interpretation / annotation** member of the variant-analysis family ‚Üí NEW concept [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]] (downstream of variant calling [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]], orthogonal to pathogenicity/tier classification). Ensembl **OverlapConsequence predicate system**: `Constants.pm` consequence‚ÜíIMPACT‚Üírank table (**IMPACT stored on the term, not computed**; frameshift HIGH / missense MODERATE / synonymous LOW / intron MODIFIER) + `VariationEffect.pm` peptide predicates; **most-severe = lowest rank** (McLaren 2016 "most specific term under any parent"). The coding engine **translates ref/alt codons** through [[genetic-code-translation]] (NCBI Standard code table 1) and compares peptides: `synonymous` (ref_pep==alt_pep, no `X`, not stop_retained) / `missense` (differ, same length; false if start_lost/stop_lost/stop_gained/partial_codon) / `stop_gained` (alt gains `*`) / `stop_lost` (ref loses `*`) / **`frameshift` purely length-based `|alt‚àíref| mod 3 ‚âÝ 0`** / inframe ins-del (√ó3). Precedence stop_gained>missense, start_lost(rank 7)>coding-substitution. Oracles GAA‚ÜíGTA missense/MODERATE ¬∑ TTA‚ÜíTTG synonymous/LOW ¬∑ CAA‚ÜíTAA stop_gained/HIGH ¬∑ TAA‚ÜíCAA stop_lost/HIGH ¬∑ ATG‚ÜíATC start_lost/HIGH ¬∑ AC‚ÜíA frameshift ¬∑ A‚ÜíATTT inframe_insertion. Sources McLaren 2016 (PMC4893825) + Ensembl Constants.pm/VariationEffect.pm (release/110) + NCBI gc.prt + Sequence Ontology (Eilbeck 2005). Two assumptions (Standard code table 1 only; single-codon SNV peptide comparison). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-call-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-CALL-001 (**variant calling** ‚Äî SNP/insertion/deletion detection from a reference‚Üîquery alignment + transition/transversion + Ti/Tv). The **calling / detection** member of the variant-analysis family ‚Üí NEW concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] (**upstream of** annotation [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]]; the germline reference‚Üîquery counterpart of the oncology tumor-vs-normal caller [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]]). `CallVariantsFromAlignment` runs `SequenceAligner.GlobalAlign(reference,query)` and walks aligned columns: **SNP** (both bases differ), **Insertion** (`-`/base), **Deletion** (base/`-`), 0-based `Position` + `"-"` gap sentinel (in-memory model; VCF padding + 1-based POS only in serialized `ToVcfLines`). SNPs classified case-insensitively **Transition** (A‚ÜîG, C‚ÜîT) vs **Transversion** (A‚ÜîC/A‚ÜîT/G‚ÜîC/G‚ÜîT); **Ti/Tv = #Ti/#Tv**, undefined `#Tv=0` ‚Üí **0** by convention; non-SNP ‚Üí `Other`. Sources VCFv4.3 (samtools/hts-specs ‚Äî REF/ALT/POS + padding-base grammar, ¬ß1.1 `G‚ÜíA` SNP / `GTC‚ÜíG` 2-base del / `GTC‚ÜíGTCT` 1-base ins) + Danecek 2011 (VCF classes) + Tan 2015 (normalized ‚ü∫ left-aligned+parsimonious) + Collins & Jukes 1994 (transitional bias, Ti rate > Tv rate). Three assumptions (gap-sentinel internal rep; indels **not** normalized ‚Üí position-only implementation-dependence in repeats; Ti/Tv zero ‚Üí 0). Alignment-based (single query vs reference), **not** a read-pileup genotype caller. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-INDEL-001 (**indel detection** ‚Äî `FindInsertions` / `FindDeletions`, the insertion/deletion facet of the aligned-column caller). **Enriches** (does not fork) the concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] ‚Äî the indel facet of the same VARIANT-CALL-001 caller, not a separate algorithm. `FindInsertions`/`FindDeletions` are **filters over `CallVariants`** returning only their class (insertion column `-`/base, deletion column base/`-`); a multi-base indel = **consecutive per-base indel columns**. Load-bearing claim = the **directional length invariant**: **insertion ‚áí ALT longer than REF** (VCF `C‚ÜíCA`), **deletion ‚áí REF longer than ALT** (VCF `TC‚ÜíT`); VCFv4.3 ¬ß1.1 `GTC‚ÜíG,GTCT` shows both anchored at `G`. Normalization theory (Tan 2015 **normalized ‚ü∫ left-aligned + parsimonious**; Algorithm 1 = suffix-then-prefix trimming) documents the ASM: the caller reports the indel at the `GlobalAlign` column with **no** normalization pass, so **position** is implementation-dependent in repeats/low-complexity only (PharmCAT `AATGA‚ÜíA`@97740414 ‚áí `GATGA‚ÜíG`@97740410, same count/type), **not** counts or types. Reference oracles: `ATGCAT`‚Üí`ATGTCAT` = 1-base insertion `T`; `ATGTCAT`‚Üí`ATGCAT` = 1-base deletion `T`; minimal_representation CFTR p.F508del `(7,117199646,CTT,-)‚Üí(...,ATCT,A)` + BRCA2 `(13,32914438,T,-)‚Üí(...,GT,G)` confirm deletion ‚áí len(REF)>len(ALT) + left-anchor padding. Three assumptions (gap-sentinel internal rep; indels not normalized ‚Üí position-only in repeats; 0-based in-memory Position). Sources VCFv4.3 + Tan 2015 (PMID 25701572) + minimal_representation (Minikel) + PharmCAT. Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.
- [[variant-snp-001-evidence]] ‚Äî evidence artifact for test unit VARIANT-SNP-001 (**SNP detection** ‚Äî `FindSnps` / `FindSnpsDirect`, the single-nucleotide-substitution facet of the aligned-column caller). **Enriches** (does not fork) the concept [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] ‚Äî the SNP facet of the same VARIANT-CALL-001 caller, not a separate algorithm (mirrors how [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] folded in the indel facet). Two entry points, **substitution columns only** (no indels): **`FindSnps`** = alignment-based filter over the caller (keeps columns where both bases differ, `Type=SNP`); **`FindSnpsDirect`** = positional / **Hamming-style** ‚Äî over two **equal-length** sequences it enumerates exactly the **Hamming-mismatch positions** (Acharya 2017, PMC5410656) and the SNP count equals the **Hamming distance**. Each SNP: `Position=i` (0-based mismatched index), `ReferenceAllele=ref[i]`, `AlternateAllele=query[i]`, `ref[i]‚âÝquery[i]` (**REF==ALT is not a variant**). Load-bearing scope claim = the **equal-length precondition**: `FindSnpsDirect` on unequal-length inputs compares only the **common prefix** `min(ref.Length,query.Length)` ‚Äî the trailing region is indel territory (VARIANT-INDEL-001), never a SNP. Identical sequences ‚Üí 0 SNPs (Hamming distance 0); comparison + Ti/Tv classification **case-insensitive** (VCFv4.3 REF alphabet A,C,G,T,N). Oracles: `ATGC`‚Üí`ATTC`={2} (G‚ÜíT) ¬∑ `AAAA`‚Üí`TGTA`={0,1,2} ¬∑ VCFv4.3 ¬ß1.1 simple SNP `G‚ÜíA`@14370. Two assumptions (unequal-length ‚Üí common prefix; 0-based in-memory Position). Sources VCFv4.3 + Wikipedia/Futuyma Transversion + Acharya 2017 (PMC5410656, Hamming) + Collins & Jukes 1994 (transitional bias). Research-grade, not for clinical use. No source contradictions.

## Concepts

- [[three-front-doors]] ‚Äî one algorithm engine exposed through skills, the C# API, and MCP, with identical results.
- [[skill-layer]] ‚Äî the Agent-Skill routing + discipline layer that keeps 427 tool schemas out of the model's context.
- [[layered-architecture]] ‚Äî the strict up-only dependency layering (Levels 0‚Äì4) enforced by architecture tests.
- [[scientific-rigor]] ‚Äî runtime honesty: `LimitationPolicy`, tool-only computation, provenance on every result.
- [[validation-and-testing]] ‚Äî 22k+ tests across ten methodologies plus the per-unit validation campaign.
- [[validation-findings-disposition]] ‚Äî the A/B/C/D triage governance process for validation findings, with green-washing detection and the spec-not-impl remedy.
- [[operating-envelope-and-limitation-policy]] ‚Äî the validated operating envelope + the `LimitationPolicy` runtime guard (Strict/Moderate/Permissive, minimum-access-mode table) and the irreducible/data-blocked/scope limitation taxonomy.
- [[property-based-testing]] ‚Äî P0 methodology (FsCheck): hundreds of generated inputs checked against expressible invariants (R/S/I/M/P/RT/D); 258/258.
- [[metamorphic-testing]] ‚Äî P0 methodology: metamorphic relations across runs (SUB/MON/INV/SYM/COMP/SHIFT) that solve the oracle problem; 258/258, ~200+ relations.
- [[fuzzing]] ‚Äî P2 methodology: random/malformed/boundary input for clean-failure; parsers the hot target; zero‚Üí258/258.
- [[snapshot-testing]] ‚Äî P1 methodology (Verify): golden-master `.verified.txt` regression capture; the least-complete methodology at 37/255.
- [[algebraic-testing]] ‚Äî P1 methodology: explicit algebraic laws (identity/associativity/involution/round-trip‚Ä¶); 89 applicable + 169 not-applicable.
- [[architecture-testing]] ‚Äî P2 methodology (ArchUnitNET): 22 IL-level module rules enforcing the [[layered-architecture]] Dependency Rule; scales by module not algorithm.
- [[differential-testing]] ‚Äî P2 methodology: two independent implementations cross-checked (ALT/BRUTE/REF/DUAL); 107/255.
- [[combinatorial-testing]] ‚Äî P3 methodology: minimal pairwise parameter-interaction coverage; 193/255 + 65 not-applicable.
- [[characterization-testing]] ‚Äî P3 methodology: golden-master pinning of behaviour before refactors (invariance, not correctness); on-demand.
- [[build-quality-gate]] ‚Äî the build-time static-analysis gate: SonarAnalyzer ratcheted to blocking under `TreatWarningsAsErrors`, fix-or-silence, review-not-blind-fix.
- [[test-unit-registry]] ‚Äî the area-prefixed Test Unit ID scheme and per-unit record behind the validation effort.
- [[definition-of-done]] ‚Äî the six-criterion acceptance bar (TestSpec, tests, ‚â•80% coverage, edge cases, CI, evidence) each unit must clear.
- [[algorithm-validation-evidence]] ‚Äî the templated per-unit `docs/Evidence/` artifact pattern (sources, worked-example dataset, deviations) behind the "Evidence documented" DoD criterion.
- [[global-alignment-needleman-wunsch]] ‚Äî the canonical DP global-alignment algorithm (`GlobalAlign`): linear-gap recurrence, O(nm), traceback, affine-as-extension.
- [[multiple-sequence-alignment]] ‚Äî aligning 3+ sequences (NP-complete): Seqeron's star (`MultipleAlign`), iterative-refinement (MUSCLE), and consistency (T-Coffee) aligners; sum-of-pairs + consensus.
- [[local-alignment-smith-waterman]] ‚Äî the canonical DP local-alignment algorithm (`LocalAlign`): zero-floor linear-gap recurrence, 0/0 border, optimum from the max cell, traceback-to-zero ‚Üí best local subsequences; linear-gap only (affine/W‚Çñ not implemented).
- [[semi-global-alignment-fitting]] ‚Äî ends-free "glocal" alignment: fitting/query-in-reference variant (Rosalind SIMS); NW recurrence with free reference end gaps, traceback from max of last row.
- [[alignment-statistics]] ‚Äî post-alignment metrics: percent identity/similarity/gaps (EMBOSS/BLAST convention, denominator includes gaps, positive-score ‚áí similar) and srspair three-line markup.
- [[coding-potential-hexamer-score]] ‚Äî CPAT hexamer usage-bias coding-potential score: mean of ln(coding/noncoding) over in-frame hexamers (wordSize 6/step 3), sign convention, ¬±1 pseudo-scores; Fickett TESTCODE as not-implemented alternative.
- [[prokaryotic-gene-prediction-rbs]] ‚Äî annotation-layer prokaryotic ORF-based gene prediction + Shine-Dalgarno RBS detection (ANNOT-GENE-001, `GenomeAnnotator.PredictGenes` / `FindRibosomeBindingSitesBothStrands` / `ScanStrandForShineDalgarno`): both-strand start‚Üístop CDS finding with `protein_length` excluding the stop, and SD consensus `AGGAGG` (+ substrings) matched upstream of a start at an aligned spacing ‚àà [minDistance,maxDistance] (score = motifLen/6). Core correctness = the reverse-strand SD mapping `forwardPosition = len ‚àí hit.position ‚àí motifLen` (scan the reverse complement, since the SD is an mRNA feature); anti-SD 3' 16S tail `YACCUCCUUA`, ~8 nt location, 5 nt literature optimum (Chen 1994). `alternative_to` the Analysis-layer six-frame [[open-reading-frame-detection]] (not contract-equivalent); the strand/spacing-aware counterpart to the bare `AGGAGG` row in [[regulatory-element-detection]]. Validation report [[annot-gene-001-report]].
- [[relative-synonymous-codon-usage]] ‚Äî RSCU (Sharp & Li 1986) codon-usage-bias measure: n_i¬∑x/Œ£x normalization, 1.0=no bias, bounded [0,n_i], Œ£-over-family=n_i invariant; pooled counts, sense codons only; base anchor of the codon-usage family (vs CAI's max-normalization).
- [[codon-adaptation-index]] ‚Äî CAI (Sharp & Li 1987) whole-gene codon-bias / expression-proxy score in [0,1]: geometric mean of relative adaptiveness w=f/max_synonym_f, low-value-sensitive, stop excluded; dual include/exclude-Met/Trp mode (exclude can give L=0‚Üí0); E. coli oracles; Seqeron deviation = 1e-6 zero-freq clamp (vs Sharp & Li's 0.5 reference-table pseudocount); one level above RSCU.
- [[rare-codon-analysis]] ‚Äî codon-usage family's *localization/diagnostic* unit (`FindRareCodons` + cluster addendum): a codon is rare when its per-family frequency < threshold (default 0.15), reports position/AA/frequency (E. coli AGA 0.04/AGG 0.02/CGA 0.06/CUA 0.04); addendum adds two published cluster methods ‚Äî Clarke & Clark 2008 %MinMax (18-codon window, signed %Min/%Max ‚àà[‚àí100,+100], rare clusters = negative peaks) and Chartier 2012 Sherlocc (7-codon window, ‚â•4 of 7 freq‚â§threshold "slow" positions = a rare-codon cluster); single-codon-AA contributes 0 to %MinMax (no NaN), overlapping windows merged; feeds [[codon-optimization]]'s AvoidRareCodons; oracles ‚àí86.36/+100/+36.47% and 7√óAGA‚Üí1 cluster; deviations None.
- [[codon-usage-comparison]] ‚Äî codon-usage family's *raw* end (`CalculateCodonUsage` + `CompareCodonUsage`): unnormalized codon-count table (non-overlapping triplets, T‚ÜíU, drop partial codon, Dictionary<codon,int>, Œ£counts=total invariant) + Total Variation Distance similarity `1‚àíŒ£|f‚ÇÅ‚àíf‚ÇÇ|/2 ‚àà [0,1]` between two codon-frequency distributions; proven identity 1.0 / symmetry / range [0,1] / disjoint‚Üí0 / partial-overlap-exact properties; empty‚Üí0, TVD-not-cosine deliberate metric choice; Kazusa-verified organism tables; shares RSCU's counting primitive, the distribution-comparison op none of the bias measures provide.
- [[codon-optimization]] ‚Äî codon-usage family's CDS-*rewriting* operation (`OptimizeSequence`): synonymous substitution to improve host expression; five strategies (MaximizeCAI / BalancedOptimization 40-60% GC / HarmonizeExpression=Mignon 2018 / AvoidRareCodons / MinimizeSecondary‚ÜíReduceSecondaryStructure); invariants protein-preservation + Met/AUG & Trp/UGG fixed + stop preserved + CAI‚àà(0,1]; RNA notation, T‚ÜíU, trim-to-codon, 1e-6 CAI clamp; E. coli/yeast/human preferred-codon fixtures; actuator to RSCU/CAI/ENC's measurement.
- [[effective-number-of-codons]] ‚Äî ENC/Nc (Wright 1990) reference-free whole-gene codon-bias measure in [20,61]: reciprocal of codon homozygosity FÃÇ=(n¬∑Œ£p¬≤‚àí1)/(n‚àí1) aggregated by degeneracy class (Nc=2+9/FÃÇ‚ÇÇ+1/FÃÇ‚ÇÉ+5/FÃÇ‚ÇÑ+3/FÃÇ‚ÇÜ); 20=max bias / 61=uniform, unbiased‚Üí61, no-bias-sim‚Üí40.5; Ile absent‚Üí(FÃÇ‚ÇÇ+FÃÇ‚ÇÑ)/2 fallback, overshoot re-adjusts to 61; reference-free counterpart of CAI; one assumption = non-source-prescribed lower clamp at 20.
- [[genetic-code-translation]] ‚Äî the codon-family's foundational table: `GeneticCode` codon‚Üíamino-acid map (64 codons ‚Üí 20 AA + 3 stops), 4 of NCBI's 33 tables (Standard/1, Vertebrate-Mito/2, Yeast-Mito/3, Bacterial-Plastid/11) as static singletons; `Translate`/`IsStartCodon`/`IsStopCodon`/`GetCodonsForAminoAcid`; DNA‚ÜîRNA T‚ÜíU + case-insensitive + stop‚Üí`*` + len‚âÝ3‚ÜíArgumentException; Met/AUG & Trp/UGG single-codon fixed points (the w‚â°1 fact behind CAI/optimization); IUPAC ambiguity codon‚Üí`'X'` (a flagged divergence from the Evidence doc's promised exception). The table [[open-reading-frame-detection|ORF detection]] and [[codon-optimization]] read. Also covers the **whole-sequence `Translator` layer** (TRANS-PROT-001 + TRANS-SIXFRAME-001): framed / six-frame translation + genetic-code-parameterized START‚ÜíSTOP ORF finding, verified against the UniProt-P01308 insulin B-chain oracle; six-frame reverse-frame numbering follows the **Biopython independent-offset** convention (‚àík = RC offset k‚àí1), the documented alternative to EMBOSS phase-locked.
- [[repetitive-element-detection]] ‚Äî repeats/tandem family anchor: tandem (head-to-tail, ‚â•2 copies, primitive unit), inverted (W¬∑G¬∑WÃÑ·¥ø / zero-gap palindrome, IUPACpal), and RepeatMasker-class assignment; ClassifyRepeat = exact-substring containment, not Smith-Waterman homology.
- [[consensus-sequence]] ‚Äî assembly CONSENSUS family anchor: column-wise majority/threshold consensus (Biopython dumb_consensus rule) ‚Äî gaps skipped, emit iff unique max and freq ‚â• threshold else ambiguous, tie‚Üíambiguous, all-gap‚ÜíN no div-by-zero; N/0.5 parameterized defaults; shared with MSA consensus step.
- [[consensus-from-alignment]] ‚Äî Motif-Analysis consensus-from-a-multiple-alignment (MOTIF-CONS-001, `MotifFinder.CreateConsensusFromAlignment`): pure most-frequent (plurality) column consensus over equal-length aligned strings, deterministic alphabetical tie-break (A<C<G<T), no threshold (always emits); Rosalind CONS `ATGCAACT` oracle; `alternative_to` the threshold/tie‚Üíambiguous assembly [[consensus-sequence]], motif-family sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] ‚Äî MotifFinder degenerate-consensus unit (MOTIF-GENERATE-001, `MotifFinder.GenerateConsensus`): collapses equal-length aligned columns into an IUPAC-ambiguity-coded string ‚Äî per column keep every base with `count > 0.25¬∑n` (strict `>`), emit the NC-IUB 1984 symbol for that base set (R/Y/S/W/K/M, B/D/H/V, N), no-pass fallback ‚Üí most-frequent (alphabetical tie); DECIPHER threshold-consensus family + NC-IUB/UCSC/Wikipedia bijective set‚Üísymbol table; `A,A,G,G,C`‚ÜíR / strict-`>` boundary / four-way‚ÜíA-fallback oracles; `alternative_to` the plurality [[consensus-from-alignment]], degenerate sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]].
- [[regulatory-element-detection]] ‚Äî Motif-Discovery regulatory-element unit (MOTIF-REGULATORY-001, `KnownMotifs` catalog scan): matches a **fixed, cited catalog of 12 canonical regulatory consensus elements** (TATA/‚àí10/‚àí35/CAAT/GC promoter boxes, Kozak + Shine-Dalgarno translation signals, poly(A), and E-box/AP-1/NF-Œ∫B/CREB TF sites) against a DNA sequence, reporting each occurrence's Name/Pattern/Sequence at its 0-based start; mixes exact and one IUPAC-degenerate (E-box `CANNTG`) match; anchors the AP-1 corrected-consensus regression (`TGAGTCA`‚Üí`TGACTCA`, `AATGAGTCAGG`‚Üí0 hits); two source-backed representative-site assumptions (NF-Œ∫B `GGGACTTTCC`, Kozak `GCCGCCACCATGG`); the curated-biological-catalog specialization of the generic exact [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the generation-direction [[iupac-degenerate-consensus]] and de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; the scored ‚àí10/‚àí35 alternative is [[promoter-detection]].
- [[promoter-detection]] ‚Äî Annotation-layer scored ‚àí10/‚àí35 promoter motif detector (ANNOT-PROM-001, `GenomeAnnotator.FindPromoterMotifs`): scans DNA for the prokaryotic ‚àí35 box `TTGACA` and ‚àí10/Pribnow box `TATAAT` plus derived prefix-5/suffix-5/prefix-4 variants, scoring each hit `Œ£ matched-position p / Œ£ all-6 consensus p ‚àà [0,1]` from the E. coli position-specific frequencies (‚àí35 sum 373, ‚àí10 sum 412); a full box scores 1.0, partial variants 0.665‚Äì0.855; `position` is a **0-based string index** (not the TSS-relative negative coordinate), `type` ‚àà {`-35 box`,`-10 box`}, ‚àí35/‚àí10 scanned independently (no pairing). Declared scope limits: **17 bp spacing not enforced**, **exact-substring not PWM/HMM/mismatch-tolerant** ‚Äî motif annotation, not full promoter prediction; no null guard. The `alternative_to` the exact-hexamer catalog scan [[regulatory-element-detection]] (same two boxes, no scoring). Validation report [[annot-prom-001-report]].
- [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] ‚Äî Motif-Discovery de-novo unit (MOTIF-DISCOVER-001, `MotifFinder.DiscoverMotifs`): finds **unknown** over-represented motifs by enumerating every length-`k` k-mer, counting overlapping occurrences, and ranking by observed/expected enrichment `Count/((N‚àík+1)/4^k)` under a zero-order i.i.d. uniform background (Compeau & Pevzner); deterministic exact single-pass, 0-based positions; `ATGC` in `ATGCATGCATGC` k=4 ‚Üí 768/9‚âà85.333, `AAA` in `AAAAAAAAAA` k=3 ‚Üí 64.0 oracles; `k>N`‚Üíempty, minCount presentation-only, zero-order-only + no-p-value simplifications; the de-novo inverse of the exact [[known-motif-search]] and distinct from the [[consensus-from-alignment]] plurality consensus.
- [[shared-motifs]] ‚Äî Motif-Discovery cross-sequence unit (MOTIF-SHARED-001, `FindSharedMotifs`): the van Helden / RSAT oligo-analysis **"matching sequences"** quorum ‚Äî enumerate every fixed-`k` exact word across a *set* of sequences and report each word present in ‚â• `minSequences` of them (each carrying its `SequenceIndices` set + `Prevalence`=matching/total); a within-sequence repeat counts **1** (presence/absence, not multiplicity); exact-word only (no degenerate/substitution); the cross-sequence sibling of the single-sequence O/E [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]] and `alternative_to` the fixed-k-quorum-vs-single-longest LCSM framing of [[longest-common-substring]] (returns all qualifying words, not one longest present in all).
- [[approximate-pattern-matching-mismatches]] ‚Äî pattern-matching PAT-APPROX family anchor (PAT-APPROX-003): Hamming-distance **approximate matching** ‚Äî a `k`-mer appears with ‚â§`d` mismatches when `HammingDistance(P,P')‚â§d` (BA1H); `Count_d`/`FindApproximateOccurrences` scan windows, `FindFrequentKmersWithMismatches` (BA1I) ranks `k`-mers by their **d-neighborhood** (Hamming-ball) tally so the winner need not occur exactly, `Neighbors` (BA1N) enumerates the ball (includes identity), `FindBestMatch` returns the leftmost min-Hamming window; oracles {GATG,ATGC,ATGT} count 5, {6,7,26,27,78}, Count_1=4, ACG/1‚Üí10; d=0 degenerates to exact so it is the mismatch-tolerant `alternative_to` [[k-mer-positions]] and the fuzzy sibling of the exact [[known-motif-search]] / de-novo [[overrepresented-kmer-discovery]]; substitution-only (no indels ‚Äî that is the alignment family), deviations none.
- [[coverage-depth-calculation]] ‚Äî assembly COVER family anchor: per-base sequencing depth over a reference (count of placed reads spanning each position, exact); average depth = Œ£depth/G = Lander-Waterman C=LN/G, breadth = covered/G = 1‚àíe^‚àíc; boundary-clip + empty-input rules; ACGTTGCAAT‚Üí1.5/1.0 oracle; Poisson (e^‚àíc gap) as a property check only; read placement (minOverlap best-match) out of scope.
- [[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]] ‚Äî assembly DBG family anchor: k-mer graph (distinct (k-1)-mers = nodes, each k-mer = one prefix‚Üísuffix edge, directed multigraph) + Eulerian-walk reconstruction (balanced/semi-balanced, Euler theorems 8.1/8.2, O(|E|) Hierholzer); spelling = path[0]+last char of each node; unique-walk oracles only (AAABBBA, a_long‚Ä¶, to_every‚Ä¶ k=4, ATGGCGTGCA); repeat/gap/error ‚Üí non-Eulerian; walk-selection unspecified so exact asserts on unique-walk inputs; OLC is the alternative formulation.
- [[overlap-layout-consensus-assembly]] ‚Äî assembly OLC family anchor: the three-stage Overlap-Layout-Consensus paradigm (`FindAllOverlaps` + `AssembleOLC`) ‚Äî overlap graph (read=node, edge on longest suffix-of-A/prefix-of-B ‚â• threshold), Layout = Hamiltonian path (NP-complete) + transitive reduction + non-branching contigs, Consensus = majority vote; GTACGTACGAT 12-edge / 5-overlap-tiling oracles; suffix-tree O(N+a) vs all-pairs O(N¬≤); NP-complete/repeat-split/greedy-suboptimal failure modes; identity-1.0 + empty-input assumptions; Hamiltonian/overlap-graph alternative to DBG's Eulerian/k-mer formulation.
- [[contig-merge-overlap-collapse]] ‚Äî assembly MERGE family anchor: suffix‚Äìprefix overlap collapse primitive (`MergeContigs`) behind greedy SCS and OLC layout; overlap = length-l suffix of X = prefix of Y, longest match reported, collapse keeps one copy so |merge|=|c1|+|c2|‚àíl; overlap 0 / out-of-range ‚Üí plain concatenation; BAA+AAB‚ÜíBAAB, chain‚ÜíAAABBBA oracles; caller-trusts-length + out-of-range‚Üíconcat API-contract assumptions; overlap-based sibling of DBG's k-mer/Eulerian formulation.
- [[scaffolding]] ‚Äî assembly SCAFFOLD family anchor: joining ordered contigs into a scaffold, adjacent contigs separated by `N`-runs of length = the (upstream) inter-contig distance estimate (ABySS 2.0 rule); positive gap `g` ‚Üí `g`√ó`N`, scaffold length = Œ£|contig|+Œ£gap; non-positive (zero/negative) estimate ‚Üí AGP unknown-size default 100 N (negative = overlap, unresolved here); each contig in ‚â§1 scaffold, unlinked ‚Üí singleton; parameterized fill char; ACGTNNNTTGGNNCCAA / AAAA+100N+TTTT oracles; downstream of DBG/OLC/merge, hands off to contig-merge on the negative-gap overlap case; 100-constant source-backed (INSDC), only the fall-back-not-resolve decision is assumed.
- [[assembly-statistics]] ‚Äî assembly STATS family anchor: contiguity/QC summary metrics over contig lengths (read-only, downstream of DBG/OLC/merge/scaffold) ‚Äî Nx = shortest length covering ‚â•x% (largest-first, inclusive ‚â•; N50/N90), Lx = the matching contig count, N90 ‚â§ N50 / L90 ‚â• L50, auN = Œ£L·µ¢¬≤/Œ£L‚±º (area under Nx curve, more stable than N50); + totals/largest/smallest/GC and 0-based inclusive N-run gaps; Miller 2010 + Wikipedia + QUAST + Heng Li 2020; Assembly A N50 70/L50 2, auN 73.333 oracles; empty‚Üízeros (not None) + upper-median-not-source-derived assumptions.
- [[quality-trimming-running-sum]] ‚Äî assembly TRIM family anchor: BWA/cutadapt running-sum quality trimming ‚Äî subtract cutoff from each Phred quality, take partial sums to the 3' end, cut at the minimum (= BWA argmax of accumulated threshold‚àíq, with `s<0` early break + `BWA_MIN_RDLEN=35` floor); Phred+33 decode (Cock 2010); `KI;<)(,%#$`@thr 10‚Üífirst 4 bases oracle; threshold<1 disables / all-high unchanged / all-low dropped / good-base-among-bad refinement; both-end pass + downstream minLength filter as assumptions; read-QC preprocessing upstream of correction/DBG/OLC.
- [[kmer-spectrum-error-correction]] ‚Äî assembly CORRECT family anchor: two-sided k-mer-spectrum read error correction (Musket/Quake) ‚Äî trusted (multiplicity > cut-off) vs untrusted k-mers, base trusted if covered by any trusted k-mer, unique alternative making all covering k-mers trusted, ambiguity/no-set‚Üíunchanged; substitution-only (count+length preserved); kmerSize=15/minKmerFrequency=2 non-behavioral defaults.
- [[centromere-analysis]] ‚Äî chromosome centromere/alpha-satellite family anchor (second Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeCentromere` + 4 additive detectors ‚Äî Levan 1964 q/p arm-ratio classes (Metacentric ‚â§1.7 / Submetacentric ‚â§3.0 / Subtelocentric <7.0 / Acrocentric ‚â•7.0 / Telocentric p=0); alpha-satellite-specific `DetectAlphaSatellite`/`FindCenpBBoxes` (171-bp tandem period ¬±5, AT>0.5, 17-bp CENP-B box `YTTCGTTGGAARCGGGA`, no embedded monomer); `DetectHigherOrderRepeat` (HOR period = smallest k with monomers k apart ‚â•95% identical across ‚â•90%, intra-HOR 50‚Äì70% vs inter-HOR 97‚Äì100%); `AssignSuprachromosomalFamily` (bundled CC0 Dfam ALR/ALRa=A/ALRb=B, SF3 pentameric/SF4 monomeric/{SF1,SF2} dimeric/SF5 irregular); base AlphaSatelliteContent is density-heuristic-not-specific + SF1/SF2-unresolved (non-redistributable consensus library) limitations.
- [[base-composition]] ‚Äî foundational sequence-composition tally (SEQ-COMPOSITION-001): exact **nucleotide** partition of Length into A/T/G/C/U/`CountN`/`CountOther` (seven counts sum to Length), **GC content** `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C+U)` ‚àà [0,1] (Biopython `gc_fraction`, empty ‚áí 0), and **amino-acid** residue counts over the 20 IUPAC letters; case-insensitive, non-canonical/degenerate codes tracked separately (not folded into A/T/G/C/U) ‚Äî the documented assumption vs Biopython (which counts S toward GC / W toward denominator), agreeing exactly over {A,T,G,C,U}; the magnitude/fraction view whose *asymmetry* counterpart is the sibling [[nucleotide-composition-skew]], base layer under [[cpg-island-detection]] dinucleotide O/E, [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]] window entropy, and the GC constraints in [[taqman-probe-design-rules]]/[[codon-optimization]]. Records [[seq-composition-001-evidence]].
- [[nucleotide-composition-skew]] ‚Äî strand compositional-skew family (Lobry 1996): **AT skew** `(A‚àíT)/(A+T)` + **GC skew** `(G‚àíC)/(G+C)`, both bounded [‚àí1,+1] (AT skew `‚àí1‚áîA=0`/`+1‚áîT=0`); zero-denominator ‚áí **0.0** (Biopython `GC_skew` convention), case-insensitive counting, ambiguous/non-canonical bases ignored; biological meaning = replication-strand asymmetry, cumulative-skew sign flip locates the origin/terminus (Charneski 2011: Firmicute AT skew from selection, not mutation); AT-skew member validated by [[seq-atskew-001-evidence]] (SEQ-ATSKEW-001), GC-skew member (`gc-skew`) not yet ingested; single-base cousin of the dinucleotide CpG O/E in [[cpg-island-detection]] and the GC-skew unit flagged in [[centromere-analysis]].
- [[dinucleotide-relative-abundance]] ‚Äî dinucleotide composition & the **Karlin genomic signature** (SEQ-DINUC-001): the 2-mer generalization of [[base-composition]] and the general case of the CpG O/E in [[cpg-island-detection]]. Two outputs over the `N‚àí1` adjacent base-steps ‚Äî **dinucleotide frequency** `f_XY = count/(N‚àí1)` and the **relative-abundance odds ratio** `œÅ_XY = f_XY/(f_X¬∑f_Y)` (`CalculateDinucleotideRatios`; `œÅ=1` no-bias independence baseline, Karlin & Burge over/under thresholds `œÅ‚â•1.23`/`œÅ‚â§0.78` documentation-only); CpG O/E is the `CG`-specialized case, differing only by the `N` vs `N‚àí1` normalization (`N/(N‚àí1)‚Üí1` long sequences, a documented modeling choice). Exact-rational oracles for `ATGCGCGT` (GC/CG œÅ=64/21, AT œÅ=32/7, TG/GT œÅ=32/21); div-by-zero guard ‚Üí ratio 0 when a constituent base is absent, `U` counted as a fifth base for RNA, case-insensitive. Also validates the codon-frequency metric owned by [[codon-usage-comparison]]/[[seq-codon-freq-001-evidence]]. Records [[seq-dinuc-001-evidence]].
- [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] ‚Äî composite **GC-analysis** unit's distinct layer (SEQ-GC-ANALYSIS-001, `GcAnalysisResult`): bundles the whole-sequence scalars OverallGcContent `(G+C)/(A+T+G+C)√ó100` (percentage √ó100, [[base-composition]] carries the `[0,1]` fraction), OverallGcSkew `(G‚àíC)/(G+C)`, OverallAtSkew `(A‚àíT)/(A+T)` ([[nucleotide-composition-skew]]) with a **sliding-window** GC%/GC-skew profile (only fully-contained windows; shorter-than-window ‚áí empty lists) and the **population variance** `œÉ¬≤=Œ£(x·µ¢‚àíŒº)¬≤/N` (√∑N, not √∑N‚àí1) of each windowed series ‚Äî a compositional-heterogeneity/isochore-style variability signal, cumulative GC-skew locating the replication origin/terminus (Grigoriev 1998), same window-GC signal the [[centromere-analysis]] heuristic uses, composition sibling of the entropy/complexity [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]]. Sources GC-content Brock/Wikipedia + GC skew Lobry 1996/Biopython `GC_skew` + Cuemath population variance (6.8 anchor); `GGGCCAT`‚Üí71.428‚Ä¶/0.2/0.0, `GGCC` w2s2‚Üí`GcSkewVariance` 1.0/`GcContentVariance` 0.0; two labelling/estimator assumptions (√ó100 vs fraction; √∑N population variance), no contradictions. Records [[seq-gc-analysis-001-evidence]].
- [[replication-origin-cumulative-skew]] ‚Äî the skew family's *localisation* algorithm (SEQ-REPLICATION-001): predicts the **replication origin from the cumulative GC-skew minimum** and the **terminus from its maximum** (Grigoriev 1998; Rosalind BA1F Minimum Skew Problem). Distinct from the scalar/windowed skew ‚Äî uses an **integer** cumulative running sum (G:+1, C:‚àí1, A/T:0, `Skew_0=0`, `|Genome|+1` prefix values over `i‚àà[0,n]`), then argmin=`PredictedOrigin` / argmax=`PredictedTerminus`, first-occurrence tie-break (BA1F sample ‚Üí 53 of {53,97}); the leading strand is G-rich so skew flips sign at origin/terminus (Lobry 1996), making the integral a valley at ori and peak at ter. `IsSignificant` redefined threshold-free as `max>min` (invented `amplitude>count√ó0.01` constant removed); flat diagram (no/balanced G/C) ‚áí origin=terminus=0/false. Diagram oracles `CCGGGG`/`GGGCCC`/`AATT`; consumes the same G/C tally as [[base-composition]]/[[nucleotide-composition-skew]], localisation counterpart of the [[windowed-gc-profile-and-variance]] variability view. Records [[seq-replication-001-evidence]].
- [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] ‚Äî protein-property member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-HYDRO-001): the **Kyte-Doolittle (1982) GRAVY index** `Œ£(kd value)/length` (Expasy/Biopython `gravy()`; positive ‚áí hydrophobic, negative ‚áí hydrophilic) + the **unweighted sliding-window hydropathy profile** (exactly `N‚àíW+1` window means, Biopython `protein_scale(edge=1.0)`); the 20-residue kd table I 4.5‚Ä¶R ‚àí4.5 (identical to [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]]'s `HydropathyScale`), window-size guidance W=9 surface / W=19 transmembrane peaks > 1.6; oracles `A`‚Üí1.8 / `FLIV`‚Üí3.825 / `RKDE`‚Üí‚àí3.85, window-3 `FLIV`‚Üí[3.7, 4.1666666667], `W>N`‚Üíempty, case-insensitive; one deviation (unknown residues **skipped** not Biopython `KeyError`), no source contradictions. The whole-sequence-scalar + raw-profile amino-acid analogue of the nucleotide [[base-composition]]; the segment-calling [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] thresholds this same profile, and it shares the kd scale with [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]]'s `CalculateHydropathy`. Records [[seq-hydro-001-evidence]].
- [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] ‚Äî full-tuple thermodynamics member of the SEQ-\* family (SEQ-THERMO-001): the **ŒîH¬∞/ŒîS¬∞/ŒîG¬∞‚ÇÉ‚Çá/Tm** of a Watson-Crick DNA duplex from the **nearest-neighbor model** ‚Äî a port of Biopython `Tm_NN` over the **DNA_NN3 / Allawi & SantaLucia 1997** table (10 WC dinucleotide ŒîH¬∞/ŒîS¬∞ stacks) plus **two-terminus initiation** (`init_A/T` 2.3/4.1 and `init_G/C` 0.1/‚àí2.8 counted off the two terminal bases). Tm `= (1000¬∑ŒîH¬∞)/(ŒîS¬∞ + R¬∑ln k) ‚àí 273.15`, `R=1.987`, `k=(dnac1‚àídnac2/2)¬∑1e‚àí9` (default 25 nM each ‚áí k=C_T/4, the F=4 non-self-complementary factor); SantaLucia-1998 salt correction `ŒîS¬∞ += 0.368¬∑(len‚àí1)¬∑ln[Na‚Å∫]` ‚áí Tm monotone in salt; ŒîG¬∞‚ÇÉ‚Çá `= ŒîH¬∞ ‚àí 310.15¬∑ŒîS¬∞/1000`. Oracles `CGTTCCAAAGATGTGGGCATGAGCTTAC` (25 nM, 50 mM Na) ‚Üí **Tm 60.32 ¬∞C**, `GCGC` ‚Üí ŒîH ‚àí30.0/ŒîS ‚àí84.91/ŒîG ‚àí3.67/Tm ‚àí18.6, `ATCG` (one A/T + one G/C end) ‚Üí ŒîH ‚àí23.6/ŒîS ‚àí71.81; **length<2 ‚áí `(0,0,0,0)`**, case-insensitive, non-self-complementary (F=4) only. Distinct from the legacy Wallace/Marmur scalar Tm ([[melting-temperature]], SEQ-TM-001) and from the 2004-unified PCR-primer engine [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (different init bookkeeping; returns the full tuple). Records [[seq-thermo-001-evidence]]; zero correctness-affecting assumptions, no source contradictions.
- [[melting-temperature]] ‚Äî the **legacy %GC scalar** melting-temperature member of the SEQ-\* family and the **third distinct Tm surface** (SEQ-TM-001, `CalculateMeltingTemperature`): a single ¬∞C number **length-dispatched** at `ThermoConstants.WallaceMaxLength = 14` between the **Wallace rule** `Tm = 4¬∑(G+C)+2¬∑(A+T)` for short oligos (Thein & Wallace 1986) and the **Marmur-Doty GC formula** `Tm = 64.9 + 41¬∑(GC‚àí16.4)/N` (‚â° `64.9 + 0.41¬∑%GC ‚àí 672.4/N`) for len‚â•14 (Marmur & Doty 1962). A **rule of thumb carrying no ŒîH¬∞/ŒîS¬∞/ŒîG¬∞**, no concentration term, no salt correction ‚Äî the canonical home of the Wallace/Marmur formulas (previously only sketched as the legacy default on [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]) and the fast approximation that [[seq-summary-001-evidence|SummarizeNucleotideSequence]]'s `MeltingTemperature` field and the primer engine's *default* per-oligo Tm both use. Oracles `ACGTTGCAATGCCGTA`‚Üí48.0 / `ATGCATGC`‚Üí24.0 (Wallace), `GCGCGCGCGCATATATATAT`‚Üí51.78 / 16-mer `ATGCATGCATGCATGC`‚Üí43.375 (Marmur-Doty); empty/null‚Üí0, case-insensitive; one ASSUMPTION (14-nt dispatch boundary), formula-variant note (repo 64.9/‚àí672.4 vs Biopython `Tm_GC` valueset-1 69.3/‚àí650), no source contradictions. The %GC rule-of-thumb `alternative_to` the two SantaLucia NN engines [[dna-duplex-nearest-neighbor-thermodynamics]] (SEQ-THERMO-001, whose `CalculateThermodynamics` is the NN facet of the same consolidated SEQ-TM-001 registry entry) and [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]]. Records [[seq-tm-001-evidence]].
- [[molecular-weight]] ‚Äî mass member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-MW-001): the average-isotopic **molecular mass in Daltons** of a **protein, DNA or RNA** sequence via one shared polymerization formula `weight = Œ£ (monomer mass) ‚àí (len‚àí1)¬∑water` (Biopython `Bio.SeqUtils.molecular_weight`; one water removed per bond ‚Äî peptide for protein, phosphodiester for nucleic acid; for protein algebraically = the Expasy `Œ£ residue masses + water`), with average free-amino-acid (protein G 75.0666‚Ä¶W 204.2252) and 5'-monophosphate nucleotide (DNA A 331.2218‚Ä¶; RNA A 347.2212‚Ä¶) mass tables and `water = 18.0153`; single monomer ‚áí free-monomer mass, circular ‚áí ‚àíone more water, double-strand adds the complement (error for protein); oracles `AGC`‚Üíprotein 249.29 / DNA 949.61 / RNA 997.61, `G`‚Üí75.0666, `A`‚ÜíDNA 331.2218 / RNA 347.2212, empty/null‚Üí0; case-insensitive, one deviation (unknown symbols **skipped** not Biopython-rejected), no source contradictions. The mass-weighted view of the [[base-composition]] tally and a whole-sequence-scalar sibling of the [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] GRAVY scalar (pI/charge is the separate [[isoelectric-point]] unit). Records [[seq-mw-001-evidence]].
- [[isoelectric-point]] ‚Äî charge/pH member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-PI-001): the **pH at which a protein's net charge is zero**, found by **bisecting the Henderson‚ÄìHasselbalch net-charge function over [0,14]** to ¬±0.01. Net charge `Œ£_basic +1/(1+10^(pH‚àípKa)) + Œ£_acidic ‚àí1/(1+10^(pKa‚àípH))` (Moore 1985, Peptides `charge_pI.cpp`; monotone-decreasing ‚áí unique root); basic/positive = {R,K,H,N-term}, acidic/negative = {D,E,C,Y,C-term}, both termini once. **EMBOSS `Epk.dat` pKa scale** (N-term 8.6/C-term 3.6/C 8.5/D 3.9/E 4.1/H 6.5/K 10.8/R 12.5/Y 10.1) ‚Äî the single-pKa-per-residue model, *not* position-dependent Bjellqvist. **Composition-only / order-independent** ("no electrostatic interactions" ‚Äî a permutation gives identical pI), the trait it shares with [[base-composition]]; the ExPASy Compute pI/Mw partner of [[molecular-weight]] and protein-property sibling of [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]]. Oracles `A`/`AG`‚Üí6.10, `D`‚Üí3.75, `K`‚Üí9.70, `DDDD`‚Üí3.23, `KKKK`‚Üí11.27, `FLPVLAGLTPSIVPKLVCLLTKKC`‚Üí9.67 (net charge 3.037398/2.914112/0.7184524 @ pH 5/7/9), `ACDEFGHIKLMNPQRSTVWY`‚Üí7.36 (EMBOSS ‚âÝ Bjellqvist 6.78454); pI‚àà[0,14] invariant, two assumptions (empty/null‚Üí7.0 guard; scale=EMBOSS parameter choice), small/highly-basic-protein accuracy caveat, no source contradictions. Records [[seq-pi-001-evidence]].
- [[protein-secondary-structure-chou-fasman]] ‚Äî conformational-propensity member of the SEQ-\* sequence-statistics family (SEQ-SECSTRUCT-001): the **Chou-Fasman (1978) PŒ±/PŒ≤/Pt sliding-window mean-propensity profile** ‚Äî for a window `W`, the arithmetic mean of each of the Œ±-helix/Œ≤-sheet/Œ≤-turn propensities (observed/expected; A 1.42/0.83/0.66 ‚Ä¶ V 1.06/1.70/0.50) over each window. The **generic profile, not** the classic 4-of-6-helix / 3-of-5-sheet nucleation-extension state machine ‚Üí default `W=7` is an API convenience not a CF constant; shares the exact SEQ-\* sliding-window mechanism with [[hydrophobicity-gravy-and-profile]] (`N‚àíW+1` unweighted window means, `W>N`‚Üíempty, unknown residues skip-and-excluded, case-insensitive). Oracles single-residue window = that residue's (PŒ±,PŒ≤,Pt) tuple, `AE`‚Üíhelix 1.465/sheet 0.60/turn 0.70, `AEV`‚Üíhelix 1.330, `AXE` W3 averages only A+E; one contested value resolved (**Lys PŒ± 1.14** two-source incl. reference impl vs CSB|SJU 1.16), three assumptions (window-7 default, skip-unknown, Lys 1.14), ~50‚Äì60% Q3 / 29-protein reliability caveat. A raw propensity profile that does **not** emit helix/sheet/turn segments ‚Äî distinct from the hydropathy segment-caller [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]], the disorder view [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] and the SEG scan [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]. Records [[seq-secstruct-001-evidence]].
- [[karyotype-analysis]] ‚Äî chromosome karyotyping/ploidy-detection family anchor (third Chromosome-analysis unit): `AnalyzeKaryotype` builds a karyotype from chromosome descriptors (split sex/autosome, group by base name, count copies, compare to expected ploidy, label nullisomy..pentasomy by absolute count; TotalChromosomes/TotalGenomeSize/MeanChromosomeLength invariants) and `DetectPloidy` estimates whole-genome ploidy from read depth (true-median ratio ‚Üí round(ratio√ó2) clamped [1,8], confidence 1‚àí|ratio√ó2‚àíploidy|√ó2, empty‚Üí(2,0)); Down/Turner + diploid/tetraploid/haploid oracles; DD4 nullisomy-unreachable-via-GroupBy, DD5 disomy-only-aneuploid-in-polyploid; deviations None. Descriptor-count sibling of depth-log-ratio [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] ‚Äî shared synteny anchor (fourth Chromosome-analysis unit; comparative-genomics COMPGEN-SYNTENY will reuse it): `FindSyntenyBlocks` builds syntenic blocks from ortholog pairs (group by chr pair, sort by ref position, collinear runs merged under maxGap, emit ‚â•minGenes; block carries strand '+'/'-', GeneCount, SequenceIdentity=NaN for coordinate-only input per MCScanX; I1‚ÄìI5) + `DetectRearrangements` classifies adjacent-block signals (diff target chr‚ÜíTranslocation, same chr diff strand‚ÜíInversion, gap asymmetry‚ÜíDeletion, overlapping source diff targets‚ÜíDuplication); forward/inverted-block + translocation(50000)/inversion(size 10000) oracles; empty/below-minGenes/maxGap-split/multi-pair edge cases; MCScanX/SyRI/MUMmer + Wikipedia; deviations None.
- [[telomere-analysis]] ‚Äî chromosome telomere family anchor (fifth Chromosome-analysis unit): telomere repeat detection + length estimation ‚Äî 3‚Ä≤ end forward TTAGGG / 5‚Ä≤ end reverse-complement CCCTAA (6-bp vertebrate unit, Meyne 1989), configurable 70%-per-window purity so imperfect repeats accepted (5/6 for 6-bp, 5/7 for Arabidopsis TTTAGGG; divergent TTAGGA‚Üí0.833), purity‚àà[0,1] tracked with length; length direct from run or qPCR T/S ratio (Cawthon 2002) EstimatedLength=referenceLength√ó(tsRatio/referenceRatio); IsCriticallyShort=(hasTelomere&&length<criticalLength)OR empty; criticalLength 3000 / minTelomereLength 500 / searchLength(truncates) / referenceLength 7000 configurable defaults not biological constants; Wikipedia/Meyne/Cawthon/Blackburn-Gall sources; deviations None. Sibling of [[aneuploidy-detection]].
- [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics common-interval / conserved-cluster unit: a conserved gene cluster = a gene-label SET contiguous in EVERY genome (order- and strand-free inside the window), the common-interval model (Uno & Yagiura 2000, Heber & Stoye 2001 k-permutation O(kn+z), Bui-Xuan/Habib/Paul 2013 unifying view, Didier et al. 2013 sequences-with-duplicates/paralogs); interval size ‚â•2 (singletons excluded), whole set (1..n) trivially common, meaningful only for K‚â•2; Seqeron does the strict O(n¬≤¬∑K) check with minClusterSize filter; strict gap-free model ‚Äî maxGap retained for API/MCP back-compat only and does NOT relax it, gene-teams gapped extension (Bergeron 2002) not implemented; golden vector Id‚Çá vs (7 2 1 3 6 4 5) ‚Üí {1,2}/{1,2,3}/{3,4,5,6}/{4,5}/{4,5,6}/{1..6} + trivial {1..7}, split-negative {2,3}, duplicates T/S ‚Üí {1,2,3,4}; order-free sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] and [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; deviations None.
- [[average-nucleotide-identity]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics ANI family anchor (first COMPGEN unit): the ANIb genome-similarity metric (Goris 2007) that operationalizes the prokaryotic species boundary (ANI‚âà95%‚Üî70% DDH) ‚Äî fragment query into 1020 nt pieces, best-match place each against the reference (`CalculateAni`), keep fragments >30% identity over ‚â•70% alignable (both recalculated over the query-fragment length), average the qualifying per-fragment identities; gapped Smith-Waterman placement recovers indels (`gapped:true`), reciprocal/symmetric ANI = mean of both directions (`CalculateReciprocalAni`, order-independent); null/empty‚Üí0, non-positive fragmentLength throws; engine decision = SequenceAligner.LocalAlign (full DP, BLAST DNA scoring) not NCBI-BLASTN, indel handling correct; sibling of [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]] in the COMPGEN family; deviations None.
- [[dot-plot-word-match]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics visual pairwise-comparison unit (`COMPGEN-DOTPLOT-001`): the word-match / k-tuple dot matrix (Gibbs & McIntyre 1970 ‚Üí EMBOSS `dottup`) ‚Äî dot at (x,y) iff the length-`wordSize` word at x in seq1 exactly matches the word at y in seq2 (case-insensitive, x=seq1/y=seq2, all overlapping occurrences via suffix tree), diagonals = similarity / main diagonal = self-comparison / repeats = extra diagonals / indels break the diagonal; `wordSize` (EMBOSS default 10) noise-vs-sensitivity trade-off (longer=less noise/less sensitive), `stepSize` x-subsampling; exact-match `dottup` not scored `dotmatcher`; AGCGT/AT k=1‚Üí{(0,0),(4,1)}, ACGTACGT self wordSize4‚Üí{(0,0),(0,4),(1,1),(2,2),(3,3),(4,0),(4,4)}, ACGT self main-diagonal oracles; word>seq/null/empty/disjoint‚Üíno dots, non-positive wordSize/stepSize throws; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters; orientation + case-insensitivity assumptions, deviations None.
- [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics ortholog & in-paralog detection unit (`COMPGEN-ORTHO-001`): orthologs by Reciprocal Best Hits (RBH ‚Äî each gene the other's best hit across two genomes, Moreno-Hagelsieb 2008 / Tatusov 1997 / Fitch 1970 speciation-vs-duplication), recent (in-)paralogs by within-genome mutual best hits (Remm 2001); best hit=max-similarity with deterministic tie-break, reciprocity mandatory (one-directional best hit is NOT an ortholog = the guarded defect), ‚â•50% coverage + min-similarity gates, partial-matching output, empty‚Üíno orthologs / single-gene‚Üíno paralogs; reciprocity/non-reciprocity(RBH count 1)/in-paralog oracles; one assumption = alignment-free 5-mer Jaccard replaces BLAST bit-score ranking (reciprocity/coverage/threshold source-backed); shared anchor for COMPGEN-RBH-001, the core/shared-gene sub-unit of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]]; sibling of ANI/synteny/conserved-clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics signed-permutation / breakpoint rearrangement-detection unit (`COMPGEN-REARR-001` + `COMPGEN-REVERSAL-001`): the Hannenhalli‚ÄìPevzner/Bafna‚ÄìPevzner theory ‚Äî signed permutation (strand=sign), extended `(0,‚Ä¶,n+1)` (endpoints=telomeres), breakpoint = consecutive pair where neither `(x,y)` nor `(‚àíy,‚àíx)` survives in Œ≤, `b(Œ±)` count = `d_BP=n‚àísim(common adjacencies)`, reversal-distance lower bound `d‚â•b/2`; `ClassifyRearrangement` ‚Üí Inversion (reversal = sign-flip + local reverse) vs Transposition (block move preserving orientation), Translocation/Deletion/Insertion/Duplication "Not implemented" (single permutation can't express them); Hunter `(‚àí2,‚àí3,+1,+6,‚àí5,‚àí4)`‚Üíb=6/d‚â•3, identity‚Üí0, single-inversion `(+1,‚àí4,‚àí3,‚àí2,+5)`‚Üíb=2 oracles; `b‚àà[0,n+1]` invariant; the signed-permutation `alternative_to` the block-signal [[synteny-and-rearrangement-detection]], sibling of ANI/ortholog/clusters/dot-plot; deviations None.
- [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics end-to-end pipeline (`CompareGenomes`): partitions each genome's genes into core (conserved = RBH ortholog pairs, Tettelin 2005 pan-genome) vs dispensable (genome-specific = the rest), reports Conserved/Specific1/Specific2 + OverallSynteny=(genes in MCScanX syntenic blocks)/min(|g1|,|g2|) clamped ‚â§1; symmetric partition, empty‚Üíall-0; orchestrates RBH ortholog detection (COMPGEN-RBH-001) + synteny (COMPGEN-SYNTENY-001); sibling of [[average-nucleotide-identity]] & [[conserved-gene-clusters-common-intervals]]; two source-backed assumptions (alignment-free RBH gate, MCScanX ‚â•5-anchor block threshold ‚Üí OverallSynteny can be 0 with conserved orthologs); deviations None.
- [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] ‚Äî protein-disorder family MoRF unit (DISORDER-MORF-001, second DISORDER-* unit): Molecular Recognition Feature prediction by the "dip within disorder" heuristic (Oldfield 2005 / Cheng-Oldfield PMC2570644 / Mohan 2006) ‚Äî a short ordered run (per-residue TOP-IDP disorder score <0.5) of total length 10‚Äì70 flanked on both sides by disorder (score ‚â•0.5) = one MoRF; 0.5 order/disorder threshold, Œ±/Œ≤/Œπ bound-state sub-types (Mohan 2006), MoRF score‚àà[0,1] rising with dip depth; terminal dip / fully-ordered / fully-disordered / out-of-band ‚Üí none; TOP-IDP normalized `(raw+0.884)/1.871` per-residue score from `PredictDisorder`; one assumption = exact flank-length params paywalled ‚Üí qualitative criterion (threshold/band/shape source-traceable); distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]; deviations None.
- [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] ‚Äî protein disorder / features family anchor (first DISORDER-* unit, DISORDER-LC-001): the SEG algorithm (Wootton & Federhen 1993/1996) partitioning a protein into low-/high-complexity segments; complexity = Shannon entropy `H=‚àíŒ£p·µ¢log‚ÇÇp·µ¢` bits/residue (max log‚ÇÇ20‚âà4.322), two-stage scan with W=12 trigger window / K1=2.2 trigger cutoff / K2=2.5 extension cutoff (NCBI `blast_seg.c` defaults); homopolymer H=0 triggers, 12-distinct H‚âà3.585>K2 no segment; X-rich/X-Y-rich label + greedy single-residue extension are flagged repository extensions not moving boundaries; distinct from [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp|intrinsic-disorder prediction]] (TOP-IDP) and the genomic-DNA [[repetitive-element-detection]] low-complexity counterpart.
- [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]] ‚Äî protein-disorder family shared anchor (DISORDER-PRED-001 + DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001 + DISORDER-REGION-001): the TOP-IDP `PredictDisorder` sliding-window intrinsic-disorder predictor (Campen 2008) that [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]] + disordered-region detection sit on; also hosts the region-detection layer (contiguous runs ‚â• minRegionLength, default RegionType classification proline-rich/acidic/basic/Ser-Thr-rich > 0.25 + Long/Standard IDR, opt-in MobiDB-lite flavor scheme); per-residue S·µ¢=mean over window of min-max-normalized TOP-IDP `(p‚àí(‚àí0.884))/1.871 ‚àà [0,1]`, disordered when S·µ¢‚â•0.542 (max-likelihood cutoff), default window 21 (edge-clipped) / minRegionLength 5; Dunker 2001 disorder{A,R,G,Q,S,P,E,K}/order{W,C,F,I,Y,V,L,N}/ambiguous{D,H,M,T} sets + Kyte-Doolittle `CalculateHydropathy`; W30‚Üí0.0/P30‚Üí1.0/E30‚Üí0.866 oracles, null/empty‚Üíempty, non-canonical skipped (all-unknown window‚Üí0.0), case-insensitive, O(n¬∑w); also anchors the raw per-residue propensity primitives (DISORDER-PROPENSITY-001: `GetDisorderPropensity` returns the RAW un-normalized Table-2 value, unknown‚Üí0.0, + the two public Dunker sets); assumptions None (params source-traced), impl = simplified single-feature heuristic not competitive with IUPred2A/MobiDB-lite; distinct sibling of [[protein-low-complexity-seg]].
- [[coiled-coil-prediction]] ‚Äî ProteinMotif family anchor (first ingested unit, PROTMOTIF-CC-001): the heptad a/d hydrophobic-core occupancy coiled-coil predictor `ProteinMotifFinder.PredictCoiledCoils` ‚Äî for each window `score = (#a/d positions with residue ‚àà {I,L,V})/(#a/d positions)` maximised over the 7 heptad registers (`p(k,r)=(k‚àír) mod 7`, core a=0/d=3), contiguous windows with score ‚â• threshold mapped to residue regions ‚â•21 residues (3 heptads) with peak `Score‚àà[0,1]`; defaults window 28 (4 heptads, Lupas 1991) / threshold 0.5 / min-region 21 (Mason & Arndt ‚â•3-heptad); INV-01..05 (score‚àà[0,1]; region‚â•21; len<window‚Üíempty; off-frame found via 7-register max); (LAALAAA)√ó5‚Üí(0,34,1.0) / no-{I,L,V}‚Üínone / (LAAAAAA)‚Üí0.5 boundary oracles; COILS 21√ó20 PSSM deliberately omitted (weights not retrievable, use COILS/Paircoil2 for P-scores) + {I,L,V}-only core-set assumption (source-verbatim); sequence-only heuristic, distinct from the ProteinPred disorder/features family ([[protein-low-complexity-seg]], [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]], [[morf-prediction-dip-in-disorder]]).
- [[common-protein-motifs]] ‚Äî ProteinMotif family second unit (PROTMOTIF-COMMON-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindCommonMotifs`): scans an amino-acid sequence against a fixed built-in `CommonMotifs` dictionary of canonical PROSITE patterns and aggregates every hit carrying its accession/name ‚Äî PS00001 `ASN_GLYCOSYLATION` `N-{P}-[ST]-{P}`, PS00005 `PKC_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x-[RK]`, PS00006 `CK2_PHOSPHO_SITE` `[ST]-x(2)-[DE]`, PS00016 `RGD` `R-G-D`, PS00017 `ATP_GTP_A` `[AG]-x(4)-G-K-[ST]`; PROSITE syntax (`x` wildcard, `[ ]` allowed set, `{ }` excluded set, `x(n)`/`x(m,n)` repetition); 0-based-inclusive `MotifMatch.Start`/`End` (PROSITE reports 1-based) + substring invariant + overlaps-all-reported (ScanProsite "overlaps, no includes"); `NFTA`/Pro-exclusion-no-match/`SAR`/`SAAE`+`SDED`/`GXXXXGKS`/`RGD`+`RGD`-overlap oracles; one API-shape assumption (0- vs 1-based origin, no correctness effect); the **protein** fixed-catalog analogue of the DNA [[regulatory-element-detection]], sibling of the windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], distinct from the caller-supplied-set DNA exact [[known-motif-search]].
- [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] ‚Äî ProteinMotif family third unit (PROTMOTIF-DOMAIN-001): protein **domain** prediction + **signal-peptide** prediction. `ProteinMotifFinder.FindDomains` scans PROSITE **domain patterns** (PS00028 C2H2 zinc finger/PF00096, PS00017 P-loop/PF00069, PS00678 WD40 15-residue/PF00400; ScanProsite‚Üíregex), 0-based inclusive hits, tandem repeats all detected ‚Äî SH3/PDZ excluded (PROSITE **PROFILEs**, no deterministic pattern). Opt-in `FindDomainsByHmm`/`Plan7ProfileHmm` reproduces the **HMMER3** engine over 3 bundled CC0 Pfam HMMs (SH3/PDZ/WD40): Viterbi/Forward log-odds (exact 1e-9 hand-HMM), local-multihit `pre_score` vs Swiss-Prot `bg->f` (~1e-5-bit hmmsearch parity), null2 bias (omega 1/256), Gumbel/exponential E-values (`E=P¬∑Z`), `p7_domaindef` multi-domain envelope decomposition (GBB1/PF00400‚Üí7 blades exact) + stochastic-traceback clustering for overlapping tandems (fixed-seed Easel LCG 42), verified vs pyhmmer 0.12.1. `PredictSignalPeptide` = von Heijne tripartite n(K/R+)/h(hydrophobic Œ±-helix)/c(polar) + ‚àí1,‚àí3 rule {A,G,S}, score (n+2h+c)/4 with evidence-based constraints (nScore>0, hScore‚â•0.5) and Probability=Score. Six resolved design decisions; MSV/bias prefilters + exact-RNG-bit parity + full-Pfam coverage out of scope (research-grade). Sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] & [[common-protein-motifs]].
- [[protein-motif-pattern-search]] ‚Äî ProteinMotif family general engine (PROTMOTIF-FIND-001, `ProteinMotifFinder.FindMotifByPattern`): the **general, arbitrary caller-supplied** PROSITE-pattern protein motif finder underneath the fixed-dictionary [[common-protein-motifs]]. Three primitives ‚Äî `ConvertPrositeToRegex` (PROSITE‚Üíregex: `x`‚Üí`.`, `[ABC]`‚Üí`[ABC]`, `{ABC}`‚Üí`[^ABC]`, `x(n)`‚Üí`.{n}`, `x(n,m)`‚Üí`.{n,m}`, `<`‚Üí`^`, `>`‚Üí`$`); `FindMotifByPattern` (all matches incl. overlaps via zero-width lookahead `(?=(pattern))` per ScanProsite, 0-based `MotifMatch.Start`/`End`, case-insensitive, empty/null‚Üíempty, invalid regex handled gracefully); and information-content scoring `CalculateMotifScore` IC=Œ£log‚ÇÇ(20/allowed_count) over constrained positions (`x`=0 bits, fixed‚âà4.32 bits) + `CalculateEValue` E=(N‚àíL+1)¬∑2^(‚àíIC), Schneider & Stephens 1990 (NOT BLAST statistics ‚Äî that citation was removed). Pins the PROSITE-pattern catalog (PS00001/00004‚Äì00009/00016‚Äì00018/00028 C2H2/00029 leucine-zipper) and fixed two impl bugs (PS00007 exact repeat counts; PS00018 EF-hand `{W}`+trailing `[LIVMFYW]`); five non-PROSITE linear motifs literature-verified (NLS1/NES1/SIM1/WW1/SH3_1); SKIP-FLAG=TRUE common sites noted. Sibling of the fixed-catalog [[common-protein-motifs]], windowed [[coiled-coil-prediction]], and longer-signature [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]]; all assumptions eliminated (0-vs-1-based coordinate convention only). Revalidated by PROTMOTIF-PATTERN-001 ([[protmotif-pattern-001-evidence]]), which adds the end-to-end `FindMotifByProsite` path and the `*`-rejection / range-only-on-`x` PA-line grammar contracts.
- [[transmembrane-helix-prediction]] ‚Äî ProteinMotif family transmembrane-helix unit (PROTMOTIF-TM-001): the classic **Kyte-Doolittle (1982) hydropathy sliding window** for membrane-spanning Œ±-helices ‚Äî slide a window `W=19`, score each window as the **arithmetic mean** of per-residue Kyte-Doolittle hydropathy (`HydropathyScale` I 4.5‚Ä¶R ‚àí4.5), emit contiguous runs with window mean **‚â• threshold 1.6** as segments (`[i‚ÇÄ, i‚ÇÅ+W‚àí1]`, peak `Score`); profile length `n‚àíW+1`, non-standard residues excluded from the mean, `<W`/null/empty‚Üíempty; window 19 & min-span=W justified by ~18‚Äì21 residues / ~3‚Äì4 nm bilayer. Oracles `D√ó10+L√ó20+D√ó10`‚Üí(5,34) peak 3.8 / `D√ó40`‚Üínone / `L√ó19`‚Üí(0,18,3.8). One assumption (`End=lastPassingProfileIndex+W‚àí1` clamped, 2026-06-16 off-by-one fix), no deviations; sequence-only hydrophobicity heuristic ‚Äî no in-out topology / positive-inside rule / TMHMM-Phobius HMM. Shares the Kyte-Doolittle scale with [[intrinsic-disorder-prediction-top-idp]]'s `CalculateHydropathy`; distinct sibling of [[coiled-coil-prediction]] (heptad a/d, not window-mean), [[common-protein-motifs]], [[protein-domain-and-signal-peptide-prediction]] (cleaved signal peptide, not membrane span) & [[protein-motif-pattern-search]].
- [[aneuploidy-detection]] ‚Äî chromosome copy-number/ploidy family anchor (first Chromosome-analysis unit): abnormal chromosome count from read depth ‚Äî per-bin CN=round(2^log2(depth/median)√ó2) clamped [0,10], whole-chromosome call needs dominant CN across ‚â•80% of bins (mosaicism tolerance), confidence=1‚àímin(1,|CN/2‚àí2^logRatio|)=1.0 at integer-CN ratios; nullisomy..pentasomy terminology; Down/Edwards/Patau/Turner/Klinefelter oracles; sex-chromosomes-not-special-cased + partial-aneuploidy-needs-80%-bins limitations.
- [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] ‚Äî epigenetics family bisulfite-sequencing unit (second EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-BISULF-001): base-level DNA-methylation calling from sodium-bisulfite reads ‚Äî distinct from the age clock (it *produces* the Œ≤-values a clock consumes). Three deterministic ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: (1) `SimulateBisulfiteConversion` ‚Äî single-strand per-base Frommer 1992 rule (unprotected C‚ÜíT, protected 5mC stays C, non-C unchanged, case preserved, ACGTCGAA{1}‚ÜíACGTTGAA); (2) `CalculateMethylationFromBisulfite` ‚Äî reuses `FindCpGSites`, Bismark C=methylated/T=unmethylated tally, level = meth/(meth+unmeth)‚àà[0,1], zero-coverage sites excluded (ACGTACGT reads‚Üí0.5&0.0); (3) `GenerateMethylationProfile` ‚Äî Schultz 2012 per-context weighted level Œ£(level¬∑coverage)/Œ£coverage (0.25‚âÝunweighted 0.5), zero-total-coverage falls back to unweighted mean; CpG needs C+G, neither-C-nor-T call ignored, past-reference ignored; research-grade, no CHG/CHH calling / no complement merge / no non-conversion-rate correction; sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]; deviations None.
- [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] ‚Äî epigenetics family anchor (first EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-AGE-001): DNAm ("epigenetic") age from methylation Œ≤-values via the Horvath 2013 multi-tissue clock ‚Äî two-stage model, linear predictor `Y = intercept + Œ£ coef_i¬∑Œ≤_i` over 353 elastic-net-selected clock CpGs (transformed-age units), then the two-branch inverse calibration `anti.trafo` (adult.age=20): `21¬∑exp(Y)‚àí1` for Y<0 (exponential), `21¬∑Y+20` for Y‚â•0 (linear), continuous at (0,20)=age 20; embedded intercept 0.695507258 + 353 `CoefficientTraining` weights cross-verified byte-identical; invariants Y=0‚Üí20 / CpGs-absent-ignored / empty-map‚ÜíF‚Åª¬π(intercept); null‚ÜíArgumentNullException, empty coefficients‚ÜíArgumentException; anti.trafo oracles (0‚Üí20, 1‚Üí41, ‚àí1‚Üí6.7254682646, ‚àí2.5‚Üí0.7237849711) + Y=0.684247258‚Üí34.369192418; scope = multi-tissue only (algorithm doc later extends to Horvath-2018 skin&blood 391-CpG + Levine-2018 PhenoAge 513-CpG no-transform); no BMIQ input normalisation (research-grade); sibling [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] (produces the Œ≤-values); third Epigenetics sibling [[chromatin-state-prediction]] (histone-mark axis).
- [[cpg-island-detection]] ‚Äî epigenetics family CpG site & island unit (fourth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CPG-001): sequence-only CpG dinucleotide detection (no methylation state ‚Äî distinct from all siblings). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `FindCpGSites` (linear scan, 0-based C position, `CGCG`‚Üí2 sites, reused by [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]); `CalculateCpGObservedExpected` (Gardiner-Garden O/E=CpG/((C¬∑G)/L), div-by-zero guard‚Üí0, oracles CGCG√ó 2.0/ACGTCGACG 3.0/ACGT 4.0/AT-only 0); `FindCpGIslands` (sliding-window merge, default ‚â•200bp/GC‚â•0.5/O-E‚â•0.6 inclusive, 0-based inclusive-Start/exclusive-End tuple, 400bp CGCG‚Üí1 island, O(n¬∑w)); GpC‚âÝCpG, case-insensitive; Takai-Jones 2002 stricter (‚â•500/55%/0.65) + Saxonov 2006 alt-expected not preset (custom args); Gardiner-Garden & Frommer 1987 + Takai-Jones + Saxonov + Wikipedia; assumptions None. Siblings [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]/[[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]].
- [[chromatin-state-prediction]] ‚Äî epigenetics family chromatin-state / histone-mark unit (third EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-CHROM-001): ChromHMM-style (Ernst & Kellis 2012) annotation of a locus from the *combination of present histone marks* ‚Äî distinct from the methylation siblings (operates on histone ChIP-seq signals, not DNA methylation). Binary present/absent mark model (ChromHMM binarizes then learns; state = function of the SET of present marks, magnitude beyond the call irrelevant = binary invariance); `PredictChromatinState` takes the six Roadmap 18-state marks {H3K4me3, H3K4me1, H3K27ac, H3K36me3, H3K27me3, H3K9me3} as [0,1] signals, calls present > threshold (default 0.5), maps pattern ‚Üí ActivePromoter(TssA, H3K4me3¬±H3K27ac)/ActiveEnhancer(H3K4me1+H3K27ac)/WeakEnhancer(H3K4me1 no H3K27ac)/Transcribed(Tx, H3K36me3)/Repressed(ReprPC, H3K27me3)/Heterochromatin(Het, H3K9me3)/BivalentPromoter(TssBiv, H3K4me3+H3K27me3)/BivalentEnhancer(EnhBiv, H3K4me1+H3K27me3)/LowSignal(Quies, none); two combinatorial rules ‚Äî bivalency is a state not a contradiction, promoter(H3K4me3) dominates enhancer(H3K4me1); companions `AnnotateHistoneModifications` (per-mark region label) + `FindAccessibleRegions` (ATAC-like contiguous-merge + minWidth); research-grade ‚Äî state-assignment logic source-backed, NOT a trained HMM (no LearnModel/Poisson binarization/spatial context); two assumptions (0.5 threshold, single-locus precedence); sibling of [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]] & [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]]; no contradictions.
- [[differentially-methylated-regions]] ‚Äî epigenetics family DMR-detection unit (fifth EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-DMR-001): methylKit (Akalin 2012) two-sample tiling-window + Fisher's-exact-test model ‚Äî *compares* methylation between two samples (distinct from the single-sample siblings), consuming the per-CpG C/(C+T) Œ≤-values [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] produces over the CpGs [[cpg-island-detection]] locates. Fixed tiles (`win.size=1000/step.size=1000/cov.bases=0`, `tileMethylCounts`), meth.diff=group2%‚àígroup1% (percentage points), per-window pooled 2√ó2 methylated/unmethylated counts ‚Üí Fisher's exact (one sample per group; replicates‚Üílogistic regression out of scope), hypergeometric single-table p `(a+b)!(c+d)!(a+c)!(b+d)!/(a!b!c!d!n!)` + two-sided ‚â§-observed sum; report q<0.01 AND |meth.diff|>25 strict (`getMethylDiff`): hyper meth.diff>+25 / hypo <‚àí25; empty‚Üíno DMRs, zero-coverage group / zero marginal‚Üíp=1.0, |meth.diff|=25‚Üíexcluded; oracles Fisher a=1/b=9/c=11/d=3‚Üí‚âà0.001346076, hyper window g1=0.0/g2=1.0‚Üí+100/p‚âà0; two evidence-backed assumptions (per-window pooling, numC/numT=round(level√ócoverage)); research-grade (no logistic path/SLIM/overlapping tiles); siblings [[epigenetic-age-horvath-clock]]/[[chromatin-state-prediction]]; no contradictions.
- [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] ‚Äî Analysis alignment-free pairwise-similarity unit (`GENOMIC-SIMILARITY-001`, `GenomicAnalyzer.CalculateSimilarity`): Jaccard index of the two sequences' distinct k-mer sets (Jaccard 1901 `|A‚à©B|/|A‚à™B|` over HashSet k-mer sets, Ondov 2016 *Mash* fraction-of-shared-k-mers), exact (no MinHash sketch) J√ó100 in `[0,100]`, O(n+m); INV symmetry / identical‚Üí100 / disjoint‚Üí0 / distinct-set (repeats once); default k=5, empty-union‚Üí0 (ASM-1 convention), √ó100 scaling; k=3 oracles 80/(100/3)/100/0; `alternative_to` positional [[alignment-statistics]], the 5-mer-Jaccard metric behind [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] and the exact-set basis Mash sketches for [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; limitations = exact-match/composition-only; deviations None.
- [[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] ‚Äî K-mer family alignment-free word-frequency **distance** unit (`KMER-DIST-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.KmerDistance`): Euclidean (L2) distance between two sequences' normalized k-mer **frequency** vectors `f_s(w)=count/(L‚àík+1)` over the union of observed k-mers (absent word‚Üí0 component), exact/O(n+m); Zielezinski 2017 word-vector model + Lau 2022 frequency normalization + Vinga-Almeida 2003 4^k-vector + Boden 2014 relative-frequency Euclidean; INV d(x,x)=0 / symmetric / ‚â•0 / disjoint-single-kmer‚Üí‚àö2; ‚àö0.11‚âà0.3316624790 (ATGTGTG/CATGTG k=3) + ‚àö0.125 (AAAA/AAAT k=1) oracles; case-insensitive (ASM-01) + empty/L<k‚Üízero-vector (ASM-02); count-based/Manhattan/Canberra/Chebyshev/cosine/D2/spaced-word not implemented, deviations None; `alternative_to` the presence/absence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]] (this captures abundance), shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]] ‚Äî K-mer family async count unit (`KMER-ASYNC-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersAsync`): the cooperatively cancelable, progress-reporting thread-pool wrapper over synchronous `CountKmers` ‚Äî numeric result identical to the sync reference (counts fixed by the k-mer formula `L ‚àí k + 1`, n·µè possible), so the distinctive validated content is *execution* not arithmetic: the .NET cancellation contract (`ThrowIfCancellationRequested`‚ÜíOperationCanceledException + Canceled state, pre-start `Task.Run(func,token)` cancellation, awaiting a canceled task throws) + `IProgress<double>` 0‚Üí1.0; INV Œ£counts=L‚àík+1 / empty¬∑k>L‚Üíempty dict / k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException via awaited task; uppercased (case-insensitive) + alphabet-agnostic (IUPAC N counted literally); ATGG‚Üí{ATG:1,TGG:1} + GTAGAGCTGT oracles; one assumption = numeric contract identical to sync (non-correctness-affecting); single-thread offload (not parallelized), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; wraps sync KMER-COUNT-001 (not yet ingested); record [[kmer-async-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-generation]] ‚Äî K-mer family *space-enumeration* unit (`KMER-GENERATE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.GenerateAllKmers`): exhaustive enumeration of ALL possible k-mers of length `k` over an alphabet ‚Äî the complete k-mer universe `Œ£^k` of size `n^k` (4^k for DNA), depends only on `k`+alphabet not on any sequence; DISTINCT from counting (produces the full n^k word set / address space, siblings extract observed substrings + counts); k-fold Cartesian product `itertools.product(Œ£,repeat=k)`, lazy recursive prefix-extension, odometer emission ‚Üí lexicographic for a sorted alphabet; INV n^k count / all-distinct-set / length-k / sorted‚Üílexicographic; k=1‚Üí{A,C,G,T}, k=2‚Üí16 (AA..TT), k=3‚Üí64, protein 20^2=400, single-letter 1^4=1 oracles; k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty alphabet‚ÜíArgumentException, unsorted‚Üípositional order, verbatim/no-dedup; O(k¬∑n^k) time/O(k) lazy space, suffix-tree N/A (generates not searches); shares the "ACGT"-default + k‚â§0-throws API contract with [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]] but NOT the `CountKmers` primitive; supplies the index space for [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]]/[[k-mer-euclidean-distance]]/[[de-bruijn-graph-assembly]]; deviations None; record [[kmer-generate-001-evidence]].
