- [[k-mer-positions]] ‚Äî K-mer family *occurrence-index* unit (`KMER-POSITIONS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindKmerPositions`): the ascending 0-based positions where a given k-mer occurs in a sequence ‚Äî *where*, not *how many* (the inverse index to the counting units) ‚Äî solving the exact Pattern Matching Problem `Occ(P,T)={i‚àà[0,L‚àík]:T[i..i+k)=P}` with all overlapping starts reported; INV-01..04 (match predicate / ascending / count=overlap-occurrences / range `[0,L‚àík]`, empty when k>L); case-insensitive upper-casing (sibling `CountKmers`), unrestricted-text alphabet, null/empty & k>L & absent ‚Üí empty (no throw), whole-seq‚Üí`[0]`; `ATAT`/`GATATATGCATATACTT`‚Üí`[1,3,9]` + `AA`/`AAAA`‚Üí`[0,1,2]` oracles; O(L¬∑k) naive span scan, suffix-tree evaluated-not-used (unordered leaves, single-query no amortization); three API-shape assumptions (0-based, case-fold, empty-not-throw), deviations None; the single-pattern K-mer sibling of multi-pattern [[known-motif-search]], distinct from the counting siblings [[both-strand-kmer-counting]]/[[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-positions-001-evidence]].
- [[both-strand-kmer-counting]] ‚Äî K-mer family strand-aware count unit (`KMER-BOTH-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.CountKmersBothStrands`): the ADDITIVE / kPAL-"balance" both-strand profile `count[w] = forward[w] + forward[RC(w)]` (count k-mers of S and of RC(S), sum per key), grounded in inversion symmetry (Shporer 2016) + kPAL balance (Anvar 2014); distinct from ‚Äî and does NOT implement ‚Äî the canonical-collapsing convention (lexicographically-smaller of {w,RC(w)} as one key, Jellyfish `-C` / Mash); INV Œ£count=2¬∑(L‚àík+1) / count[w]=count[RC(w)] strand-symmetric / palindrome RC(w)=w‚Üícount doubled on one key; two linear passes O(n¬∑k), suffix-tree evaluated-not-used; case-insensitive/IUPAC-complemented, empty¬∑k>L‚Üíempty dict, k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException (inherited from `CountKmers`); ATGGC k=2‚Üí{AT:2,TG:1,GG:1,GC:2,CC:1,CA:1} + ACGT‚Üí{AC:2,CG:2,GT:2} + AAA‚Üí{AA:2,TT:2} oracles; built on the same sync `CountKmers` primitive as [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]; two API-shape assumptions, deviations None; record [[kmer-both-001-evidence]].
- [[k-mer-statistics]] ‚Äî K-mer family *summary-statistics* unit (`KMER-STATS-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.AnalyzeKmers`): a companion summary layer over the shared `CountKmers` multiset that reduces the count profile to `KmerStatistics` {TotalKmers=L‚àík+1=Œ£counts, UniqueKmers=**distinct** count, MaxCount, MinCount, AverageCount=total/distinct (rounded 2dp), Entropy=Shannon **k-entropy** `‚àíŒ£ p(Œ±)log‚ÇÇp(Œ±)`, `p=mult/(L‚àík+1)`, bits}; the one distinct piece of content is the k-entropy (Manca 2021 + Entropy‚ÄìRank Ratio, corroborated by Wikipedia/BioInfoLogics count tables); GOTCHA `UniqueKmers` = distinct count NOT the count==1 singletons (that is KMER-UNIQUE-001); INV Total=Œ£counts / Unique=distinct(CountKmers) / homopolymer‚ÜíH0,max=min=total / all-distinct‚ÜíH log‚ÇÇD,max=min=1 / k>L¬∑empty‚Üíall-zero; GTAGAGCTGT k=1 (10/4/4/1/2.5/1.8464) + k=3 (8/8/1/1/log‚ÇÇ8=3.0) + ATCGATCAC k=3 (7/6/2/1/2.5216) + AAAA k=2 (3/1/3/3/0) oracles; case-insensitive, k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException; two presentation-only assumptions (AverageCount 2dp, Entropy unrounded); shares the `CountKmers` primitive with [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]], distinct from generation/positions/distance siblings; deviations None; record [[kmer-stats-001-evidence]]. Also the home of the **second entry point** for the same k-entropy: `SequenceComplexity.CalculateKmerEntropy` (SEQ-COMPLEX-KMER-001, record [[seq-complex-kmer-001-evidence]]) ‚Äî the entropy member of the `SEQ-COMPLEX-*` complexity family (siblings [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]]/[[dust-low-complexity-score]]), identical formula from a different class.
- [[unique-and-mincount-kmers]] ‚Äî K-mer family *frequency-filtering* unit (`KMER-UNIQUE-001`, `KmerAnalyzer.FindUniqueKmers` + `FindKmersWithMinCount`): selects k-mers by their per-k-mer **Count** (overlapping occurrences, Compeau & Pevzner `Count(Text,Pattern)`) at opposite ends of the frequency distribution ‚Äî `FindUniqueKmers` = the `Count==1` **singletons**, `FindKmersWithMinCount` = the `Count‚â•minCount` **recurrent** k-mers ordered by count desc; total/distinct/unique terminology (BioInfoLogics: unique = "appear only once"; Wikipedia L‚àík+1 total); GOTCHA "unique"=singleton set here ‚âÝ [[k-mer-statistics]]'s `UniqueKmers`=distinct count (ATCGATCAC k=3 ‚Üí 5 unique vs 6 distinct, ATC=2 excluded); oracles ATCGATCAC k=3‚Üí{TCG,CGA,GAT,TCA,CAC}, AGAT k=2‚Üí{AG,GA,AT}, ACGTACGT k=4 FindKmersWithMinCount(‚Ä¶,2)‚Üí{(ACGT,2)}/(‚Ä¶,1)‚Üíall-4-count-desc/FindUniqueKmers‚Üí{CGTA,GTAC,TACG}, AAAAA k=3‚Üí‚àÖ; case-insensitive, k‚â§0‚ÜíArgumentOutOfRangeException, empty¬∑k>L‚Üíempty; two assumptions (minCount‚â§1‚Üíall distinct count-desc; upper-casing), deviations None; filters the shared `CountKmers` multiset like [[asynchronous-kmer-counting]]/[[both-strand-kmer-counting]]; record [[kmer-unique-001-evidence]].
- [[longest-common-substring]] ‚Äî Sequence-Comparison longest-common-substring / common-region-detection unit (`GENOMIC-COMMON-001`): the maximal *contiguous* substring shared by two strings (distinct from the gapped longest common *subsequence*) via a generalized suffix tree (LCS = deepest internal node whose subtree holds leaves from both strings, Œò(n+m) build + DFS, Gusfield 1997); `FindLongestCommonRegion` (0-based positions in both) + `FindCommonRegions(minLength)` (all distinct shared runs ‚â• minLength), None=empty/len 0/pos ‚àí1, identical‚Üíwhole seq at 0/0; documented deterministic first-found-in-`other` tie-break (CACAGAG/TACATAGAT ties ACA vs AGA ‚Üí ACA); Wikipedia + GeeksforGeeks sources, shares the suffix-tree exact-match engine with [[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[longest-repeated-substring]] ‚Äî Repeat-Analysis LRS + repeat-enumeration unit (`GENOMIC-REPEAT-001`): the longest substring recurring within *one* DNA sequence (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindLongestRepeat`) + all distinct substrings occurring ‚â•2√ó with length ‚â• minLength (`FindRepeats`), both via the *single-string* suffix tree's deepest internal node with ‚â•2 leaves (string depth = repeat length; CMU ¬ß2.1 / Wikipedia / GeeksforGeeks App-3 / Gusfield 5.4); overlaps counted, no-repeat/empty‚Üí`RepeatInfo.None`, `minLength‚â§0`‚Üí`max(1,minLength)`, ACGT-only, no reverse-complement/maximal-repeat classification; FindRepeats via sorted-suffix adjacent-LCP *every-prefix* enumeration (O(n¬≤), FINDINGS_REGISTER short-prefix fix); ATCGATCGA‚ÜíATCGA{0,4}, AAAAAAAAAA‚ÜíAAAAAAAAA{0,1}, ATATATA‚ÜíATATA{0,2}, ACGTACGTTTTTACGT@3‚Üí8-substring oracles; the *single-string* sibling of [[longest-common-substring]], distinct from the tandem/inverted [[repetitive-element-detection]] anchor; tie-break + ascending-positions assumptions, deviations None.
- [[open-reading-frame-detection]] ‚Äî Analysis ORF-detection unit (`GENOMIC-ORF-001`): six-frame ATG‚Üífirst-in-frame-stop enumeration (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindOpenReadingFrames`), standard code (start ATG / stops TAA-TAG-TGA), reported span **includes** the stop (Length%3==0) while the translated protein **excludes** it; THE correctness rule = every in-frame ATG reaching a stop reported, so **nested ORFs sharing a stop** both returned (Rosalind `MGMTPRLGLESLLE`/`MTPRLGLESLLE`), ATG-with-no-stop‚Üínone; `minLength` in **nucleotides** inclusive (default 100), 0-based Position, Frame 1‚Äì3 + IsReverseComplement, INV-01..05 (starts ATG / ends stop / len%3==0 / ‚â•minLength / six-frame), O(n¬≤) worst / O(n) typical; Rosalind_99‚Üí4 distinct proteins + ATGAAAAAATAA‚ÜíMKK oracles; Rosalind + Wikipedia + NCBI ORFfinder + transl_table=1 sources; deviations None (one fixed greedy bug); deliberately **not** contract-equivalent to annotation `GenomeAnnotator.FindOrfs` (ANNOT-ORF-001: ATG/GTG/TTG, aa-length, strand/start flags) or `Translator.FindOrfs` (genetic-code-parameterized); coding potential is a separate step ([[coding-potential-hexamer-score]]).
- [[known-motif-search]] ‚Äî Motif-Analysis known-motif-search anchor (`GENOMIC-MOTIFS-001`): multi-pattern **exact** substring matching of a caller-supplied set of known query motifs (`GenomicAnalyzer.FindMotif`) ‚Äî the "you know what you're looking for" exact-equality baseline, distinct from motif *discovery* and *degenerate* (IUPAC/PROSITE/PWM) matching; THE correctness rule = all **overlapping** occurrences reported (AAA in AAAAA‚Üí{0,1,2}, per Gusfield/Biopython `count_overlap` 3-not-2); 0-based sorted positions, per-motif position lists with absent motifs omitted, upper-cased result keys, empty/whitespace motif‚Üíno entry (`Array.Empty<int>()`); EcoRI GAATTC‚Üí{0,9} + `{ACGT,AA,TTT}` in ACGTACGTAA oracles; Tufts/Gusfield + Biopython `Seq.search` + Wikipedia "Restriction site" sources; shares exact-all-occurrences semantics with [[longest-common-substring]]/[[dot-plot-word-match]]; deviations None.
- [[alpha-diversity]] ‚Äî Metagenomics diversity family anchor (first META-* unit, META-ALPHA-001): within-sample diversity indices from one taxon‚Üíabundance map (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateAlphaDiversity` ‚Üí `AlphaDiversity` record) ‚Äî observed richness S_obs, Shannon H=‚àíŒ£p·µ¢ln(p·µ¢) in nats, Simpson concentration Œª=Œ£p·µ¢¬≤, inverse Simpson 1/Œª (Hill order-2 effective species), Pielou evenness J=H/ln(S) for S>1 else 0, Chao1 S_obs+f‚ÇÅ¬≤/(2f‚ÇÇ) (f‚ÇÇ=0‚Üíbias-corrected S_obs+f‚ÇÅ(f‚ÇÅ‚àí1)/2, non-integer/proportional‚ÜíS_obs); Whittaker 1960 Œ±/Œ≤/Œ≥ framework, Shannon 1948/Simpson 1949/Hill 1973/Chao 1984/Pielou 1966; counts-or-proportions internally normalized, non-positive filtered, O(n); empty/null‚Üíall-0, single species‚ÜíH0/Œª1/J0; one accepted deviation = Chao1 count-vs-proportion gate; between-sample [[beta-diversity]] its sibling; deviations else None.
- [[metagenomic-binning]] ‚Äî Metagenomics family binning unit (third META-* unit, META-BIN-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.BinContigs`): groups mixed-community contigs back to their genome of origin (MAGs) by k-means over a composite distance `|ŒîGC|+|Œîcoverage|+TNF-Pearson-distance` (GC-sorted deterministic centroid init, ‚â§50 iters, minBinSize 500 kb filter) ‚Üí `GenomeBin` records; completeness=`min(L/expectedGenomeSize√ó100,100)` (default 4 Mbp) + contamination=`min(gcStdDev/0.5√ó100,100)` are LENGTH-RATIO/GC-VARIANCE **proxies** (CheckM marker-gene QC now built as a SEPARATE opt-in path ‚Äî CheckM Eqs. 1‚Äì2 over CC0 Pfam marker sets, `EstimateBinQualityFromMarkerCounts`/`DetectMarkers`, NOT wired into `BinContigs`; see [[meta-bin-001-markerqc-evidence]]); INV unique BinId / metrics [0,100] / GC [0,1] / TotalLength=Œ£ / disjoint partition / Coverage=mean; M5 50.0 / M6 0-100 / M7 1.0-0.0 / M12 25 oracles; opt-in TETRA z-score signature (`CalculateTetranucleotideZScores`/`TetranucleotideZScoreCorrelation`) ‚Äî RC-extended strand, 256-word Markov expectation `E=N(n1n2n3)¬∑N(n2n3n4)/N(n2n3)`, Schbath variance, Pearson correlation of z-vectors (scale-invariant), z(ACGT)=‚àö5 for ACGTACGTGGCC, N(n2n3)=0/non-positive-var‚Üíz=0; Maguire 2020 limits (plasmids 1-29%/GIs 38-44% poorly recovered), similar-GC+coverage‚Üíco-bin; three prior assumptions resolved, deviations None; record [[meta-bin-001-evidence]]; Metagenomics-family sibling of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]].
- [[taxonomic-classification]] ‚Äî Metagenomics family taxonomic-classification unit (fourth META-* unit, META-CLASS-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.ClassifyReads` + `BuildKmerDatabase` + `TaxonomyTree.Lca`): faithful Kraken (Wood & Salzberg 2014) per-read/contig assignment ‚Äî canonical-k-mer (`min(kmer,revcomp)`, default k=31) database mapping each k-mer to the **LCA of all owning reference taxa**, per-read **classification tree** (hit taxa + ancestors weighted by k-mer count) scored over **root-to-leaf (RTL)** paths ‚Üí assigned taxon = max-scoring path's leaf, equal-max ‚Üí LCA of leaves, no k-mer hits ‚Üí **Unclassified** (taxonomy root, C=0); Confidence = **C/Q** (Kraken 2: C = clade k-mers under assigned label, Q = non-ambiguous k-mers queried); ambiguous (non-ACGT) k-mers skipped/not in Q, upper-cased, semicolon/pipe taxonomy strings; invariants |out|=|in| / 0‚â§C/Q‚â§1 / C‚â§Q / Q=len‚àík+1 (all-ACGT) / canonical uniqueness / DB-build LCA / LCA siblings‚Üíparent, ancestor/descendant‚Üíancestor, self‚Üíself, disjoint‚Üíroot; empty/short-<k/no-match ‚Üí Unclassified, empty DB ‚Üí all Unclassified; scoped to **per-read classification** (abundance *profiling* Taxonomic_Profile is a separate later unit); research-grade, no deviations / no open questions; siblings [[metagenomic-binning]] (per-contig MAGs) & [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]] (consume the abundance profile); record [[meta-class-001-evidence]].
- [[beta-diversity]] ‚Äî Metagenomics diversity family between-sample unit (second META-* unit, META-BETA-001): between-sample dissimilarity from two taxon‚Üíabundance maps (`MetagenomicsAnalyzer.CalculateBetaDiversity` ‚Üí `BetaDiversity` record) ‚Äî Bray-Curtis BC=1‚àí2¬∑Œ£min(N_ij,N_ik)/Œ£(N_ij+N_ik) (abundance-sensitive, range [0,1], NOT a true metric) + Jaccard distance J=1‚àí|A‚à©B|/|A‚à™B| (presence/absence via abundance>0, true distance metric); Whittaker 1960 Œ±/Œ≤/Œ≥ (beta=turnover), Bray & Curtis 1957, Jaccard 1901; single union-pass O(u), no BC normalization (caller-scaled), +SharedSpecies/UniqueToSample1/2 counts; identical‚Üí0/0, disjoint‚Üí1/1, both-empty‚Üí0/0 & one-empty‚Üí1 guards; fish-tank BC 13/33 & J 1/3, symmetry BC 3/5 & J 2/3 oracles; one accepted deviation = UniFracDistance placeholder 0 (no phylo tree); within-sample sibling [[alpha-diversity]]; ecological-Jaccard shares the index math but not domain with sequence [[kmer-jaccard-similarity]].
- [[functional-prediction]] ‚Äî Metagenomics family functional-prediction unit (fifth META-* unit, META-FUNC-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.PredictFunctions` + `FindPathwayEnrichment`): predicts a community's *functional* capability (PICRUSt / KO-pathway style) in two exact-numeric pieces ‚Äî (A) homology-based annotation transfer: exact-signature `string.Contains` hit scored by BLOSUM62 self-score S, bit `S'=(ŒªS‚àílnK)/ln2` and E-value `E=K¬∑m¬∑n¬∑e^(‚àíŒªS)=m¬∑n¬∑2^(‚àíS')` (ungapped BLOSUM62 Œª=0.3176/K=0.134, Altschul/`blast_stat.c`), best hit = lowest E-value / highest bit (INV-01..03,06); (B) hypergeometric pathway ORA `P(X‚â•x)=1‚àíŒ£ C(M,i)C(N‚àíM,n‚àíi)/C(N,n)` in log-Gamma space, background=union-of-pathways default + query unioned in, sorted ascending, p‚àà[0,1], x/M/n=0‚Üíp=1 (INV-04,05); oracles WWW‚ÜíS'18.0202932787533/E 3.3852730346546e‚àí5 + N8000/M400/n100/x20‚Üí7.88e‚àí8; *Simplified* ‚Äî exact substring not gapped alignment (ASM-01, divergent homologs missed), no gapped Œª/K / composition stats / HMM / FDR; asks "what can they do" vs the "who is there" of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[metagenomic-binning]] and the diversity of [[alpha-diversity]]/[[beta-diversity]]; BLAST significance distinct from percent-id [[alignment-statistics]]; ORA half owned by [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] (the dedicated META-PATHWAY-001 unit); record [[meta-func-001-evidence]].
- [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] ‚Äî Metagenomics family pathway-enrichment unit (META-PATHWAY-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindPathwayEnrichment` / `HypergeometricUpperTail`): the GO::TermFinder / clusterProfiler over-representation statistic ‚Äî score each pathway by the hypergeometric **right-tail** `P(X‚â•x)=1‚àíŒ£_{i=0}^{x‚àí1}C(M,i)C(N‚àíM,n‚àíi)/C(N,n)` (N=background, M=pathway size, n=query, x=overlap; sampling without replacement, upper tail only), `phyper(x‚àí1,M,N‚àíM,n,lower.tail=FALSE)` reference (the q=x‚àí1 shift gives P(X‚â•x)); log-Gamma summation to N=8000, p‚àà[0,1], pathways sorted ascending; p=1 when x/M/n=0, **M‚Üîn symmetry**, without-replacement feasibility drops C(¬∑,¬∑)=0 terms; background = explicit `backgroundGenes` else union-of-pathway-members default (query always unioned in), members intersected with background; **no BH/Bonferroni FDR** correction; Boyle 2004 + PNNL ORA ¬ß8.2 sources, oracles 7.88e‚àí8 + 1/252 + 5/6 + 251/252; one caller-overridable background-defaulting assumption; **owns** the ORA machinery that [[functional-prediction]] uses as component B; generic statistic (GO/proteomics), research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-pathway-001-evidence]].
- [[taxonomic-profile]] ‚Äî Metagenomics family community-abundance profiling unit (sixth META-* unit, META-PROF-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.GenerateTaxonomicProfile`): the **aggregation/estimation** step downstream of per-read [[taxonomic-classification]] ‚Äî takes an `IEnumerable<TaxonomicClassification>` and returns a `TaxonomicProfile` with **relative-abundance maps at four ranks** (kingdom/phylum/genus/species, abundance = count(taxon)/Œ£count(classified)), **inline species-level diversity** (Shannon H=‚àíŒ£p·µ¢ln(p·µ¢) in nats + Simpson concentration Œª=Œ£p·µ¢¬≤), and **read counts** (TotalReads/ClassifiedReads); Unclassified excluded from denominators, empty rank strings filtered, per-rank Œ£‚âà1.0; invariants ClassifiedReads‚â§TotalReads / ClassifiedReads=Œ£(counts any rank) / Shannon‚â•0 / 0‚â§Simpson‚â§1; oracles Shannon=ln(3) (3 uniform), Simpson=0.375 ([2,1,1]); empty‚Üí0/0/empty & single taxon‚Üí1.0/H0/Œª1 (vs empty‚ÜíŒª0); count-based tally (NOT MetaPhlAn marker-coverage, no genome-size correction), inherits upstream classifier accuracy; the profiling unit [[taxonomic-classification]] deliberately deferred, sibling of [[alpha-diversity]] (richer six-index within-sample summary) / [[beta-diversity]]; MetaPhlAn/Segata 2012, research-grade, no contradictions; record [[meta-prof-001-evidence]].
- [[antibiotic-resistance-gene-detection]] ‚Äî Metagenomics family AMR gene-detection unit (seventh META-* unit, META-RESIST-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.FindAntibioticResistanceGenes`): ResFinder-style screen of assembled contigs against a **caller-supplied** resistance-gene reference DB, reporting the single **best-matching gene per contig** ‚Äî `BestUngappedMatch` slides each reference across the contig (offsets ‚àí(m‚àí1)..n‚àí1, overhanging both ends), keeps the max-match window (tie‚Üíshorter/higher-identity), then identity=matches/w (BLAST gapless, Heng Li 2018) & coverage=w/m (fraction of **reference** length, so contig-edge/split genes still scored), reported iff identity‚â•idThreshold AND coverage‚â•covThreshold; best match = max identity, tie‚Üímax coverage (Zankari 2012 "best-matching gene", CARD RGI best-hit); INV-01..05, defaults 0.90 ID / 0.60 cov (named constants), Perfect=1.0/1.0 (CARD); oracles CGTACGT@AAACGTACGT‚Üí1.0/1.0, CGTTCGT vs CGTACGT‚Üí6/7‚âà0.857/1.0, edge CGTA‚Üí1.0 / 4‚ÅÑ7‚âà0.571; *Simplified* ‚Äî gapless ungapped (ASM-01, indel matches under-scored vs gapped BLAST; substitution + edge-truncation exact), no SNP/protein-homology (CARD variant/homolog models out of scope), nucleotide-only case-sensitive, legacy `FindResistanceGenes` motif stub separate; asks "**which known resistance genes are present**" vs the who/what/how-diverse of [[taxonomic-classification]]/[[functional-prediction]]/[[alpha-diversity]]; BLAST-style homology screen sharing machinery with [[functional-prediction]] but scoring nucleotide identity/coverage not BLOSUM62 bit-score (identity denominator = [[alignment-statistics]] rule); provenance note flagged (evidence 0.80/0.98 vs impl 0.90 default); record [[meta-resist-001-evidence]].
- [[significant-taxa-detection]] ‚Äî Metagenomics family differential-abundance unit (eighth META-* unit, META-TAXA-001, `MetagenomicsAnalyzer.MannWhitneyU` / `FindSignificantTaxa`): per-taxon **two-group Mann‚ÄìWhitney U (Wilcoxon rank-sum)** test asking "which taxa differ in abundance between two groups?" ‚Äî non-parametric, rank-based, suits compositional/zero-inflated data (Xia & Sun 2017). Pool‚Üímidranks (tied values averaged, accumulate Œ£(t¬≥‚àít))‚Üí`U1=R1‚àín1(n1+1)/2`, `U2=n1¬∑n2‚àíU1`; `m_U=n1¬∑n2/2`, tie-corrected `œÉ_U=sqrt(n1¬∑n2¬∑(n1+n2+1)/12 ‚àí n1¬∑n2¬∑Œ£(t¬≥‚àít)/(12n(n‚àí1)))`; `z=(|U‚àím_U|‚àícc)/œÉ_U` on `max(U1,U2)`, cc‚àà{0,0.5} (0.5 on by default = SciPy `use_continuity`); two-tailed `p=2¬∑(1‚àíŒ¶(z))` clamped [0,1], Œ¶ via `StatisticsHelper.NormalCDF` (A&S 7.1.26, ‚âà1e‚àí6 accuracy). `FindSignificantTaxa` runs it per taxon over label-defined ({1,2}) groups ‚Üí `SignificantTaxon` ascending by p. INV-01..06 (U1+U2=n1¬∑n2, 0‚â§U‚â§n1¬∑n2, p‚àà[0,1], Significant‚áîp<threshold, all-tied‚ÜíœÉ0‚Üíz0‚Üíp1, group-swap symmetric); oracles SciPy x[19,22,16,29,24]/y[20,11,17,12]‚ÜíU1=17/U2=3/œÉ=4.0825/z_cc=1.5922‚Üíp‚âà0.11135 (z_nocc=1.7146‚Üíp‚âà0.08641) + tortoise/hare U_T=11/U_H=25/sum=36; empty group‚ÜíArgumentException, absent taxon‚Üíabundance 0 (ASM-03); asymptotic-not-exact, no FDR (caller applies BH), ignores compositionality; **consumes** [[taxonomic-profile]] abundance vectors; distinct-by-**test** from the hypergeometric [[pathway-enrichment-ora]] and Fisher's-exact [[differentially-methylated-regions]]; siblings [[alpha-diversity]] / [[beta-diversity]]; record [[meta-taxa-001-evidence]].
- [[methylation-context-classification]] ‚Äî epigenetics family CpG/CHG/CHH context-classification unit (sixth/final EPIGEN-* unit, EPIGEN-METHYL-001): sequence-only trinucleotide classifier partitioning cytosines into CpG/CHG/CHH from the downstream base(s) ‚Äî distinct because it handles the *non-CpG* CHG/CHH contexts [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]] does not call from reads. Rule (Cornish-Bowden 1985 IUPAC H={A,C,T}="not G"): CpG‚ü∫b‚ÇÅ=G, CHG‚ü∫b‚ÇÅ‚ààH & b‚ÇÇ=G, CHH‚ü∫b‚ÇÅ‚ààH & b‚ÇÇ‚ààH; CpG/CHG symmetric, CHH asymmetric (Krueger-Andrews 2011). Three ops on `EpigeneticsAnalyzer`: `GetMethylationContext` (O(1), null when not a classifiable C), `FindMethylationSites` (O(n) scan ‚Üí one site/classifiable C, 0-based, sequence-only level=0/coverage=0 placeholder), `GenerateMethylationProfile` (shared with [[bisulfite-methylation-calling]], Schultz 2012 weighted Œ£(level¬∑cov)/Œ£cov, zero-coverage‚Üíunweighted-mean fallback); CGACAGCAA‚ÜíCpG@0/CHG@3/CHH@6 + weighted (8+2)/(10+10)=0.5 oracles; G-never-H (CGG‚ÜíCpG), terminal-CG-still-CpG, incomplete-trailing / non-ACGT unclassified; Lister 2009 realism (IMR90 99.98% CG vs H1 ES ~25% non-CG); single-strand only, no symmetric-strand pairing; two assumptions (level=0 placeholder, 0.5 MethylatedCpG count cutoff); no contradictions.
- [[rna-base-pairing]] ‚Äî MiRNA family anchor + shared RNA base-pairing primitive (first MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PAIR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): deciding **whether two RNA bases can pair** and building the antiparallel miRNA-mRNA duplex from that rule. `CanPair`‚ü∫{A-U,U-A,G-C,C-G,G-U,U-G} = Watson-Crick {A-U,G-C} (Agarwal 2015) + the single standard **G-U wobble** (Crick 1966); `IsWobblePair`‚ü∫{G-U,U-G}, wobble‚äÜpairable, wobble counted **separately** from matches (PMC4870184). `GetReverseComplement` = antiparallel RNA reverse complement for seed‚Üítarget motif (Lewis 2005; let-7a `GAGGUAG`‚Üí`CUACCUC`). `AlignMiRnaToTarget` pairs miRNA[i]‚Üîtarget[len‚àí1‚àíi] over the shorter overlap, ungapped, emitting `|`(WC)/`:`(wobble)/space(mismatch); counts sum to min(len), Gaps=0; ŒîG = **simplified** Turner-2004 stacking sum over consecutive paired runs (sign reliable ‚Äî fully-WC ‚â§0, all-mismatch ‚â•0 ‚Äî magnitude not). Oracles AAAA/UUUU‚Üí4 matches, GGGG/UUUU‚Üí4 wobbles, AAAA/AAAA‚Üí4 mismatches; DNA T‚ÜíU normalised, unknown base‚ÜíN never pairs, empty‚Üíempty duplex. The **shared** pairing rule RNA secondary-structure classification also uses; **not** target-site efficacy prediction (that is `FindTargetSites`/MIRNA-TARGET-001), and the A-opposite-position-1 preference is Argonaute recognition, not base pairing; record [[mirna-pair-001-evidence]].
- [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] ‚Äî MiRNA family precursor-hairpin unit (second MiRNA unit, MIRNA-PRECURSOR-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): finding stem-loop pre-miRNA precursors (~60-120 nt) from which Dicer excises the ~22 nt mature duplex. **Default heuristic** `FindPreMiRnaHairpins` counts uninterrupted complementary pairs ({A-U,G-C}+G-U wobble, [[rna-base-pairing]] primitive) from both ends inward ‚Üí accept iff stem ‚â•18 bp (Krol 2004) + loop 3-25 nt (Bartel 2004); extracts mature(5' arm)/star(3' arm), balanced dot-bracket, Turner-2004 ŒîG; **documented limitation** ‚Äî consecutive-pairing is stricter than real structure, rejects natural miRBase precursors (hsa-mir-21 16 end-pairs, let-7a-1 5, tests M18/M19). **Opt-in** `AssessHairpinByMfe`/`FindPreMiRnaHairpinsByMfe` fold with the RNA-STRUCT-001 Zuker‚ÄìStiegler engine and read the hairpin from the real MFE structure (single dominant hairpin/no multibranch + stem ‚â•16 (Ambros 2003) + loop 3-25 + MFEI ‚â•0.85 (Zhang 2006, AMFE=100¬∑|ŒîG¬∞|/n, MFEI=AMFE/GC%)) ‚Üí detects hsa-mir-21 (ŒîG¬∞ ‚àí35.13/MFEI 1.0037) & let-7a-1; rejects a stronger-ŒîG¬∞ multibranch 5S-rRNA-like on **structure**. **Opt-in** `PredictDroshaDicerCleavage` = published ruler (Drosha +11 bp basal junction/Han 2006, Dicer 22-nt 5'-count/Park 2011, RNase III 2-nt overhang/Lee 2003, CNNC 16-18 nt confidence flag/Auyeung 2013; hsa-miR-21-5p cross-check). **Opt-in** `ClassifyPreMiRna` = logistic regression over [ŒîG,AMFE,MFEI,GC,%paired], 13 public-domain miRBase positives vs Altschul-Erickson di-shuffle negatives (Bonnet 2004 convention), held-out AUC 1.0, no GPL miRDeep2 code; read-stacking miRDeep2 signal out of scope (needs reads); record [[mirna-precursor-001-evidence]].
- [[seed-sequence-analysis]] ‚Äî MiRNA family seed-extraction unit (third MiRNA unit, MIRNA-SEED-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`): **string-level** extraction and comparison of the mature-miRNA 5' seed ‚Äî the primary determinant of animal target recognition ‚Äî not binding prediction. `GetSeedSequence` returns positions **2-8** (7 nt, extended seed) via `Substring(1,7)` uppercase (casing only, **no** T‚ÜíU); `<8 nt`/null/empty ‚Üí `""`. `CreateMiRna(name, sequence)` normalises `ToUpperInvariant()`+`T‚ÜíU`, extracts the seed from the normalised sequence, stores `SeedSequence` + fixed **zero-based** `SeedStart=1`/`SeedEnd=7`. `CompareSeedRegions` = Hamming over the 7-nt seed (`Matches`+`Mismatches`=7, mismatches also count any length diff), `IsSameFamily` ‚ü∫ **exact seed-string equality**; empty seed ‚Üí zeroed result. **miRNA family = identical 2-8 seed** (let-7a/-7b/-7c-5p all `GAGGUAG` ‚Üí same family; miR-21-5p `AGCUUAU` differs); self‚Üí0 mismatches. Domain context: TargetScan site ladder 8mer/7mer-m8/7mer-A1/6mer over the 2-7-vs-2-8 distinction, but matching-to-target + site-class assignment is deferred to target-site prediction (MIRNA-TARGET-001, future); seed‚Üítarget motif reverse complement is owned by [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement`). **Intentionally simplified** ‚Äî exact-7-mer family equality (no isomiR/offset/noncanonical seeds, not a curated taxonomy); 2-7-vs-2-8 terminology collapse flagged, no source contradictions; record [[mirna-seed-001-evidence]].
- [[mirna-target-site-prediction]] ‚Äî MiRNA family target-site-prediction unit (fourth & **final** MiRNA unit, MIRNA-TARGET-001, `MiRnaAnalyzer`, **completes** the family): finding mRNA target sites for a miRNA and classifying the **Bartel/TargetScan hierarchy**. `FindTargetSites(mRna, miRna, minScore=0.5)` = two-pass, `T‚ÜíU`, 0-based-inclusive antiparallel scan for the seed reverse complement (`seedRC=revcomp(m‚ÇÇ‚Ä¶m‚Çà)`, 6mer core `seedRC[2..7]`): pass-1 upgrades 6mer-core hits to **8mer** (pos 2-8 + A opposite pos 1) / **7mer-m8** (2-8) / **7mer-A1** (2-7 + A1) / **6mer** (2-7); pass-2 finds **offset-6mer** (3-8) only where not overlapping a retained higher-priority site (INV-04). Heuristic `Score‚àà[0,1]` (base 1.0/0.52/0.32/0.15/0.10, +0.05 >10 matches, ‚àí0.01/mismatch) + heuristic `FreeEnergy` (sign-reliable) ‚Äî ranking aid, **not** calibrated repression. **Depends on** [[seed-sequence-analysis]] (the 2-8 seed determines targeting) + [[rna-base-pairing]] (`GetReverseComplement` motif + `AlignMiRnaToTarget` `|`/`:`/space duplex). **Opt-in `ScoreTargetSiteContextPlusPlus`** = source-fitted TargetScan **context++** (Agarwal 2015): per-site-type MLR, sum of `coeff√óscaledScore`, continuous features min-max scaled + indicators raw; realises Intercept/Local_AU/sRNA1/sRNA8/Site8/3P_score/Min_dist/Len_3UTR/Off6m, **computes** TA_3UTR=log10 N (`ComputeTa3Utr`, Garcia 2011) + SA (Turner-2004 McCaskill partition unpaired-prob) + PCT (Friedman Bls‚Üípublished sigmoid); SPS/Len_ORF/ORF8m/PCT-`b0..b3` caller-supplied (compiled TargetScan tables, not bundled) ‚Üí honest **partial** `ContextScorePartial` + `OmittedFeatures` (8mer let-7a all-G-flank partial CS = ‚àí0.7561913315126536). `Centered`/`Supplementary` enum members not emitted (accepted); bulged/centered/supplementary/noncanonical + isoforms out of scope; no contradictions; record [[mirna-target-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **notation layer** (RNA-DOTBRACKET-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): parse an extended-**WUSS** structure string into base pairs `(i,j)` and validate well-formedness. `ParseDotBracket` uses **one stack per bracket family** ‚Äî `()`/`<>`/`{}`/`[]` + uppercase(5' open)/lowercase(3' close) letter pairs ‚Äî each an **independent pairing system** (ViennaRNA / Infernal `vrna_db_from_WUSS()`: any matched pair = a base pair, symbol has no meaning); a shared stack would mis-pair `([)]`. `ValidateDotBracket` ‚ü∫ every family's stack empty at end & never underflows; a closer must match a **same-family** opener. **Pseudoknots** (crossing families) are valid; `(]` (mismatched families) is not. Non-bracket WUSS symbols `-`/`,`/`:`/`.` are single-stranded (Rfam). Oracles `((((....))))`‚Üí4 pairs, `([)]`‚Üí(0,2)+(1,3), `<<<<[[[[....>>>>]]]]`‚â°`((((AAAA....))))aaaa`‚Üítwo crossing 4-bp helices; valid `(((...)))`/`(([[]]))`/`([)]`, invalid `(((...)` / `...)` / `)(` / `(]`. Notation-only (does not fold/score); distinct from the base-pairing chemistry [[rna-base-pairing]]; the structure the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] unit emits and the MFE folder reads. Two API-contract assumptions (malformed‚Üíbest-effort parse; empty/null‚Üívalid). Record [[rna-dotbracket-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **energy layer** (RNA-ENERGY-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the individual **Turner 2004 nearest-neighbor free-energy terms** summed into a fold's ŒîG¬∞ at 37 ¬∞C (`CalculateStackingEnergy`/`CalculateStemEnergy`/`CalculateHairpinLoopEnergy`/`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy`), all verified exact against **NNDB Turner04**. Model `ŒîG¬∞total = init + Œ£stacking + Œ£loops`. **WC stacking all negative**, GC-rich most stable (`GC/CG` ‚àí3.42, `GG/CC` ‚àí3.26; `AA/UU` ‚àí0.93); **G-U wobble variable** ‚Äî mostly negative but **two positive** (`UG/GU` +0.30, `GU/UG` +1.29), note-a `GG/UU`=‚àí0.5, **note-b special 3-stack** `5'GGUC/3'CUGG`=‚àí4.12 (vs ‚àí1.77). **Hairpin-loop initiation positive and NOT monotonic** (3‚Üí5.4, 4‚Üí5.6, 6‚Üí5.4, 8‚Üí5.5, 9‚Üí6.4; Jacobson-Stockmayer `ŒîG(n)=ŒîG(9)+1.75RT¬∑ln(n/9)` beyond 9). **Special UNCG/GNRA tri/tetra/hexaloops** use NNDB total energies keyed by closing pair+loop (replace the model; GNRA>random). **All-C loop** penalty (3-nt +1.5, >3-nt 0.3n+1.6), terminal mismatch (96 entries), **+0.45 per-AU/GU-end**. A single base pair contributes **0** stacking (needs ‚â•2 adjacent); empty/poly-A‚Üí0. Oracles GC 3-bp stem ‚àí5.78, NNDB hairpin example-1 `GGGAUAAAUCCC` ‚àí3.42, GGUC/CUGG ‚àí4.12. The **energy** the folding units consume (pre-miRNA `FreeEnergy`, RNA-STRUCT-001 MFE), assigned to [[rna-base-pairing]] pairs, distinct from the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] notation. No contradictions; three defined conditions (37 ¬∞C, 2-dp, unknown stacks‚Üí0), not assumptions. Record [[rna-energy-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **folding/search layer** (RNA-MFE-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **Zuker‚ÄìStiegler dynamic-programming MFE folder** that searches structure space for the fold of lowest total free energy (`CalculateMinimumFreeEnergy` / `PredictStructure`). Loop decomposition (hairpin / stacking / bulge-interior / multibranch); DP matrices **C(i,j)=min(hairpin, interior/bulge over an inner pair, multiloop)** + multiloop **M** (‚â•1 component)/**M1** (exactly one) + exterior **F** (Ward 2017); **standard affine multiloop model ‚Üí O(n¬≥) time / O(n¬≤) space** ("simplest model is best"; logarithmic model would be O(n‚Å¥)). The unit that **consumes** the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] Turner-2004 terms (summing them over candidate structures) and **produces** a [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] structure; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles `CACAAAAAAAUGUG`‚Üí`((((......))))` ‚àí1.41 (NNDB Example 1), `CACAGAAAGUGUG` ‚àí1.91 (Example 2). Invariants MFE ‚â§ 0 (INV-01, empty structure always available), suffix-monotone `MFE(s) ‚â§ MFE(prefix)` (INV-02), optimized DP == classic O(n¬≥) baseline (INV-03); empty/null / unfoldable homopolymer / sequence `< minLoopSize+2` ‚Üí 0 (hairpin loop ‚â• 3 nt); intramolecular ‚áí no helix-init constant. The folder the [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] opt-in `AssessHairpinByMfe` path uses (once generically called *RNA-STRUCT-001* before that artifact was ingested ‚Äî RNA-STRUCT-001 is now the **distinct sibling** Nussinov predictor [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]], sharing this unit's Zuker MFE machinery). Two documented simplifications (multiloop per-unpaired `c=0`; 2-dp rounding), no source contradictions; sources Zuker & Stiegler 1981 + Lorenz 2011 (ViennaRNA) + Ward 2017 + NNDB Turner 2004 + Mathews 2004. Record [[rna-mfe-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **probabilistic/ensemble layer** (RNA-PARTITION-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): the **McCaskill 1990** partition function ‚Äî the Boltzmann-weighted counterpart of MFE folding that computes the equilibrium `Z = Œ£_P exp(‚àíE(P)/RT)` over all pseudoknot-free structures plus per-base-pair binding probabilities and the Boltzmann probability of a given structure, in **O(n¬≥) time / O(n¬≤) space**. Inside recursion `Q_ij = Q_{i,j-1} + Œ£_{i‚â§k<j-m} Q_{i,k-1}¬∑Q^b_{kj}` (base `Q_ij=1` for i‚â•j‚àím), total **`Z = Q_{1n}`** (disjoint/unambiguous decomposition); pair probability needs the **outside** recursion `p_kl = Q^b_kl¬∑O_kl/Z` ‚Äî the external-only term is **wrong for nestable pairs** (`GGGAAACCC` P(2,6)=6/20 not 1/20; outside matches Boltzmann brute force to 3.3e-16). Oracles (E_bp=0 ‚áí Z counts structures) `AAAA`‚Üí1, `GC`‚Üí1, `GGGGCCCC`‚Üí16, `GGGAAACCC`‚Üí20; invariants Z ‚â• 1 (empty structure weight 1), P(i,j) ‚àà [0,1] + symmetric, per-base pairing sum ‚â§ 1, monotone in E_bp; WC + GU pairing only, min-loop forbids j‚àík ‚â§ m. The **`alternative_to` / ensemble counterpart** of the single-optimum [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] MFE folder; Boltzmann-weights the [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] energies (ViennaRNA default 37 ¬∞C = Turner standard); builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. One simplification (fixed-per-pair `E_bp` energy model vs full Turner NN ‚Äî energy model only, invariants conformant with McCaskill 1990), no source contradictions. Record [[rna-partition-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **crossing-helix layer** (RNA-PKPREDICT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict the optimal fold that may contain a single **canonical H-type pseudoknot** ‚Äî two helices whose pairs **cross** (`i<k<j<l`), the one feature the nested [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] and [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill|McCaskill ensemble]] cannot represent. **pknotsRG class** (Reeder & Giegerich 2004): "two crossing helices with three intervening loops", H-type 5'‚Üí3' stem1-5'‚Üíloop1‚Üístem2-5'‚Üíloop2‚Üístem1-3'‚Üíloop3‚Üístem2-3', two-layer dot-bracket `((((..[[[[..))))..]]]]`; full grammar **O(n‚Å¥)/O(n¬≤)**. Canonization rules (equal-length bulge-free helices / maximal extent / fixed overlap boundary) bound the search. Energy = Turner NN stacking on **both** helices (same model as nested, `Energy.lhs`) + penalties **initiation 9.0** (anti-spurious-knot gate ‚Äî a knot is reported only when it beats both the penalty and the best nested alternative) / **unpaired loop nt 0.3** / **base pair inside knot 0.0** kcal/mol. **Depends on** [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] (helix scoring) and [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] (MFE fallback baseline `FreeEnergy ‚â§ CalculateMfeStructure().FreeEnergy` + folds internal loops); emits two-layer [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]; builds on [[rna-base-pairing]]. Oracles designed H-type `GGGGAACCCCAACCCCAAGGGG`‚Üíknot with two crossing 4-bp helices; plain `GGGGAAAACCCC`‚Üíno knot = MFE; BWYV `GGCGCGGCACCGUCCGCGGAACAAACGG` (PDB 437D) **not** recovered (tertiary-stabilized, outside NN model ‚Äî documented limit of all NN-only pseudoknot predictors). Two boundaries: PARTIAL pknotsRG coverage (single H-type only; recursive/over-arching/multiple knots not implemented) + tertiary-stabilized knots not recovered. No contradictions. Record [[rna-pkpredict-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **crossing detection layer** (RNA-PSEUDOKNOT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure.DetectPseudoknots`): given a **set of base pairs** describing a known structure, a pure **O(n¬≤) combinatorial scan** finds every **crossing** pair-of-pairs `i<k<j<l` (Antczak 2018) ‚Äî one pair's opener inside the other while its closer lies outside. Two exhaustive negatives: **nested** `i<k<l<j` (one pair fully inside) and **disjoint** `j<k` (side-by-side). Each crossing pair-of-pairs = one pseudoknot (binary relation); ‚â•2 pairs required, endpoints normalized min-max to open<close, deterministic. Oracles `([)]`=(0,2)+(1,3)‚Üíone, nested (0,5)+(1,4)‚Üínone, disjoint (0,2)+(3,5)‚Üínone. The **detection/analysis facet** ‚Äî genuinely distinct from the energy-driven [[rna-pseudoknot-prediction]] predictor (input = pair set vs sequence, machinery = combinatorial scan vs Turner-NN energy DP, cost = O(n¬≤) vs O(n‚Å¥)) ‚Äî and the crossing primitive that predictor's validity invariant leans on. Operates on the pairs the [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]] parser emits; complements the nested-only [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding]] / [[rna-partition-function-mccaskill]]. One scope note: pseudoknot-**order** assignment (Antczak DBL layering / Smit 2008 removal) Not Implemented. Sources Antczak 2018 + Smit & Knight 2008 + biotite + Wikipedia, no contradictions. Record [[rna-pseudoknot-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-stem-loop-enumeration]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **enumeration layer** (RNA-STEMLOOP-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): **scan a sequence for every stem-loop (hairpin)** it can form under size constraints ‚Äî `FindStemLoops(sequence, minStem, minLoop, maxLoop, allowWobble)` / `FindHairpins`, extending an antiparallel WC/wobble stem outward around each candidate loop, **O(n¬≤¬∑L)**. The general, sequence-agnostic hairpin *finder* ‚Äî distinct from the single-optimal-fold [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (O(n¬≥) DP), the hairpin *energy* unit [[rna-hairpin-001-evidence]], and the miRNA-specific [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]] precursor detector. Loop **‚â•3 nt** (steric floor, shared with the MFE/Turner units), optimal **4-8 nt**. **Tetraloops** ‚Äî GNRA / UNCG / CUUG, UUCG the most stable, UUCG+GNRA ~70% of 16S-rRNA tetraloops, ~3.0 kcal/mol bonus via [[rna-free-energy-turner-model|Turner 2004]]. `FindPseudoknots` shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing primitive with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]]. Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], emits [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]]. Invariants non-overlap / ‚â§1 pair per base / contiguous loop / antiparallel stem; limitations no PK-from-sequence, simplified energy, hairpin loops only, single structure. Record [[rna-stemloop-001-evidence]].
- [[rna-secondary-structure-prediction]] ‚Äî RNA secondary-structure family **top-level prediction umbrella** (RNA-STRUCT-001, `RnaSecondaryStructure`): predict a structure from a sequence by a **Nussinov base-pair-maximizing** DP ‚Äî `Predict` / `PredictWithConstraints` (forced pairs, Mathews 2004) / `ToDotBracket` / `FromDotBracket`. Nussinov & Jacobson 1980 O(n¬≥)/O(n¬≤) maximizes the **(weighted) base-pair count** (WC ‚àí2.0 / wobble ‚àí1.0), signalling **relative stability, not physical energy units** ‚Äî the **`alternative_to`** the physical Turner-kcal/mol [[rna-minimum-free-energy-folding|MFE folder]] (RNA-MFE-001), same problem / different objective. A **distinct sibling** test unit, **not an alias** of RNA-MFE-001: both share the `RnaSecondaryStructure` Zuker MFE machinery (this unit's D5 added `CalculateMfeStructure`/`PredictStructureMfe`). Builds on [[rna-base-pairing]], converts to/from [[rna-dot-bracket-notation]], consumes [[rna-free-energy-turner-model]] stem-loop terms, shares the `i<k<j<l` crossing test with [[rna-pseudoknot-detection]] (detects, never predicts, pseudoknots). Oracles `GGGGAAAACCCC`‚Üí`((((....))))`, poly-A‚ÜíMFE 0; min loop 3 nt (steric), single-sequence only, int21/int22 lookup tables blocked. Record [[rna-struct-001-evidence]].
- [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]] ‚Äî Oncology family anchor (first ONCO-* unit, ONCO-ACTION-001): **clinical actionability assessment** by the OncoKB Therapeutic Levels of Evidence (Chakravarty 2017). A **pure ranking** ‚Äî given a variant's caller-supplied leveled drug associations, return the **maximum** level under the fixed combined order `R1 > 1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4 > R2` (sensitivity axis `1 > 2 > 3A > 3B > 4`, resistance axis `R1 > R2`), the two axes reported separately (a variant may carry both); no leveled association ‚Üí **NotActionable**. Seven tiers: 1 (FDA in-indication) / 2 (NCCN in-indication) / 3A (clinical evidence in-indication) / 3B (another indication) / 4 (biological evidence) / R1 (standard resistance) / R2 (investigational resistance); 1/2/R1 = standard vs 3A/3B/4/R2 = investigational (SOP v3, consistent with AMP/ASCO/CAP Li 2017). **Knowledgebase is a caller input** ‚Äî the library ranks, it does not embed/annotate the OncoKB DB; NotActionable-name is the library's; not for clinical use; record [[onco-action-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] ‚Äî Oncology family, second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ANNOT-001): **cancer variant tier classification** by the **AMP/ASCO/CAP 2017 four-tier** consensus (Li MM et al. 2017). A **pure decision rule** over caller-supplied evidence level (A‚ÄìD) + population MAF + cancer-association flag ‚Üí **Tier I** (strong, Level A/B) / **II** (potential, Level C/D) / **III** (unknown, no level + rare + cancer assoc) / **IV** (benign, no level + MAF ‚â• 1% **or** no assoc). Population frequency is the **III‚ÜîIV discriminator**; **evidence level dominates frequency** (a significant biomarker stays Tier I at high MAF). 1% (0.01) is the guideline **primary benign cutoff**, inclusive (MAF 0.01 ‚Üí Tier IV). `AnnotateCancerVariants` = one annotation per variant in input order; `GetCOSMICAnnotation` = null-on-miss lookup against a **caller-supplied** COSMIC catalog (external DB, not embedded). Distinct from but **consistent with** the sibling OncoKB level-ranking [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; not for clinical use; record [[onco-annot-001-evidence]].
- [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] ‚Äî Oncology family, third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ARTIFACT-001): **sequencing artifact detection** (`FilterArtifacts`) ‚Äî the **QC** sibling that removes false-positive somatic calls from DNA damage / mapping bias **before** clinical interpretation (distinct from the two clinical-significance ONCO units). Three disjoint signals: **substitution class** (OxoG oxidation G>T/C>A per Chen 2017 vs FFPE cytosine-deamination C>T/G>A per Do & Dobrovic 2015; else not-an-artifact), the **GIV** read-pair imbalance ratio (`GIV_G_T = count(G>T in R1)/count(G>T in R2)`, neutral 1 / damaged > 1.5, Chen 2017 + Damage-estimator), and **FisherStrand** FS = ‚àí10¬∑log10(two-sided Fisher-exact p) on the `[ref_fwd,ref_rev,alt_fwd,alt_rev]` 2√ó2 table (GATK, FS ‚âà 0 no bias / high = artifact). Result ‚äÜ input; **no BAM parser** (per-strand/read-mate evidence supplied on the variant record); GIV thresholds from the Nature Methods summary; not for clinical use; record [[onco-artifact-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] ‚Äî Oncology family, fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-ASCAT-001): the **upstream tumor copy-number layer** ‚Äî allele-specific integer copy number (nA/nB) from per-locus **logR/BAF** by a joint **purity œÅ / ploidy œà** grid fit (**ASCAT**, Van Loo 2010: `nA/nB` inversion, minimise length-weighted squared minor-allele distance to non-negative integers, BAF=0.5 down-weighted √ó0.05, GoF = (1‚àíd/maxdist)¬∑100, **Œ≥=1 for sequencing**). Four disjoint stages: (1) ASCAT core (œÅ,œà) fit; (2) **ASPCF** penalised-least-squares joint segmentation `L=Œ£(y‚àí»≥)¬≤+Œ≥|S|` via O(n¬≤) DP (Nilsen 2012) with common change points + BAF mirroring (Ross 2021); (3) **subclonal** two-state mixture `n_obs=f¬∑n‚ÇÅ+(1‚àíf)¬∑n‚ÇÇ` over bracketing integers (Battenberg / Nik-Zainal 2012); (4) **multiplicity/CCF** VAF inversion `VAF=(m¬∑CCF¬∑p)/(c¬∑p+2(1‚àíp))`, clamp m to [1,major-CN] (McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / DeCiFering). Planted-truth tests invert the forward model (œÅ‚ÇÄ=0.80, œà‚ÇÄ‚àà{2,3}). The allele-specific/clonal counterpart to the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; substrate beneath the clinical-interpretation ONCO siblings; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ascat-001-evidence]].
- [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] ‚Äî Oncology family, fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CCF-001): the **downstream clonal-structure layer** ‚Äî estimate each mutation's **cancer cell fraction** `CCF = f¬∑(œÅ¬∑N_T+2(1‚àíœÅ))/(œÅ¬∑m)` (`EstimateCCF`; McGranahan 2016 / PICTograph / Tarabichi 2021, corroborated three ways; m ‚àà [1,tumor CN], œÅ ‚àà (0,1]) with a reported-value **[0,1] cap** that exposes the uncapped raw (the raw formula can exceed 1 ‚Äî CNAqc 1.06 noise case), then **`ClusterCCFValues`** deconvolutes the CCF vector into clones/subclones by a **deterministic 1D Lloyd k-means** (Lloyd 1982, quantile seeding, no RNG) with **highest-centroid = clonal** (Tarabichi 2021). Consumes the purity œÅ / copy number N_T / multiplicity m from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (whose ¬ß4 carries the same CCF closed form); two source-consistent assumptions ([0,1] cap; Lloyd k-means as the concrete 1D method); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ccf-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] ‚Äî Oncology family, sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CHIP-001): the **pre-interpretation biological-origin filter** for liquid biopsy ‚Äî removes **clonal-hematopoiesis (CHIP)** false positives, the dominant cfDNA confounder (Razavi 2019: 81.6% controls / 53.2% cancer). `IdentifyCHIPVariants` flags a driver-gene variant ({DNMT3A,TET2,ASXL1,TP53,JAK2,SF3B1,SRSF2,PPM1D}, top-3 DNMT3A/TET2/ASXL1) at **VAF ‚â• 0.02** (Steensma 2015 / Genovese 2014); `FilterCHIP` removes CH calls by **matched-WBC subtraction** (present in matched WBC ‚áí blood-derived, the definitive origin test, Razavi 2019) plus a **conservative labelled gene+VAF heuristic fallback** (over-removes; strict mode = empty gene panel); `CallVariantOrigin` = the strict **Bolton 2020** rule (WBC VAF ‚â• 2% AND ‚â• 10 reads AND ‚â• œÜ√ó tumour VAF, œÜ=2.0 / 1.5 lymph node). The **biological-origin sibling** of the technical-artifact QC filter [[sequencing-artifact-detection]], upstream of the clinical-interpretation and clonal-structure ONCO units; two source-consistent assumptions (canonical default gene set, ‚â•1-alt-read WBC presence test); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-chip-001-evidence]].
- [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]] ‚Äî Oncology family, seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CLONAL-001): the **probabilistic clonal-structure classifier** ‚Äî per-mutation **Bayesian CCF posterior** `P(c) ‚àù Binom(a|N,f(c))` (uniform prior, 100-point grid `c‚àà[0.01,1]`) with expected allele fraction `f(c) = Œ±Mc/(2(1‚àíŒ±)+Œ±q)` (Landau 2013 ABSOLUTE-style; multiplicity M generalisation, Satas 2021 DeCiFering Eq. 1), classified **clonal iff `P(CCF>0.95) > 0.5`** (two distinct thresholds: 0.95 CCF cut, 0.5 posterior-mass cut) via `ClassifyClonality(variants, purity)`, plus the point-estimate `IdentifyClonalMutations` (strict CCF > 0.95, boundary excluded ‚Üí indices {0,2,4}). The **`alternative_to`** the point-estimate + Lloyd-k-means [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] ‚Äî same clonal/subclonal question, but classifies each mutation on its own read-count uncertainty without clustering; consumes purity Œ± / local copy number q / multiplicity M from the upstream [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]]; one API-shape assumption (per-variant local copy number q over a genome-wide ploidy scalar); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-clonal-001-evidence]].
- [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] ‚Äî Oncology family, eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-001): the **total-copy-number classification layer** ‚Äî a single **log2 copy ratio** ‚Üí absolute integer CN `n = 2¬∑2^log2` (CNVkit `_log2_ratio_to_absolute_pure`, diploid ref_copies=2) ‚Üí discrete **CNA state** via CNVkit's `absolute_threshold` hard-threshold caller (default `‚àí1.1/‚àí0.25/0.2/0.7` ‚Üí DeepDeletion/Loss/Neutral/Gain/Amplification; CN = index of the **first** threshold with `log2 <= thresh`, **boundary-inclusive ‚Üí lower bin**; above the last ‚Üí `ceil(2¬∑2^log2)` open-ended Amplification; NaN ‚Üí neutral CN 2), corroborated by **GISTIC2** (Mermel 2011: ¬±0.1 noise band subsumed by the neutral bin + +0.848/‚àí0.737 high-amplitude cutoffs). The **total-CN** counterpart to the allele-specific [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] and the per-segment oncology-state sibling of the whole-chromosome [[aneuploidy-detection]] (both share the `n = 2¬∑2^log2` conversion); distinct from SV-CNV-001's `round`-based integer CN (no state classification). One diploid-ploidy=2 assumption; threshold-variant note (docs germline `‚àí0.4/0.3` vs code tumor `‚àí0.25/0.2`); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-001-evidence]].
- [[focal-amplification-detection]] ‚Äî Oncology family, ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-002): the **focal-amplification layer** ‚Äî a two-part predicate `DetectFocalAmplifications` keeps segments both **amplified** (log2 gain > GISTIC2 `t_amp` 0.1) **and** **focal** (SegLen / ArmLength < `broad_len_cutoff` 0.98 ‚Äî Mermel 2011's length-based, not amplitude-based, focal-vs-arm-level split; strict `< 0.98`, exactly 0.98 ‚Üí arm-level), then `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes` maps each focal amplification's arm prefix to a built-in oncogene panel (17q‚ÜíERBB2 ¬∑ 8q‚ÜíMYC ¬∑ 7p‚ÜíEGFR ¬∑ 11q‚ÜíCCND1 ¬∑ 12q‚ÜíMDM2 **and** CDK4, NCBI Gene cytobands). Orthogonal to the log2‚Üí5-state [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) ‚Äî a **length** question, not an amplitude bin ‚Äî sharing only the GISTIC2 `t_amp`=0.1 amplitude gate. Sources GISTIC2 Mermel 2011 + GISTIC2 docs (`broad_len_cutoff`/`t_amp`) + CNVkit (single-copy gain log2 0.585 > 0.1) + NCBI Gene. Worked oracles A 17q 0.50‚ÜíERBB2 / B 8q 0.99 arm-level / C 7p log2 0.05 not-amplified / D 11q 0.98 boundary. Two assumptions (amplitude+length fusion; caller-supplied arm label + length, no cytoband table); deletions out of scope (ONCO-CNA-003); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-002-evidence]].
- [[homozygous-deletion-detection]] ‚Äî Oncology family, tenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CNA-003): the **deep-deletion layer**, the **deletion mirror of ONCO-CNA-002** ‚Äî filter segments whose classified integer copy number is **exactly 0** (a homozygous / deep deletion: cBioPortal `‚àí2` "Deep Deletion", Cheng et al. 2017 "zero copies of both alleles" / two hits; **reuses** [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 = `DeepDeletion` call, **no new threshold**), then `IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` maps each arm prefix to a built-in tumour-suppressor panel (17p‚ÜíTP53 ¬∑ 13q‚ÜíRB1 **and** BRCA2 ¬∑ 9p‚ÜíCDKN2A ¬∑ 10q‚ÜíPTEN ¬∑ 17q‚ÜíBRCA1, NCBI Gene cytobands). A single-copy loss (`‚àí1`, heterozygous, CN ‚â• 1) is NOT a homozygous deletion. The loss-side counterpart of the amplification unit [[focal-amplification-detection]] (`IdentifyDeletedTumorSuppressors` mirrors `IdentifyAmplifiedOncogenes`) and a consumer of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]]'s CN-0 state. Two assumptions (CN-0 reuse, caller-fixed panel); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-cna-003-evidence]].
- [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] ‚Äî Oncology family, eleventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-CTDNA-001): the liquid-biopsy **quantification / limit-of-detection** layer for **circulating tumor DNA (ctDNA)** ‚Äî the Poisson detection probability `DetectionProbability` **p = 1 ‚àí e^(‚àín¬∑d¬∑k)** (n genome equivalents, d mutant allele fraction, k reporters; Patent US 11,085,084 restating Avanzini 2020, corroborated by Pessoa 2023's Œª = n¬∑d = 15) with a detectability test (caller threshold default 0.95 **and** Œª = n¬∑d¬∑k ‚â• 1; only p is non-assumption), **`CalculateTumorFraction` = 2 √ó mean clonal-heterozygous VAF** (copy-neutral diploid, CNAqc/Antonello 2024 v = œÄ/2), `CalculateMeanVaf` = mean altReads/totalReads across reporters (Newman 2014 CAPP-Seq across-reporter fraction, detection 0.025%‚Äì10%), and a genome-equivalents helper (3.3 pg/haploid, Devonshire 2014 ‚áí ‚âà303 GE/ng, Alcaide 2020). The **quantification counterpart** on the same cfDNA input as the biological-origin filter [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] (measures signal vs filters it), sharing the diploid-heterozygous VAF inversion with [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] / [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]; underpins MRD monitoring; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ctdna-001-evidence]].
- [[driver-gene-classification-20-20-rule]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twelfth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-DRIVER-001): the **gene-level** driver classifier ‚Äî the Vogelstein 2013 **20/20 rule** classifying a cancer gene **Oncogene** (> 20% missense at **recurrent** positions, ‚â• 2√ó = activating), **TumorSuppressor** (> 20% **truncating / inactivating** ‚Äî nonsense / frameshift / splice donor-acceptor / stop gain-loss = loss of function), or **Ambiguous** (neither criterion, or exact dual-pass tie), via `IdentifyDriverMutations` (driver ‚äÜ somatic) + `MatchCancerHotspots` (caller-supplied (gene, position) hotspot set) + `ScoreDriverPotential` (= max of the two criterion fractions in [0,1]; CADD/SIFT/PolyPhen are caller-supplied, not implemented). Oracles: IDH1 10 missense@codon 132 ‚Üí recurrent-missense 1.00 ‚Üí Oncogene; dispersed 8/10 truncating ‚Üí 0.80 ‚Üí TumorSuppressor; truncating exactly 0.20 ‚Üí NOT TSG (strict `>`). A **heuristic, not a statistical test** (passenger truncations / low-recurrence drivers mislead it; 20/20+ / MutSigCV successors out of scope), **orthogonal** to the variant-level clinical classifiers [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] and [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. Three assumptions (strict `> 0.20`, dual-pass tie-break by larger fraction with Ambiguous on tie, ScoreDriverPotential proxy); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-driver-001-evidence]].
- [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-EXPR-001), and the wiki's **first expression/transcriptome method**: the per-gene **outlier z-score** `z = (r ‚àí Œº)/œÉ` against a caller-supplied **reference (base) population** (cBioPortal's diploid or all-samples convention) with **œÉ = sample SD, divisor (n ‚àí 1)** (settled by `NormalizeExpressionLevels.java`), classified over/under-expressed under the **strict ¬±2** default threshold (exactly ¬±2 is NOT an outlier), plus the **combined-z signature/pathway activity** `a = (Œ£·µ¢ z·µ¢)/‚àök` (Lee et al. 2008, the GSVA `zscore` method). Zero-SD reference **throws** (reference-code `fatalError`, a behavioural deviation from the prose "z ‚Üê NA" spec ‚Äî the two cBioPortal sources disagree); reference `{2,2,4,6,6}` ‚Üí œÉ=2 so x=10‚Üí3.0 over / x=8‚Üí2.0 boundary-not-outlier / x=4‚Üí0.0 / x=‚àí1‚Üí‚àí2.5 under, signature `{3,1,‚àí1,1}`‚Üí2.0 & single-gene `{2.5}`‚Üí2.5 oracles. **Orthogonal** to the copy-number / clonal-structure ONCO units ([[copy-number-alteration-classification]], [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]]) ‚Äî the diploid reference option touches copy number only as an input filter. Two scope assumptions (caller-supplied cohort + signature; inputs pre-normalized) + one behavioural deviation (throw not NA); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-expr-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] ‚Äî Oncology family, fourteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-001), and the wiki's **first gene-fusion / read-evidence structural-rearrangement method**: the STAR-Fusion / Arriba **split-read + discordant-pair + minimum-support** candidate-fusion caller (BCR-ABL1 / EML4-ALK / TMPRSS2-ERG). **DETECTED** iff (junction ‚â• `MIN_JUNCTION_READS`=1 AND total ‚â• `MIN_SUM_FRAGS`=2) OR (zero junction AND discordant ‚â• `MIN_SPANNING_FRAGS_ONLY`=5), where **total support = split_reads1 + split_reads2 + discordant_mates** (Arriba) and the **gene5p ‚âÝ gene3p** distinct-gene invariant rejects self-fusions; results ordered by descending support (STAR-Fusion scores by "abundance of fusion-supporting reads"). Plus a standalone **exon-phase in-frame** check `(5' coding bases ‚àí 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (Genomics England / Wikipedia Reading-frame). Oracles: EML4-ALK(3,2,4)/TMPRSS2-ERG(1,0,1)/CD74-ROS1(0,0,5) DETECTED, NCOA4-RET(0,0,4) span<5 / KIF5B-RET(1,0,0) sum<2 / ALK-ALK same-gene REJECTED, frame 300/0‚Üíin 301/0‚Üíout 301/1‚Üíin. Consumes **already-grouped candidate breakpoint counts** (Arriba schema, not raw BAM ‚Äî chimeric-read extraction is a separate `FindChimericReads`) and does **not** scan for a premature stop before the junction (Arriba `stop-codon` value, ONCO-FUSION-003 scope). **Orthogonal** to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units, distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two scope assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] ‚Äî Oncology family, fifteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-002), the wiki's fusion **annotation/naming** method: the **HGNC gene-fusion designation** `GetFusionAnnotation(5p,3p) = "5p::3p"` (Bruford et al. 2021 ‚Äî `::` double-colon separator, **5‚Ä≤-partner-first** directional order irrespective of chromosomal location, HGNC approved symbols, read-throughs keep the hyphen `INS-IGF2`) plus the **directional known-fusion match** `MatchKnownFusions` against a **caller-supplied** set keyed by `5‚Ä≤::3‚Ä≤`, case-insensitive. A **Framework** algorithm ‚Äî format/keying source-backed (Bruford 2021 + consortium extension letter), set contents caller-supplied (no bundled Mitelman/COSMIC/ChimerDB). `BCR::ABL1` worked example; `A::B ‚âÝ B::A` reciprocal-direction and hyphen ‚âÝ `::` corner cases; null/empty rejected. The **naming layer downstream** of the read-evidence caller [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] (annotation round-trips through a `DetectFusions` `FusionCall`), distinct from the ONCO-FUSION-003 premature-stop scope; orthogonal to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. Two assumptions (caller-supplied set, case-insensitivity); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-002-evidence]].
- [[fusion-breakpoint-frame-and-protein-prediction]] ‚Äî Oncology family, sixteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-FUSION-003), the **protein-consequence** third member of the fusion trio: given a fusion breakpoint it computes the **four-state** `BreakpointFrameStatus` (`InFrame`/`OutOfFrame`/`StopCodon`/`NotPredicted`) and reconstructs the **fusion protein**. Follows **Arriba's two-way** native-frame model (Uhrig 2021 `reading_frame`/`site` columns) ‚Äî the in/out call is whether the 3‚Ä≤ gene is read in its NATIVE frame via the exon-phase rule `(5' coding bases ‚àí 3' start phase) mod 3 == 0` (reused from [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] ONCO-FUSION-001) ‚Äî deliberately **not** AGFusion's three-way class (`in-frame (with mutation)`, contiguous ORF multiple-of-3 but 3‚Ä≤ frameshifted, maps to **`OutOfFrame`**). Gated by breakpoint-site classification: a breakpoint in UTR/intron/non-coding-exon/intergenic ‚Üí `NotPredicted`. `PredictFusionProtein` follows AGFusion `model.py` exactly: 5‚Ä≤ CDS prefix + 3‚Ä≤ CDS suffix ‚Üí concatenate ‚Üí translate (transl_table=1) ‚Üí **truncate at first stop** (out-of-frame trims to whole codons first). Oracles `ATGAAA|GATGGT`‚Üí`MKDG`, `ATGAAA|GATTAAGGT`‚Üí`MKD` (in-frame premature stop), `ATGA|AAGGT` phase-0‚Üí`OutOfFrame` yet clean `MKG` (the Arriba-vs-AGFusion divergence point) / phase-1‚Üíin-frame, `ATGAA|GATGGT`‚Üítrim-to-9 `MKM`. Downstream of ONCO-FUSION-001 (elaborates its binary in-frame check into a full consequence + transcript/peptide reconstruction, the premature-stop scope both siblings deferred here), orthogonal to the naming unit [[gene-fusion-nomenclature-known-fusion-lookup]] and to the copy-number/clonal and clinical-interpretation ONCO units. One API-shape assumption (caller supplies CDS strings + junction offsets, no bundled GTF); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-fusion-003-evidence]].
- [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] ‚Äî Oncology family, seventeenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HETERO-001): the **scalar-summary ITH-metric layer** that reduces the reconstructed clonal structure to comparable numbers ‚Äî the **MATH score** `100¬∑1.4826¬∑median(|VAF‚àímedian VAF|)/median(VAF)` (Mroz & Rocco 2013 / Mroz 2015 / maftools `mathScore.R`, three-way identical; the ratio of the width to the centre of the mutant-allele-fraction distribution, no clustering needed), the **Shannon clonal diversity** `H = ‚àíŒ£ p·µ¢ ln p·µ¢` (natural log, Liu 2017 / Shannon 1948), the **subclone count** (Liu richness = number of occupied CCF clusters), and the **subclonal fraction** `#(CCF<0.95)/n` (Landau 2013 threshold). MATH oracles 49.42 (odd) / 59.304 (even); Shannon 0 / ln2 / ln4; zero-median-VAF‚Üíthrow, MAD=0‚ÜíMATH=0. **Depends on** [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (subclone count + Shannon p·µ¢ consume its CCF clusters) and reuses the 0.95 clonal threshold of [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]]; a summary layer, NOT per-mutation reconstruction; shares the Shannon-index math but not the domain with [[alpha-diversity]]. Two source-consistent assumptions (Shannon p·µ¢ = per-cluster mutation proportions; R even-count median); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hetero-001-evidence]].
- [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] ‚Äî Oncology family, eighteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HLA-001), the wiki's **first HLA / immuno-oncology antigen-presentation method**: two disjoint pieces sharing the HLA locus ‚Äî (1) **HLA allele nomenclature parsing/validation** of the WHO IPD-IMGT/HLA name `HLA-[Gene]*[F1]:[F2][:F3][:F4][suffix]` (Marsh 2010 colon-delimited convention; Field1 type/allele-group / Field2 specific protein / Field3 synonymous / Field4 non-coding; **two-field "four-digit" minimum**, four-field maximum, `HLA-` prefix required, numeric fields, `N/L/S/C/A/Q` expression-suffix set ‚Äî `HLA-A*24:02:01:02L` valid, `HLA-A*02`/`A*02:01`/five-fields/`‚Ä¶X` rejected), and (2) **allele-specific HLA LOH** by the **LOHHLA** rule (McGranahan 2017 *Cell* / `mskcc/lohhla`): per-allele copy number from tumor-vs-germline logR + BAF, call HLA LOH iff min copy number **< 0.5** AND allelic-imbalance paired Student's t-test **p < 0.01** ‚Äî both strict `<`, the p-test the explicit "avoid over-calling LOH" guard; oracles (1.8, 0.30, 0.001)‚ÜíLOH allele 2 / (1.60, 0.40, 0.05)‚Üíno (p‚â•0.01) / (1.50, 0.50, 0.001)‚Üíno (0.5 not <0.5) / (1.70, 0.40, 0.01)‚Üíno (0.01 not <0.01); the **HLA-locus specialization** of the genome-wide allele-specific copy-number / LOH derivation [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (same logR + BAF allelic-contrast idea restricted to the HLA genes), a mechanism of immune escape via lost neoantigen presentation; one assumption (both alleles <0.5 ‚Üí distinct `HomozygousLoss` label, thresholds unchanged); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hla-001-evidence]].
- [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] ‚Äî Oncology family, nineteenth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-HRD-001): the **HRD composite genomic-scar score** `HRD = LOH + TAI + LST`, an **unweighted sum** of three large-scale copy-number scar counts with the **HRD-high cutoff ‚â• 42** inclusive (Telli 2016 + Stewart 2022, independently corroborated). All three components **derived per segment** from the [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] major/minor CN substrate in `DetectHRD(segments)`: **HRD-LOH** = LOH regions > 15 Mb & < whole chromosome, excluding whole-chr-LOH chromosomes (Abkevich 2012 / oncoscanR / scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`, no centromere table needed); **TAI** = imbalanced (major ‚âÝ minor CN) segments reaching a sub-telomere but not crossing the centromere (Birkbak 2012 / scarHRD `calc.ai_new.R`, sub-1 Mb dropped, single-segment whole-chr imbalance excluded); **LST** = adjacent ‚â• 10 Mb same-arm regions separated by < 3 Mb after iterative 3 Mb smoothing (Popova 2012 / scarHRD `calc.lst.R`, autosomes only). TAI + LST need the per-chromosome centromere `[start,end]` **acen** table embedded for GRCh38/GRCh37 (UCSC cytoBand cross-verified vs NCBI GRC ‚Äî resolving the prior "centromere table unretrievable" blocker). Oracles (14,14,14)‚Üí42 HRD-high / (14,13,14)‚Üí41 negative / (0,0,0)‚Üí0. The genomic-scar aggregation layer above [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], distinct from the total-CN [[aneuploidy-detection]]; one even-ploidy AI-path assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-hrd-001-evidence]].
- [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twentieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-IMMUNE-001), the wiki's **second expression/transcriptome method**: **immune infiltration estimation** ‚Äî quantifies the tumor immune microenvironment two ways. (1) **Cell-type deconvolution** of the linear mixture `m = S¬∑f` (Œ£f=1, f‚â•0): CIBERSORT **ŒΩ-SVR** `DeconvoluteImmuneCellsNuSvr` (Newman 2015 / Sch√∂lkopf 2000 linear-kernel ŒΩ-SVR ‚Äî z-standardize m + signature columns, sweep ŒΩ‚àà{0.25,0.5,0.75} by **lowest RMSE**, zero-clip negatives + normalize to Œ£=1; cross-validated by planted-truth `m=S¬∑f` recovery + scikit-learn `NuSVR`/libsvm match) with the NNLS/LLSR baseline `DeconvoluteImmuneCells` (Abbas 2009) retained. (2) **ESTIMATE** ssGSEA immune/stromal enrichment `EstimateInfiltration` (**simplified** = rank-weighted mean of signature genes, not full KS running-sum) + opt-in **tumor purity** `EstimateTumorPurity` = `cos(0.6049872018 + 0.0001467884¬∑ESTIMATE)` (verbatim, confirmed 3 sources + tidyestimate R; **Affymetrix-only** calibration, negative cosine ‚Üí **NaN**, monotone-decreasing). MCP-counter geometric-mean marker abundance noted. Signature matrices: **LM22** (547 genes √ó 22 cell types) **caller-supplied** ‚Äî Stanford licence forbids redistribution/modification/commercial use, no exact-CIBERSORT parity claim, `LoadSignatureMatrix` LM22-format loader only; **ABIS-Seq** (Monaco 2019, CC BY 4.0, 1296 genes √ó 17 types) **bundled** as embedded resource via `LoadBundledAbisSignatureMatrix` so deconvolution works out-of-the-box (not an LM22 substitute); synthetic 5-marker `DefaultSignatureMatrix` for tests. Oracles: planted {CD8 0.60,B_naive 0.30,Mono 0.10}‚Üí{0.5971,0.2989,0.1040} corr 0.99997; sklearn cross-check ŒΩ=0.75 {A 0.5085,B 0.1795,C 0.3120}; ABIS {NK 0.60,MonoC 0.40}‚Üí{‚âà0.650,‚âà0.350} corr 0.996 (tol 0.06) & pure MonoC 1.0 exactly; ABIS ref `CD8A`/T CD8 Mem=1060.1507652944399. Corner cases: collinear cell types (resting/activated NK) recover support but looser proportions; missing/non-overlapping genes ‚Üí unreliable/zero; non-hematopoietic content in residual; ESTIMATE solid-tumors-only. Antigen-agnostic quantitative sibling of the immuno-oncology [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]], shares the ssGSEA signature-scoring layer with [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]]; two scope assumptions (LM22 caller-supplied, simplified ssGSEA) + Affymetrix purity domain, no contradictions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-immune-001-evidence]].
- [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-LOH-001): the standalone genome-wide **LOH caller** ‚Äî `DetectLOH` counts **HRD-LOH** regions (minor CN 0 **and** major CN ‚âÝ 0 = allelic loss not homozygous deletion; length **strictly > 15 Mb**, length = end ‚àí start; excluding any **whole-chromosome** global-LOH chromosome via `chrDel`) and `CalculateLOHFraction` returns the length-weighted per-chromosome LOH fraction ‚àà [0,1]. Abkevich 2012 (intermediate-size LOH ‚Üî BRCA1/2 deficiency) + scarHRD `calc.hrd.R`/`scar_score.R` (exact R criterion + 15 Mb cut-off + `chrDel`; major CN capped to 1 so LOH state, not absolute CN, drives merging) + oncoscanR `score_loh` (independent corroboration; adjacent/overlapping LOH merged ‚â§ 1 bp first). Synthetic 7-segment dataset ‚Üí score **1** (only the 20 Mb chr1 segment; exactly-15 Mb / het-retained / homozygous-deletion / whole-chr-LOH all excluded); LOH-fraction 0.333/0.0/1.0. This **is** the LOH term the composite [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] sums with TAI + LST (centromere-free, unlike its siblings), reads its segments off [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]], and is the genome-wide counterpart of the HLA-locus [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (LOHHLA). Two assumptions (segment input shape; length-weighted LOH-fraction is a definitional/API choice); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-loh-001-evidence]].
- [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MHC-001): the wiki's first **MHC / peptide-presentation prediction** method ‚Äî the affinity gate of neoantigen candidate scoring, three layers over one `Strong`/`Weak`/`NonBinder` output. (1) **Classification**: IC50 tiers `< 50` Strong / `< 500` Weak / `‚â• 500` NonBinder (Sette 1994 ‚âà 500 nM CTL threshold + IEDB) and NetMHCpan-4.1 %Rank tiers (class I SB `< 0.5` / WB `< 2`, class II `< 2` / `< 10`, all strict `<`; Reynisson 2020), + peptide-length validity (class I **8‚Äì14**, class II 13‚Äì25). (2) **Matrix prediction**: BIMAS **product rule** (T¬Ω = const ¬∑ ‚àè coeffs, 180 coeffs + const, unlisted = 1.0; Parker 1994) and SMM **additive** rule `IC50 = 50000^(1‚àíscore)` (Peters & Sette 2005 / IEDB log50k; 0‚Üí50000, 0.5‚Üí223.6068, 1‚Üí1 nM). (3) Ported **MHCflurry 2.0** pan-allele class-I NN (BLOSUM62 `left_pad_centered_right_pad` 45√ó21 peptide + 37-residue allele pseudosequence 37√ó21, `tanh` Dense `feedforward`/`with-skip-connections`, `to_ic50 = 50000^(1‚àíx)`, geometric-mean ensemble; matches `mhcflurry` 2.1.5 to < 0.03 %). **Framework/packaging** ‚Äî trained matrices caller-supplied (BIMAS CGI defunct / Parker paywalled / IEDB non-commercial) and 80 MB ensemble not embedded (one member for CI + `LoadWeightPack`), explicitly analogized in-file to CIBERSORT LM22 of [[immune-infiltration-deconvolution]]. Downstream of neoantigen generation [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] (ONCO-NEO-001), presentation-machinery sibling of [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the platform); class I 8‚Äì14 resolved vs NetMHCpan-4.1; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mhc-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-informed-mrd-detection]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MRD-001): the liquid-biopsy **MRD calling / statistical-detection** layer that `depends_on` and reuses the Poisson quantification primitive [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] (ONCO-CTDNA-001). Two engines. (1) **Signatera positivity** (`DetectMRD`): tumor-informed workflow ‚Äî up to 16 WES-selected clonal somatic SNVs tracked in plasma cfDNA ‚Äî **MRD-positive iff ‚â• 2 of the 16 tracked variants are detected** (Reinert 2019 / PMC9265001 Table 1; 0/1‚Üínegative, 2/3‚Üípositive), panel Poisson `p = 1 ‚àí e^(‚àínfm)`, sensitivity scales with panel size (>8 markers at ‚â§0.1% VAF, LoD 0.01% / specificity >99.5%; post-op ctDNA+ ‚Üí HR 7.2 relapse), longitudinal `TrackVariantsOverTime` (per-timepoint + first-positive). (2) **INVAR GLRT** (Wan 2020 + INVAR2 verbatim): per-locus mixture `q = p¬∑g + e(1‚àíp)`, EM ctDNA-fraction, `LR = logL(pÃÇ) ‚àí logL(0)` (pure background ‚Üí pÃÇ‚âà0/LR‚âà0; AF/SNR-weighted, monotone), `IntegratedMutantAlleleFractionV2` background-subtracted depth-weighted, fragment-size-weighted GLRT (`EstimateInvarSignalWithSize`/`FragmentSizeProfile`/`InvarMolecule`; discrete `COUNT/TOTAL` default + opt-in Gaussian-KDE `FromKernelDensity`; flat P1==P0 ‚Üí reduces to no-size), outlier suppression `SuppressOutlierLoci` (repolish binomial + Bonferroni), control-derived background `EstimateLocusBackground`/`PassesBothStrandsFilter`. Distinct from ONCO-CTDNA-001 (multi-variant verdict vs single-reporter probability); one flagged per-variant "detected"=‚â•1 alt read assumption (tunable); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-mrd-001-evidence]].
- [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-MSI-001): the **microsatellite-instability biomarker** ‚Äî MSI from unstable-loci fraction + status classification. Two inputs, two classifiers. (1) **Continuous MSI score** = `unstable loci / valid loci` (as %) with **MSI-High cutoff ‚â• 20%** inclusive (MSIsensor2 niu-lab README verbatim; per-site **chi-square** tumor-vs-normal repeat-length test at **FDR 0.05**, score = "% sites with a somatic indel", Niu 2014; tumor-only mode unchanged; the original cohort's **3.5%** separation is dataset-specific, not the production cutoff) ‚Üí classified **binary** MSI-H (‚â•20%) vs not-High only. (2) **Categorical Bethesda** marker-count over the validated 5-marker panel (BAT-25/BAT-26/D2S123/D5S346/D17S250): **0/5‚ÜíMSS ¬∑ 1/5‚ÜíMSI-L ¬∑ ‚â•2/5‚ÜíMSI-H** (Boland 1998, cross-checked vs the 2004 revised-Bethesda ‚â•40% / ‚â•20%&<40% fraction form BJC 2014). Key modelling choice: **no MSI-L band is fabricated for the continuous score** ‚Äî the three-way MSS/MSI-L/MSI-H scheme applies only to the discrete marker count. Oracles 5/25‚Üí20%‚ÜíMSI-H(boundary) ¬∑ 4/25‚Üí16%‚Üínot-High ¬∑ 0/25‚Üí0%‚ÜíMSS-range; corner cases zero-valid-loci‚Üíundefined(throws) ¬∑ unstable>valid/negative‚Üíthrows ¬∑ MSS-vs-MSI-L 1-marker low-confidence. An independent immunotherapy/mismatch-repair biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]], consumed by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-msi-001-evidence]].
- [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-NEO-001): the **upstream partner** of the affinity gate [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] ‚Äî **neoantigen candidate peptide window generation** (`GenerateNeoantigenPeptides`). Given a somatic **missense SNV** at 1-based position `p` in a protein of length `L`, enumerate **every length-`k` window of the mutant protein that spans the mutated residue** (valid 0-based start `s ‚àà [max(0, p‚àí1‚àík+1), min(p‚àí1, L‚àík)]`, count `= last ‚àí first + 1`; an interior mutation gives exactly `k` windows per length), each paired with its matched **wild-type (germline)** peptide at the same coordinates + the mutation offset ‚Äî the mutant/WT **agretope** on which the differential agretopic index (DAI, Wells 2020 TESLA) is computed. Class I search lengths **8‚Äì11** (pVACtools Hundal 2020; a 21-mer with the substitution centred = ProGeo-neo Li 2020's ¬±10-flank construction contains exactly every overlapping 8‚Äì11-mer; NetMHCpan 8‚Äì14 / 9-mer-dominant Jurtz 2017 motivates enumerating 8‚Äì11 not 9 alone). Oracles: interior **Y5C** on `MKTAYIAKQRSTVWLNDEFGH` ‚Üí 5 windows per k = 8/9/10/11 ‚Üí **20** candidates (each WT = mutant with `C`‚Üí`Y` at the offset); **terminal M1V** k = 9 ‚Üí exactly 1 truncated window `VKTAYIAKQ`/`MKTAYIAKQ` offset 0; corner cases non-coding/synonymous ‚Üí no peptide, length outside 8‚Äì11 not enumerated, short-protein skips that `k`. **Missense-only** (frameshift/indel/fusion neopeptides out of scope, separate translation) and **binding affinity out of scope** (IC50/%Rank scoring caller-supplied via the downstream [[mhc-peptide-binding-prediction]] ONCO-MHC-001 gate, whose resolved class I 8‚Äì14 window propagates to this generator's default); presentation-platform sibling [[hla-nomenclature-and-allele-specific-loh]] (HLA LOH removes the restricted allele). Two source-backed scoping assumptions; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-neo-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PHYLO-001): the **clonal-tree reconstruction** layer ‚Äî assemble per-cluster **cancer cell fractions (CCF)** into a rooted **clonal-evolution tree**, deciding parent‚Üíchild descent via two per-sample CCF-ordering constraints from **LICHeE** (Popic 2015) and **PICTograph** (Zheng 2022): **lineage precedence** (ancestor CCF ‚â• descendant CCF ‚àí Œµ per sample, + presence pattern `u.CCF=0 ‚áí v.CCF=0`; LICHeE Eq. 2) and the **sum rule** (children CCF sum ‚â§ parent CCF + Œµ per node ‚Äî the cell-fraction **pigeonhole generalization**; LICHeE Eq. 5 / PICTograph sum condition ‚Äî what forces **branching vs nesting**), plus **trunk** (CCF-‚âà1 root-path clusters = clonal) vs **branch** (subclones) identification. A **constraint-satisfaction / perfect-phylogeny** builder, **not** distance-based Neighbor-Joining / UPGMA. Oracles: linear Normal‚ÜíA‚ÜíB‚ÜíC (1.0/1.0/0.6/0.3, Trunk {A}); two-sample branching A‚Üí{B,C} (B 0.6/0.0, C 0.0/0.7 ‚Äî each private, absent in the other's sample, so mutually non-ancestral; sum under A per sample 0.6 & 0.7 ‚â§ 1.0); equal 0.6/0.6 siblings forced into a chain Normal‚ÜíA‚ÜíB‚ÜíC by the sum rule (0.6+0.6=1.2 > 1.0). Two reconstructed-tree **invariants** as oracles (ancestor CCF ‚â• descendant per edge; per-node sum rule); empty‚Üíroot-only, single cluster‚Üítrunk. **Downstream of** the CCF clustering [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] (ONCO-CCF-001, which produces the clusters it orders), the structural counterpart of the per-mutation trunk‚Üîclonal / branch‚Üîsubclonal [[clonal-subclonal-classification-ccf-posterior]], and the structure the heterogeneity metrics [[intratumor-heterogeneity-metrics]] summarize. Two source-consistent assumptions (deepest-valid-ancestor deterministic tie-break; default Œµ=0 strict inequalities); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-phylo-001-evidence]].
