- [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-seventh ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PLOIDY-001): two **post-hoc genome-state summaries** over already-called allele-specific segments (shared `AlleleSpecificSegment` = Major+Minor CN, not raw logR/BAF): (1) **average ploidy** `EstimatePloidy` = length-weighted mean total CN **œà = Œ£(CN_i¬∑L_i)/Œ£(L_i)** (Patchwork PMC4053982; n-scale Van Loo 2010, pure diploid ‚Üí 2.0, >2.7n aneuploidy; CN 2/4/3 at 100/100/50 Mb ‚Üí 3.0, genuinely length-weighted not plain segment mean); (2) **whole-genome doubling** `DetectWholeGenomeDoubling` = facets-suite `is_genome_doubled` / Bielski 2018 rule ‚Äî WGD iff **autosome-restricted fraction at major CN ‚â• 2 strictly > 0.5** (`mcn = tcn ‚àí lcn`; major not total CN, so all-1:1 ‚Üí not doubled), denominator = **reference chromosome-size table** (`ReferenceGenome {GRCh38,GRCh37}`, UCSC hg38/hg19 Ensembl-verified, Œ£chr1‚Äì22 = 2,875,001,522 / 2,881,033,286 bp) NOT supplied segments, autosomes only (sex chromosomes excluded); half+1‚Üítrue / exactly-half‚Üífalse (strict) / 100 Mb amp‚Üí0.035 false / chrX-only‚Üífalse oracles, legacy `DetectWholeGenomeDoublingFromSuppliedLength` keeps the supplied-length denominator (60%‚Üítrue/50%‚Üífalse). **Distinct from** the joint grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 *fits* œÅ/œà from raw logR/BAF; this *summarizes* œà post-segmentation), reads the same segment substrate as [[loss-of-heterozygosity-detection]] / [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]]. Two assumptions (input shape; resolved reference-genome WGD denominator); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-ploidy-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-eighth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-PURITY-001): a **standalone closed-form tumor-purity estimator** that inverts the **CNAqc expected-VAF generative model** `v = m¬∑œÄ¬∑c/[2(1‚àíœÄ)+œÄ(n_A+n_B)]` (Antonello 2024) to recover purity œÄ from a somatic-SNV VAF + local allele-specific copy number: `EstimatePurityFromVAF` = the copy-neutral diploid heterozygous special case **œÄ = 2¬∑VAF** (clonal c=1, het m=1, n_tot=2; VAF 0.30‚Üí0.60, band 0.55‚Äì0.65‚ÜîVAF 0.275‚Äì0.325, invariant 0‚â§œÄ‚â§1) and `EstimatePurity` = the general inversion `œÄ = 2v/(m¬∑c + 2v ‚àí v¬∑n_tot)` recovering œÄ=1 on a 2:1 (n_tot=3) segment for both m=1 (v=1/3) and m=2 (v=2/3). The `2(1‚àíœÄ)+œÄ¬∑n_tot` denominator (normal diploid weighted 1‚àíœÄ + tumour) is confirmed by **FACETS** (Shen & Seshan 2016) and inverted the other way by **ABSOLUTE** (Carter 2012). Corner cases: multiplicity ambiguity on amplified segments (two VAF peaks 1/3, 2/3 ‚Äî need CN state + m), subclonal c<1 depresses VAF (use **clonal** mutations or underestimate purity), purity <0.1 below detection, no informative variants ‚Üí undefined. **`alternative_to`** the joint logR/BAF grid fit [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] (ONCO-ASCAT-001 ‚Äî same purity scalar, different substrate + method), mutation-VAF counterpart to the ploidy-side [[tumor-ploidy-estimation-and-whole-genome-doubling]], shares the diploid `œÄ=2¬∑VAF` inversion with [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]]. Two modelling-scope assumptions (copy-neutral-diploid default, median cross-variant aggregation); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-purity-001-evidence]].
- [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] ‚Äî Oncology family, twenty-ninth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-001): the wiki's first **mutational-signature** method ‚Äî the **SBS-96 trinucleotide context catalog**, the classification step that builds the 96-channel single-base-substitution spectrum downstream signature fitting decomposes. A **channel** = a substitution + its centred trinucleotide context: **6** subtypes named by the **pyrimidine** of the mutated Watson‚ÄìCrick pair (`C>A/C>G/C>T/T>A/T>C/T>G`) **√ó 4** 5‚Ä≤ bases **√ó 4** 3‚Ä≤ bases = **96**, labelled `5'[REF>ALT]3'` (COSMIC SBS96 + SigProfilerMatrixGenerator Bergstrom 2019 + Alexandrov 2013, identical 6√ó4√ó4 definition). The defining rule is **pyrimidine-strand folding**: a **purine (A/G) reference** base is reverse-complemented (context via A‚ÜîT/C‚ÜîG then reverse, plus the substitution) onto the pyrimidine strand before counting; a C/T reference classifies to itself, centre unchanged. Worked fold TGA/G‚ÜíT ‚Üí revcomp TCA + G>T‚ÜíC>A ‚Üí `T[C>A]A`; oracles A,C,A,A‚ÜíA[C>A]A ¬∑ G,T,C,A‚ÜíG[T>C]A ¬∑ A,A,T,A‚ÜíT[T>A]T. Catalog **partition** invariants: exactly 96 canonical keys, Œ£ per-channel counts = number of classifiable SBS variants. Corner cases: purine-ref must fold (never counted directly), non-SBS variants (indels/DBS) excluded, non-ACGT context unclassifiable, ref==alt out of scope. **Catalog/classification only** ‚Äî the NMF/NNLS signature-exposure fitting against COSMIC reference signatures is a separate downstream concern. A somatic-mutation-spectrum biomarker orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and the mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; one cosmetic label-rendering assumption; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-001-evidence]].
- [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirtieth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-002): the **downstream signature-deconvolution** partner of the catalog [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] (which it `depends_on`) ‚Äî decompose the 96-channel SBS spectrum into **signatures √ó exposures** two ways. **Supervised refit** by **non-negative least squares** `min_x ‚ÄñS¬∑x‚àíd‚Äñ‚ÇÇ¬≤, x‚â•0` (MutationalPatterns/deconstructSigs; Lawson-Hanson active-set ‚Äî clamp any would-be-negative coefficient to 0 and refit, S=[[1,1],[0,1]], d=[0,1]‚Üíx=[0,0.5]; reconstruction `S¬∑x`, **cosine ‚â• 0.95** quality gate, raw counts + proportion `x/Œ£x` exposures). **Unsupervised de-novo extraction** by **NMF** `V ‚âà WH` (Lee & Seung multiplicative updates, **Frobenius** default + **KL/Poisson** enhancement, both **monotonically non-increasing**; Alexandrov blind-source-separation W=signatures/H=exposures; COSMIC **L1-normalize** each W column to 1). Shared **cosine similarity** `A¬∑B/(‚ÄñA‚Äñ‚ÄñB‚Äñ)‚àà[0,1]` (identical‚Üí1, orthogonal‚Üí0, [1,1]/[1,0]‚Üí1/‚àö2, scale-invariant, **zero-norm‚Üí0.0** by convention). **Rank selection** = Brunet-2004 **cophenetic correlation** (consensus of argmax-over-H connectivity matrices; rank-1 trivially 1.0) + SigProfiler **silhouette stability**; **reference matching** = greedy best-cosine to COSMIC. Sharp edges: NMF **non-convex ‚Üí local minimum** (planted-truth + fixed-seed recovery only), **permutation/scale ambiguity**, Œµ-guarded denominators. The NNLS refit and NMF extraction are `alternative_to` each other over the same `V ‚âà WH` model; the fitted exposure profile feeds the clinical-interpretation ONCO units, orthogonal to [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] / [[microsatellite-instability-detection]]; five modelling assumptions (Frobenius, seeded init, proportions, zero-cosine, consensus/silhouette/greedy matching); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-002-evidence]].
- [[signature-exposure-bootstrap-confidence-intervals]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirty-first ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-003): the **signature-exposure uncertainty** layer over the NNLS refit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) ‚Äî a **resample ‚Üí refit ‚Üí percentile** loop that turns the point-estimate exposure vector into a **per-signature confidence interval**. Resample the 96-channel catalog `R` times (default 1000; sigminer ‚â•100), re-run the ONCO-SIG-002 **NNLS** `FitSignatures` per replicate, and report the **[2.5%, 97.5%] percentiles** (Efron 1979 percentile CI) read off the finite bootstrap sample by the **type-7** quantile (Hyndman & Fan 1996, `h=p¬∑(n‚àí1)`, R/NumPy default). **Two resampling schemes** differing only by whether total burden N is fixed: **multinomial** (sigminer `sample(...,prob=catalog/Œ£)` = fixed-N multinomial(N,p), the byte-for-byte **default**) vs **Poisson** (Senkin 2021 MSA variant, each channel `Poisson(observed‚Çñ)`, N unfixed, justified by the Poisson‚Üîmultinomial conditional equivalence). The **discriminating** corner case is a single non-zero channel: multinomial **collapses deterministically** (width 0, point=mean=lower=upper) while **Poisson(Œª>0) fluctuates** (variance=mean ‚Üí positive width ‚Äî the reason the Poisson variant was added); plus N=0‚Üí[0,0] and R=1‚Üílower=upper=mean. Invariants Lower‚â§Mean‚â§Upper, exposures ‚â•0 (NNLS), fixed-seed determinism; type-7 oracles [0,1,2,3,4]‚Üí0.1/2.0/3.9 and [2,4,6,8]‚Üí2.15/5.0/7.85. The uncertainty layer two steps above the [[sbs96-mutational-signature-catalog]] spectrum; two source-aligned assumptions (type-7 interpolation, fixed seed 42); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-003-evidence]].
- [[mutational-process-classification]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirty-second ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SIG-004): the **aetiology-annotation** layer over the fit [[mutational-signature-fitting-and-extraction]] (which it `depends_on`) ‚Äî turn per-signature **exposures** into a set of **active mutational processes** via **normalize ‚Üí cutoff ‚Üí map ‚Üí aggregate**. Normalize to relative contributions `W·µ¢ = exposure·µ¢/Œ£exposure` (deconstructSigs "weights between 0 and 1"); drop any `W·µ¢ < 0.06` (the deconstructSigs `signature.cutoff = 0.06` / `weights[weights < signature.cutoff] <- 0`, **strict `<`** so exactly 0.06 is retained, empirically 1.4% false-negative rate); map each surviving COSMIC label to its **proposed aetiology** (SBS1/5‚Üí**Aging** clock-like, SBS2/13‚Üí**APOBEC**, SBS4‚Üí**Tobacco**, SBS7a‚Äìd‚Üí**UV**, SBS6/15/20/26‚Üí**MMR deficiency**; COSMIC + Alexandrov 2020); **sum** member contributions per process ‚Üí **active-process set** + `argmax` **dominant process**. Worked oracle SBS2/13/1/4 = 50/30/15/5 (Œ£=100) ‚Üí APOBEC 0.80 (dominant) / Aging 0.15 / Tobacco 0 (SBS4 0.05 below cutoff). Corner cases: surviving mass can sum < 1 (rest "unknown"), several processes reported simultaneously, an unmapped or "Unknown"-aetiology label contributes to no process (SBS5's aetiology is literally "Unknown (clock-like)" yet grouped as Aging), Œ£=0 ‚Üí no active/dominant process, custom `signature.cutoff` overridable. The interpretation layer answering "**which processes are active?**" one step above ONCO-SIG-002's "how much of each signature?" and ONCO-SIG-003's "how confident?"; orthogonal to the copy-number-scar [[homologous-recombination-deficiency-score]] and mismatch-repair [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (whose MMR signal SBS6/15/20/26 echo here as a signature-based read), feeds [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]; two source-aligned assumptions (per-process summation, per-signature-cutoff-then-group); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sig-004-evidence]].
- [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirty-third ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SOMATIC-001): the **foundational somatic SNV caller** at the head of the pipeline ‚Äî classify each candidate variant **Somatic / Germline / NotDetected** by comparing **tumor allele frequency `f_t`** against **matched-normal `f_n`** (`VAF = altReads/totalReads`). Strelka's somatic state `S = {(f_t,f_n): f_t‚âÝf_n}` restricted to a **ref/ref normal genotype** (Saunders 2012; the raw somatic probability over-calls in LOH/CN regions) / Strelka2 continuous-VAF somatic-LOD+VAF comparison (Kim 2018). **Three configurable thresholds**: tumor **LoD f_t ‚â• 0.05** (Yan 2021 WES 5% LoD, ‚â§5% frequently sequencing errors ‚Üí NotDetected), normal **"absent" ceiling f_n ‚â§ 0.01** (`normalVafThreshold`), f_n above ceiling with substantial f_t ‚Üí **Germline** (Mutect2 germline filter, Benjamin 2019). Bounded monotone **somatic score `max(0, f_t ‚àí f_n)` ‚àà [0,1]** (a documented simplification, not a caller LOD). **Tumor-only mode**: no matched normal ‚Üí Mutect2 `‚Ñì_n = 1`, tumor-only call; `FilterGermlineVariants` returns the somatic **subset** of input. Oracles A 0.25/0.00‚ÜíSomatic(0.25) ¬∑ B 0.48/0.50‚ÜíGermline(0) ¬∑ C 0.02‚ÜíNotDetected ¬∑ D CHIP-like 0.30/0.03‚ÜíGermline ¬∑ E tumor-only 0.20/(0/0)‚ÜíSomatic ¬∑ boundaries f_t=0.05 present / f_n=0.01 absent. The **upstream caller** whose raw call set the two pre-interpretation QC filters clean ‚Äî technical-artifact [[sequencing-artifact-detection]] + biological-origin [[clonal-hematopoiesis-cfdna-filtering]] ‚Äî before the clinical-significance units; two flagged source-consistent assumptions (1% normal ceiling parameterized not invented; score a documented simplification); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-somatic-001-evidence]].
- [[chromothripsis-inference]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirty-fourth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-SV-001), and the wiki's **first complex-rearrangement / chromothripsis** method: a **region-level pattern classifier** that consumes a per-segment integer copy-number profile (+ breakpoints / a clustered-SV count) and classifies **Chromothripsis** vs **NotComplex** by the **Korbel & Campbell 2013** six hallmark criteria, computing two directly ‚Äî criterion B **oscillating copy-number states** (an oscillation = an adjacent-segment CN-state reversal; profile must alternate between ‚â§3, canonically **two**, states) gated by the Magrangeas-2011 **‚â•10 first-pass oscillation screen**, the Cort√©s-Ciriano-2020 confidence tiers (**‚â•7** adjacent oscillating segments high / **4‚Äì6** low / **<4** not-called), the **>60%** two-state fraction, and the **‚â•6 clustered intrachromosomal SV** burden floor; and criterion A **breakpoint clustering** via the exponential-null coefficient-of-variation flag (**CV>1**, exponential CV=1). Oracles `2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2,1,2`‚Üí10 two-state‚ÜíChromothripsis ¬∑ `2,1,2,1,2,1`‚Üí5<10‚ÜíNotComplex ¬∑ `2,3,4,5,6,7` monotone‚Üí0 oscillations/>2 states‚ÜíNotComplex (progressive amplification/BFB ‚Äî the "clustering necessary but not sufficient" failure mode). **Consumes** the per-segment CN states of [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] (ONCO-CNA-001) ‚Äî a pattern classifier over that profile, not a per-segment caller ‚Äî orthogonal to the single-junction [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] and the length-based [[focal-amplification-detection]], distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]. Two operationalisation assumptions (oscillation = CN-state-transition count; clustering = CV>1 vs exponential null); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-sv-001-evidence]].
- [[tumor-mutational-burden]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirty-fifth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-TMB-001): the **tumor-agnostic immunotherapy biomarker** ‚Äî the continuous **TMB = (counted somatic mutations) / (sequenced coding region in Mb)** in mut/Mb (Chalmers 2017 Methods; the assay's **coding footprint** is the denominator ‚Äî FoundationOne 315-gene = **1.1 Mb**, F1CDx 324-gene ‚âà 0.8 Mb, WES ‚âà 30‚Äì40 Mb, taken as a parameter) and the **TMB-High = TMB ‚â• 10 mut/Mb** classification (FDA pembrolizumab tumor-agnostic approval June 16 2020, F1CDx companion diagnostic, Marcus 2021; boundary **inclusive** ‚Äî 10.0 High, 9.9 not; mut/Mb reporting + cutoff cross-confirmed by the Friends of Cancer Research Harmonization Project, Merino 2020). Panel counting **includes synonymous** alterations to reduce sampling noise while WES counts nonsynonymous; germline/driver filtering happens **upstream** ‚Äî this unit counts the caller-supplied somatic list of [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] (ONCO-SOMATIC-001). Oracles 11/1.1‚Üí10.0 High (315-gene) ¬∑ 300/30‚Üí10.0 High (WES) ¬∑ 150/10‚Üí15.0 High ¬∑ 99/10‚Üí9.9 not-High ¬∑ 0‚Üínot-High; corner cases `targetRegionMb=0`‚Üídivision-by-zero throws, negative count/region rejected, **<0.5 Mb** panels compute but are known-unstable (documentation, not error), TMB monotone non-decreasing in count / non-increasing in region. An independent immunotherapy biomarker alongside [[microsatellite-instability-detection]] (MSI-H) and correlated with the neoantigen load of [[neoantigen-peptide-generation]], acted on by [[cancer-variant-tier-classification-amp-asco-cap]] / [[clinical-actionability-oncokb-levels]]. **One flagged conflict**: the unsupported registry three-tier "Low <6 / Intermediate 6‚Äì20 / High >20" scheme (no authoritative source for the 6/20 boundaries) resolved to the single source-backed two-tier ‚â•10 cutoff; research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-tmb-001-evidence]].
- [[variant-allele-frequency-and-binomial-ci]] ‚Äî Oncology family, thirty-sixth ONCO-* unit (ONCO-VAF-001): the **foundational VAF primitive** the VAF-based Oncology family sits on ‚Äî three model-free quantities. (1) **Empirical VAF = altReads/totalReads** (= alt AD / sum AD, GATK Mutect2 FAQ; the model-free ratio, **not** Mutect2's model-estimate `AF` field). (2) The **Wilson score binomial confidence interval** on the proportion `center=(pÃÇ+z¬≤/2n)/(1+z¬≤/n)`, `margin=(z/(1+z¬≤/n))¬∑‚àö(pÃÇ(1‚àípÃÇ)/n+z¬≤/4n¬≤)`, **z=1.96** for 95% (Wilson 1927) ‚Äî the genuinely distinct statistical content **not represented elsewhere**, chosen over **Wald** because it stays within [0,1] with non-zero width at the extremes (`pÃÇ=0`‚Üílower exactly 0 / `pÃÇ=1`‚Üíupper exactly 1) where Wald overshoots/collapses. (3) The CNAqc purity/ploidy correction **`AdjustVAFForPurity`** = `m¬∑CCF = VAF¬∑(2(1‚àíœÄ)+œÄ¬∑n_tot)/œÄ` (inverting CNAqc *Genome Biology* 2024 `v=mœÄ/(2(1‚àíœÄ)+œÄ¬∑n_tot)`, normal ploidy 2). Oracles 25/100‚Üí0.25 ¬∑ 0/10‚Üí0.00 ¬∑ 10/10‚Üí1.00, Wilson (25,100)‚Üí0.2592 [0.1755,0.3430] & no-overshoot (0,10)‚Üí[0,0.2775] / (10,10)‚Üí[0.7225,1], correction (0.40,0.80,2)‚Üí1.00 / (0.20,0.50,2)‚Üí0.80 / (0.30,0.50,4)‚Üí1.80; corner cases VAF>1 alignment-artifact/totalReads=0/œÄ=0 all guarded. The empirical VAF is the same `altReads/totalReads` [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] compares and [[ctdna-detection-and-tumor-fraction]] averages; `AdjustVAFForPurity` shares the CNAqc/Tarabichi model [[tumor-purity-from-mutation-vaf]] inverts for œÄ and [[cancer-cell-fraction-clonal-clustering]] divides by m for CCF; two source-backed assumptions (z=1.96 verbatim, normal CN=2); research-grade, not for clinical use; record [[onco-vaf-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics pan-genome family anchor (first PANGEN-* unit, PANGEN-CLUSTER-001): greedy incremental homolog/ortholog clustering (`ClusterGenes`) on the CD-HIT model (Li & Godzik 2006) ‚Äî process genes long‚Üíshort, assign each to the first existing cluster whose representative it matches at ‚â• identity threshold else start a new cluster; global identity = identical aligned positions / alignment length (`-G 1`), Roary default 95% for orthologs (Page 2015); homolog groups only (no gene-neighbourhood/synteny paralog-split step), alignment-free identity may underestimate when internal indels are needed; sibling of [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]] / [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]] / [[average-nucleotide-identity]]; upstream of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]]; deviations None; record [[pangen-cluster-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics pan-genome family, second PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-CORE-001): the **pan-genome partition** `ConstructPanGenome` **downstream** of the clustering step ‚Äî split gene clusters across N genomes into **core / accessory / unique** by cluster **occupancy** with the fractional Roary rule `occupancy/N ‚â• coreFraction` ("at least 99% of samples", **not** `floor(coreFraction¬∑N)`; hard core >99% / soft core 95‚Äì99% / shell 15‚Äì95% / cloud <15%, Page 2015), compute **genomic fluidity** `œÜ=[2/(N(N‚àí1))]¬∑Œ£_{k<l}(U_k+U_l)/(M_k+M_l)` ‚àà[0,1] (Kislyuk 2011; 0 identical / 1 disjoint; 3-genome oracle 10/18=0.5ÃÑ), and classify **open ‚ü∫ alpha<1 / closed ‚ü∫ alpha>1** by the **Heaps'-law** decay exponent (Tettelin 2008, micropan); the N-genome occupancy counterpart of the pairwise-RBH [[genome-comparison-core-dispensable]], both the Tettelin 2005 core/dispensable model; downstream of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two source-backed assumptions (clustering delegated to k-mer-Jaccard `ClusterGenes`, empty-pair fluidity term‚Üí0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-core-001-evidence]].
- [[pan-genome-heaps-law-fit]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics pan-genome family, third PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-HEAP-001): the **pan-genome growth model** / dedicated **Heaps'-law fitting engine** underneath the partition's open/closed facet ‚Äî binarize the gene **presence/absence matrix** (count>0‚Üí1), extract the **new-gene curve** by the micropan first-appearance rule (a cluster is new at genome i‚â•2 when cumulative presence is 1 at row i and 0 at row i‚àí1; genome index starts at 2), pool over random orderings (n.perm 100), fit the **power law** `y=K¬∑x^(-alpha)` by bounded least squares `J=sqrt(Œ£(y‚àíK¬∑x^(-alpha))¬≤)/|x|` over K‚àà[0,10000]/alpha‚àà[0,2] from start `(mean(y at x==2),1)`, classify **open ‚ü∫ alpha<1 / closed ‚ü∫ alpha>1** (micropan verbatim, boundary not-open); exact oracles x=[2,3] y=[8,4]‚Üíalpha ln2/ln(3/2)‚âà1.7095 K‚âà26.164 closed, constant y=[1,1]‚Üíalpha 0 K 1 open, Tettelin 2005 qualitative anchor; the fitting engine whose alpha [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]] reports, consuming the families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]]; two assumptions (optimizer method non-correctness-affecting, fixed-seed RNG); no contradictions; record [[pangen-heap-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] ‚Äî comparative-genomics pan-genome family, fourth PANGEN-* unit (PANGEN-MARKER-001): **phylogenetic marker selection** `SelectPhylogeneticMarkers` + the `CountParsimonyInformativeSites` primitive ‚Äî from gene clusters across N genomes pick **single-copy core genes** (present **exactly once in every genome**, panX; **core** = "at least 99% of samples", Roary; paralog clusters filtered out) that carry **variable positions**, then **rank by descending parsimony-informative-site count** capped at `maxMarkers`; a **parsimony-informative site** (Zvelebil & Baum 2008) = a column with ‚â•2 states, each in ‚â•2 sequences ‚Üí **monomorphic**/**singleton** columns score 0, a single-copy core cluster with **0 PIS** excluded; the input-selection step **upstream of** core-genome tree building (panX‚ÜíFastTree), makes no tree-accuracy claim (recombination caveat); oracles `AAAAA`/`AAACA`/`AACCG`/`ACCTG`‚ÜíPIS 2 (cols 3,5), 3-genome selection excludes paralog/not-core/conserved; selects the single-copy subset of [[pan-genome-core-accessory-partition]], consumes families of [[pan-genome-gene-clustering]], single-copy-ortholog constraint shared with [[ortholog-detection-reciprocal-best-hits]]; one assumption (no in-repo aligner ‚Üí PIS over equal-length members, unequal‚ÜíPIS 0); no contradictions; record [[pangen-marker-001-evidence]].
- [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] ‚Äî the anchor for the **phylogenetics** `PHYLO-*` family (first PHYLO-* unit, PHYLO-BOOT-001): **Felsenstein's bootstrap** (Felsenstein 1985) ‚Äî attach a **confidence to each clade** of an inferred tree by **resampling alignment columns (sites) with replacement** into same-length pseudo-alignments (taxa kept, characters resampled), rebuilding a tree per replicate (distance matrix ‚Üí UPGMA/NJ), and scoring each **non-terminal clade of the reference tree** by the **fraction of replicate trees containing a clade with the identical terminal-leaf-name set** (Biopython `get_support`; Lemoine 2018 "proportion of pseudo-trees containing that branch"); binary per-replicate, only reference-tree clades scored, support = `count/replicates`, thresholds 70%/95% descriptive; oracles two-group `AAAAAAAAAA`/`GGGGGGGGGG` UPGMA+JukesCantor seed 42 ‚Üí support{A,B}={C,D}=1.0, all-identical `ACGTACGT`‚Üíall clades 1.0; invariants support‚àà[0,1] / determinism / keys=non-trivial reference clades / null/<2-seq/replicates<1 throw; the **first general distance-based-phylogenetics concept** in the wiki (no NJ/UPGMA/distance-matrix page yet), **distinct from** the CCF-constraint oncology builder [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix, no resampling) and a confidence layer over the tree the marker selector [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] feeds; two source-consistent assumptions (rooted-clade scoring vs unrooted bipartitions matching Biopython, proportion [0,1] vs percentage √ó100); no contradictions; record [[phylo-boot-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-comparison-metrics]] ‚Äî the second phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-COMP-001): **tree comparison** ‚Äî three operations on an already-built rooted binary `PhyloNode` tree. **Robinson‚ÄìFoulds distance** (`RobinsonFouldsDistance` = symmetric difference `A+B` of the two trees' canonical split/bipartition sets, Robinson & Foulds 1981; raw count, proper metric, **even**, rooted-clade = Wikipedia dummy-leaf-at-root; **max RF = 2(n‚àí2) rooted vs 2(n‚àí3) unrooted**), **MRCA** (`FindMRCA`, deepest common ancestor, O(n) recursive leaf-name match, not-in-tree‚Üínull), **patristic distance** (`PatristicDistance` = `dist(x,MRCA)+dist(y,MRCA)` branch-length sum, not-in-tree‚ÜíNaN, zero-branches‚Üí0); invariants RF identity/symmetric/‚â•0/even, MRCA symmetric/always-ancestor/unique, patristic PD(x,x)=0/symmetric/‚â•0; scope rooted-binary-only (two ¬ß7 decisions); the deterministic **compare** counterpart to the resampling-confidence [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] (agreement vs disagreement of the same split primitive, no resampling), distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-comp-001-evidence]].
- [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] ‚Äî the third phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-DIST-001): the **pairwise evolutionary-distance** primitive emitting the symmetric *n√ón* matrix distance-based tree building (NJ/UPGMA) consumes ‚Äî `CalculatePairwiseDistance`/`CalculateDistanceMatrix` over four methods **Hamming** (raw diff count) / **p-distance** (`differences/comparableSites`, uncorrected) / **Jukes‚ÄìCantor JC69** (`-3/4¬∑ln(1‚àí4p/3)`, equal-base/equal-rate) / **Kimura-2-parameter K2P** (`-1/2¬∑ln((1‚àí2S‚àíV)¬∑‚àö(1‚àí2V))`, S=transition/V=transversion); matrix symmetric / zero-diagonal / non-negative / *n√ón*, correction ordering **JC69‚â•p & K2P‚â•p**, triangle inequality expected-not-guaranteed; **pairwise deletion** (gaps + ambiguous IUPAC N/R/Y skipped, only A,C,G,T compared), case-insensitive; **saturation** JC69‚Üí+‚àû at p‚â•3/4 / K2P‚Üí+‚àû at V‚â•1/2, all-gap/empty‚Üí0 (`0/n‚Üí0`), unequal-length‚ÜíArgumentException, null‚ÜíArgumentNullException; oracles `ACGTACGT`/`TCGTACGT`‚ÜíHamming 1/p 0.125/JC69‚âà0.137, pure-transition `GCGT` K2P‚âà0.34657 vs pure-transversion `CCGT`‚âà0.31713, mixed‚âà0.30679, gap‚Üí7 comparable sites; the **upstream substrate** the family sits on ‚Äî [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples + re-runs it per replicate, [[tree-comparison-metrics]] compares the trees it feeds; distinct from the column-selecting [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] and the distance-matrix-free [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]]; two API-contract assumptions (empty/all-gap‚Üí0, pairwise deletion); no contradictions; record [[phylo-dist-001-evidence]].
- [[tree-statistics]] ‚Äî a phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` unit (PHYLO-STATS-001): **whole-tree descriptive statistics** read off a single rooted binary `PhyloNode` ‚Äî `GetLeaves` (terminal nodes, no children; count via `.Count()` = Biopython `count_terminals`), `CalculateTreeLength` (**total tree length = Œ£ all branch lengths**; undefined/default 0 branch ‚Üí 0; the minimum-evolution quantity, Rzhetsky & Nei 1992; Biopython `total_branch_length`/DendroPy `Tree.length()`), `GetTreeDepth` (**tree height = edges on the longest root-to-leaf path**, counts edges not nodes; single-node 0; empty tree ‚àí1); oracles balanced `((A:1,B:1):1,(C:1,D:1):1)`‚Üí4/6/2, caterpillar‚Üí4/5/3, single leaf‚Üí1/branch-len/0, null root‚Üí‚àÖ/0/‚àí1; the **descriptive-summary** sibling of the **compare/query** [[tree-comparison-metrics]] (its Œ£-all-branches length is the whole-tree analogue of patristic distance's per-path sum), over the same `PhyloNode` [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]] resamples and [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] feeds via UPGMA/NJ; one assumption (null `PhyloNode`‚Üîempty-tree convention); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[distance-based-tree-construction]] ‚Äî the phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` **tree-building core** (PHYLO-TREE-001): the step that **consumes an [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]] and emits a `PhyloNode` tree** via two agglomerative methods on `PhylogeneticAnalyzer` (`BuildTree` from sequences / `BuildTreeFromMatrix` from a pre-computed matrix; returns `PhylogeneticTree` Root/Taxa/DistanceMatrix/Method). **UPGMA** (Sokal & Michener 1958) ‚Äî rooted **ultrametric**, molecular-clock, nearest-pair merge, arithmetic-mean distance update, **height = d/2**, incremental branch lengths, O(n¬≥)/O(n¬≤). **Neighbor-Joining** (Saitou & Nei 1987) ‚Äî **unrooted** (midpoint-rooted final join preserving patristic distances), clock-free, join the **minimum-Q** pair `Q(i,j)=(n‚àí2)¬∑d(i,j)‚àíŒ£d(i,k)‚àíŒ£d(j,k)`, branch lengths `Œ¥(f,u)=d(f,g)/2+(Œ£d(f,k)‚àíŒ£d(g,k))/(2(n‚àí2))`, **correct topology for additive matrices**, **negative branches preserved (no clamping)**, O(n¬≥); invariants INV-01..05 (all taxa leaves, binary, n leaves / n‚àí1 internal, UPGMA‚â•0) + UPGMA ultrametric/rooted/height=d/2 + NJ additive-correct/may-be-negative/no-clock; oracles UPGMA 5S-rRNA ‚Üí(a,b)@17‚Üí((a,b),e)@22‚Üí(c,d)@28‚Üífinal@33 (root 16.5, all tips 16.5), NJ 5-taxon ‚ÜíQ‚ÇÅ(a,b)=‚àí50, Œ¥(a,u)=2‚Ä¶Œ¥(e,w)=1; the **hinge** of the family ‚Äî downstream of [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]], wrapped per-replicate by [[phylogenetic-bootstrap-support]], its output compared/queried by [[tree-comparison-metrics]] and summarized by [[tree-statistics]], serialized by Newick ([[phylo-newick-001-evidence]]); distinct from [[tumor-phylogeny-clonal-tree-reconstruction]] (no distance matrix) and [[phylogenetic-marker-selection]] (selects columns, builds no tree); no deviations, no contradictions; record [[phylo-tree-001-evidence]].
- [[bed-format-parsing]] ‚Äî FileIO file-parsing `PARSE-*` family anchor (first PARSE-* unit, PARSE-BED-001): UCSC **BED** interval parsing keyed on the **0-based half-open** coordinate model (`chromStart` 0-based / `chromEnd` 1-based-exclusive, length `chromEnd‚àíchromStart`, `chromStart==chromEnd` = zero-length insertion; contrast 1-based GFF/GTF/VCF), the **BED3‚ÜíBED12** column ladder (`chrom`/`chromStart`/`chromEnd` + optional `name`/`score`/`strand`/`thick*`/`itemRgb`/`block*`), and the UCSC validation rules (`chromStart ‚â§ chromEnd` else null, score clamp [0,1000], strand ‚àà +/‚àí/., first-line column-count lock, BED12 first-blockStart-0 / blockCount = array lengths / no-overlap / last-block-reaches-end); the malformed-input target of [[fuzzing]]; deviations None (rules verbatim from UCSC FAQ + Wikipedia); record [[parse-bed-001-evidence]].
- [[phred-quality-encoding]] ‚Äî the FASTQ quality-score encoding concept (shared by FileIO parsing + Assembly trimming): Phred score `Q=‚àí10¬∑log‚ÇÅ‚ÇÄ(p)` / `p=10^(‚àíQ/10)`, the +10-Q=10√ó-fewer-errors ladder (Q20/Q30 QC thresholds), the two live ASCII offsets **Phred+33** (Sanger/Illumina 1.8+, ASCII 33‚Äì126, Q0‚Äì93) vs **Phred+64** (Illumina 1.3‚Äì1.7, ASCII 64‚Äì126, Q0‚Äì62) with boundary chars (`!`=Q0/`I`=Q40/`~`=Q93 vs `@`=Q0/`h`=Q40/`~`=Q62), deterministic per-record offset auto-detection (`<'@'`‚Üí+33, high-band‚Üí+64, ambiguous `@`‚Äì`I`‚Üídefault +33), why a mis-detected offset silently corrupts all downstream Q-stats/trim/filter, and **cross-variant conversion** as a pure ¬±31 re-offset (score invariant; Phred+64‚ÜíPhred+33 always safe, Phred+33‚ÜíPhred+64 overflows for Q>62); anchored on the primary FASTQ spec **Cock et al. 2010**; traced by [[parse-fastq-001-evidence]] and the dedicated Phred-handling unit [[quality-phred-001-evidence]], reused by [[quality-trimming-running-sum]].
- [[fastq-quality-statistics]] ‚Äî the FASTQ **quality-statistics** surface (QUALITY-STATS-001), **distinct from and downstream of** [[phred-quality-encoding]] (which the encoding concept explicitly flags as a separate surface): summary/QC scalars over the **decoded** per-base Phred scores ‚Äî **mean** (arithmetic mean of scores, *not* error-probability-averaged), **median** (odd = middle, **even = mean of the two central order statistics**), **min/max**, **population variance/std dev** (`œÉ¬≤=(1/N)Œ£(Q·µ¢‚àíŒº)¬≤`, **√∑N not N‚àí1** ‚Äî the quality string is the complete population), and the **`% ‚â• Q20` / `% ‚â• Q30`** fractions with **inclusive `‚â•`** thresholds (Illumina: `% ‚â• Q30` the NGS run-quality benchmark); **encoding-independent** (operates on decoded scores, so Phred+64 with the same scores gives identical stats ‚Äî **consumes** the decode contract of [[quality-phred-001-evidence]] / [[phred-quality-encoding]]); `CalculateQ30Percentage` == `CalculateStatistics(...).PercentAboveQ30`; oracles `5?I`‚Üí20/30/40 mean 30.0/median 30/var 200/3/œÉ‚âà8.16497/%‚â•Q20 100/%‚â•Q30‚âà66.67, even `5II?`‚Üímedian 35.0, single `I`‚ÜíœÉ=0; corner cases even/odd median, single-element œÉ=0, empty/null ‚Üí zeroed `QualityStatistics` (TotalBases=0); record [[quality-stats-001-evidence]].
- [[insdc-feature-location]] ‚Äî the shared INSDC (DDBJ/ENA/GenBank) feature-table **location-descriptor** grammar underlying both GenBank and EMBL flat files (same location string, different line syntax): 1-based-inclusive coordinates (contrast BED 0-based), descriptors `n..m`/single `n`/between-bases `n^m`/`<`/`>` partials/`complement`/`join`/`order`/`complement(join(‚Ä¶))` with the no-nested-join/order rule, remote refs `accession.version:span`; operator assembly semantics (`join`/`order` concatenate in order, `complement` reverse-complements, `complement(join(a,b))==join(complement(b),complement(a))`), offline-first caller-supplied remote resolver, `<`/`>`-verbatim-slice assumption; oracles `join(1..3,7..9)`/`ACGTACGTAC`‚Üí`ACGGTA`, `complement(Y.1:1..4)`‚Üí`GTTT`; traced jointly by [[parse-genbank-001-evidence]] and [[parse-embl-001-evidence]].
- [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] ‚Äî anchor for the **population-genetics** `POP-*` family (**first POP-\* unit**, POP-ANCESTRY-001): estimate an individual's **ancestry proportions Q** (genome fraction from each of K reference populations) from unlinked SNP genotypes via **supervised/projection ADMIXTURE** ‚Äî reference allele frequencies **F fixed/known**, only Q estimated by EM. Alexander, Novembre & Lange 2009 model: genotype g‚àà{0,1,2}=allele-1 copy count, **log-likelihood Eq. 2** `L=Œ£·µ¢Œ£‚±º{g¬∑ln(Œ£_k q¬∑f)+(2‚àíg)¬∑ln(Œ£_k q¬∑(1‚àíf))}` under simplex `Œ£_k q_ik=1`; **FRAPPE EM Eq. 4** `q^{n+1}=(1/2J)Œ£‚±º[g¬∑a_ijk+(2‚àíg)¬∑b_ijk]` (a/b = posteriors an allele-1/allele-2 copy came from k), EM monotone ascent, convergence Eq. 5 ŒîL<Œµ=10‚Åª‚Å¥, O(IJK¬≤); oracles symmetric K=2/J=2 f_A=[0.8,0.2]/f_B=[0.2,0.8] g=[2,0] ‚Üí one EM iter **(0.8,0.2) exactly** ‚Üí converges (1.0,0.0), single-SNP g=2‚Üí(0.9,0.1)/g=1‚Üí(0.5,0.5) uninformative-het/g=0‚Üí(0.1,0.9), identical panels uniform fixed point; INV simplex Œ£_k q=1 & EM L non-decreasing, missing g‚àâ{0,1,2} skipped, empty inputs‚Üíempty; **label non-identifiability** (K! maxima under population relabeling) **pinned by fixed labelled reference panels** (ADMIXTURE manual ¬ß2.10/¬ß2.14) so Q interpretable relative to supplied labels; scope = estimate-Q-given-fixed-F only (does NOT jointly learn F, run unsupervised block-relaxation, choose K, or model linkage); **distinct from** the tree-building phylogenetics `PHYLO-*` family ([[distance-based-tree-construction]], [[evolutionary-distance-matrix]]) ‚Äî a mixture-weight/EM decomposition of one admixed individual, not a tree; two research-grade assumptions (maxIterations budget + Œµ convergence; skip-missing); no contradictions; record [[pop-ancestry-001-evidence]].
- [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] ‚Äî population-genetics `POP-*` family diversity-statistics unit (**second POP-\* unit**, POP-DIV-001, sibling of the anchor [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]): four classical within-population variation scalars from an aligned sample (n seqs, length L, S segregating sites) ‚Äî **nucleotide diversity œÄ** = Œ£_{i<j} d_ij/(C(n,2)¬∑L) (Nei & Li 1979, mean per-site pairwise differences), **Watterson's Œ∏_W** = S/a_n with harmonic a_n = Œ£_{i=1}^{n‚àí1} 1/i (per-site S/(a_n¬∑L); Watterson 1975), **Tajima's D** = (kÃÇ ‚àí S/a_1)/‚àö(e_1¬∑S+e_2¬∑S(S‚àí1)) (Tajima 1989 ‚Äî normalized œÄ-vs-Watterson difference; **kÃÇ = pairwise-difference COUNT not per-site œÄ**; D‚âà0 neutral, D<0 excess rare alleles‚Üísweep/expansion, D>0 deficit‚Üíbalancing/contraction), and **heterozygosity/gene diversity** H_exp = (1/L)Œ£(1‚àíŒ£p¬≤) with unbiased haploid H_obs = n/(n‚àí1)¬∑H_exp ‚â° œÄ (Nei 1978); Wikipedia oracle n=5/L=20/S=4 ‚Üí kÃÇ=2.0/œÄ=0.1/S/a_1‚âà1.92/Œ∏_W‚âà0.096/**D‚âà0.273** (TD-C01/TD-C02); guards n<3‚ÜíD undefined‚Üí0, S=0/monomorphic‚Üíall 0, Var‚â§0‚ÜíD=0, `CalculateTajimasD(kÃÇ,S,n)` expects kÃÇ not œÄ; **distinct from** the anchor's ancestry-proportion EM (within-population *variation amount* vs *ancestry decomposition*), summary-only (no variant calling / phasing / recombination / Fu-Li / Fay-Wu); all formulae exact-match, no deviations; record [[pop-div-001-evidence]].
- [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] ‚Äî **foundational** population-genetics `POP-*` primitive (POP-FREQ-001): turn per-locus **genotype counts** into **allele frequencies**, derive **minor allele frequency (MAF)**, and **filter variants by MAF** ‚Äî the numeric substrate under the rest of the POP family (the fixed reference frequencies **F** of [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]] and the per-site `p_i` behind the heterozygosity term of [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] are exactly these quantities). Biallelic allele freq `p = f(AA)+¬Ωf(AB)` / `q = f(BB)+¬Ωf(AB)` via counts `total=2¬∑(n_AA+n_AB+n_BB)`, `major=2¬∑n_AA+n_AB`, `minor=2¬∑n_BB+n_AB` (**INV `p+q=1`**, `major+minor=total`; oracle 49/42/9 ‚Üí 0.70/0.30); VCF/PLINK dosage `alt_freq = Œ£g/(2n)`, `MAF = min(alt_freq, 1‚àíalt_freq)` (**INV `0 ‚â§ MAF ‚â§ 0.5`**, symmetric ‚Äî alt_freq 0.7 ‚Üí MAF 0.3; monomorphic ‚Üí 0; 50/50 ‚Üí 0.5); MAF filter = inclusive `[minMAF,maxMAF]` band with conventional HapMap/common(>0.05)-vs-rare(<0.05) thresholds; edge cases zero samples‚Üí(0,0), empty vector‚ÜíMAF 0, **negative count ‚Üí `ArgumentOutOfRangeException`**; scope = biallelic counting/normalization only (no HWE test, no multiallelic, no phasing/imputation); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-freq-001-evidence]].
- [[population-differentiation-fst]] ‚Äî population-genetics `POP-*` differentiation unit (POP-FST-001): measure **how differentiated populations are** ‚Äî fraction of total variation due to between-population structure ‚Äî from per-population allele frequencies (**consumes** [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]; distinct from within-sample [[genetic-diversity-statistics]] and from ancestry decomposition [[ancestry-estimation-admixture]]). **Wright 1965 variance Fst** `Fst = œÉ_S¬≤/(pBar(1‚àípBar))`, two-pop size-weighted `pBar=(n1¬∑p1+n2¬∑p2)/(n1+n2)` / `œÉ_S¬≤=(n1(p1‚àípBar)¬≤+n2(p2‚àípBar)¬≤)/(n1+n2)`, multi-locus **ratio-of-sums** `Œ£œÉ_S¬≤/Œ£het` ‚Äî the **population parameter from known allele freqs**, explicitly **NOT** the Weir & Cockerham 1984 Œ∏ estimator (no bias correction); **F-statistics** heterozygosity partition `Fis=1‚àíHi/Hs`/`Fit=1‚àíHi/Ht`/`Fst=1‚àíHs/Ht` with **exact** `(1‚àíFit)=(1‚àíFis)(1‚àíFst)`; INV Fst‚àà[0,1] (0=panmixia/1=fixed differences), Fis‚àà[‚àí1,1] (negative under excess heterozygotes), pairwise matrix symmetric + zero diagonal, **not a metric** (fails triangle inequality); oracles fixed p1=1/p2=0‚Üí**1.0 exactly**, pop1=(.9,.8)/pop2=(.1,.2)‚Üí1/2, Cavalli-Sforza/Elhaik ref values, Hartl-Clark bands (0.05/0.15/0.25); edge cases denominator 0 (empty/both-fixed-same/monomorphic)‚Üí**return 0**; scope = Wright Fst + heterozygosity F-statistics only (no significance test, no bootstrap CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-fst-001-evidence]].
- [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]] ‚Äî population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-HW-001): the **Hardy-Weinberg equilibrium chi-square test** ‚Äî does a biallelic locus's observed genotype counts match the `p¬≤/2pq/q¬≤` proportions expected under random mating? **Consumes** genotype counts from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]] (POP-FREQ-001, whose scope explicitly leaves the HWE test here) and turns them into a **hypothesis test**. Estimate `p = (2¬∑n_AA + n_Aa)/(2n)` / `q = 1‚àíp`, expected counts `E = {p¬≤n, 2pqn, q¬≤n}`, **Pearson œá¬≤ = Œ£ (O‚àíE)¬≤/E** over the 3 genotype classes, **df = 1** (`#genotypes ‚àí #alleles = 3 ‚àí 2`), p-value from chi-square CDF (lower-incomplete-gamma approx), default **Œ± = 0.05** critical value **3.841**; returns `InEquilibrium`/`ChiSquare`/`PValue`. Oracles Ford moth (1469,138,5)‚Üí`p‚âà0.954`/`œá¬≤‚âà0.83`‚Üíin-eq, perfect (25,50,25)‚Üí`œá¬≤=0`, excess-het (10,80,10)‚Üí`œá¬≤=36 ‚â´ 3.84`‚Üíout-of-eq; edge cases **zero samples‚ÜíInEquilibrium true, PValue 1** (no evidence against H‚ÇÄ), monomorphic‚Üí`œá¬≤=0`, **expected-0 term skipped** (div-by-zero guard); deviation causes non-random mating/selection/mutation/migration/drift/**genotyping error**; scope = biallelic chi-square only (no Wigginton 2005 **exact test**, no multiallelic); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-hw-001-evidence]].
- [[linkage-disequilibrium]] ‚Äî population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-LD-001): **non-random association between alleles at two loci** ‚Äî a **pairwise inter-locus** quantity distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), and the single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]; **consumes** allele/haplotype frequencies from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. `D = p_AB ‚àí p_A¬∑p_B` (Robbins 1918), normalized `D' = |D|/D_max` clamped [0,1] (Lewontin 1964, sign-branched `D_max`) and `r¬≤ = D¬≤/(p_A¬∑q_A¬∑p_B¬∑q_B)` (Hill & Robertson 1968); implemented **phase-free** via the diploid-frequency result `R_AB=r_AB` (Wright 1933) ‚Äî `r¬≤` = squared Pearson correlation of 0/1/2 genotype dosage vectors `Cov¬≤/(Var¬∑Var)`, `D` recovered from `Cov_diploid=2D ‚áí D=Cov/2`; `FindHaplotypeBlocks` = simplified adjacent-pair Gabriel 2002 (consecutive `r¬≤ ‚â• threshold`, default **0.7**, ‚â•2 variants); INV `0‚â§r¬≤‚â§1`/`0‚â§|D'|‚â§1`, empty‚Üí`r¬≤=0,D'=0`, monomorphic/zero-variance‚Üí`r¬≤=0` (guarded div), distance+IDs preserved, blocks Start‚â§End/‚â•2/non-overlapping/position-ordered; perfect correlation **and** perfect anti-correlation both ‚Üí`r¬≤=1`/`D'=1` (sign-blind); scope = two-biallelic-loci r¬≤/D' + adjacent-pair blocks only (no full LD matrix, no phasing/EM, no LD-decay fit, no exact Gabriel CI); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-ld-001-evidence]].
- [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]] ‚Äî population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-ROH-001): detect **long uninterrupted homozygous stretches** (**runs of homozygosity**, `FindROH`) in one individual and summarize their burden as the genomic inbreeding coefficient **F_ROH** ‚Äî a **per-individual segment-detection** problem distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), two-locus [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]]. **Window-free consecutive-runs** scan (Marras 2015 / detectRUNS): walk position-sorted 0/1/2 genotypes (1 = heterozygous = "opposite"), grow a run, **terminate** when opposite calls exceed `maxOppRun` (a few tolerated to absorb genotyping error) or an inter-SNP gap exceeds `maxGap` (breaks even an all-homozygous run); retain a stretch only if it passes **both** `minSNP` **and** `minLengthBps` (PLINK `--homozyg-snp 100` **and** `--homozyg-kb 1000`, one alone insufficient). **F_ROH = Œ£L_roh / L_auto** (McQuillan 2008 verbatim; `L_auto` = SNP-covered autosome ‚âà2,674 Mb; r=0.86 vs pedigree; min-length lever ‚â•0.5/1.5/5 Mb, 1.5 Mb best); oracle Œ£L_roh=20 Mb/L_auto=100 Mb ‚Üí **0.20**, whole-genome ‚Üí 1.0; INV each run once/Start‚â§End/SnpCount, one tolerated het keeps one run / het beyond splits, gap>maxGap breaks, below minSNP-or-minLength discarded, unsorted ordered internally, genotype 2 = homozygous, leading hets skipped, F_ROH‚àà[0,1]; two API-encoding assumptions (0/1/2 encoding; **missing-genotype handling out of scope** ‚Äî no missing sentinel, non-`1` treated homozygous); scope = consecutive-runs scan + F_ROH only (no PLINK sliding-window scoring, no missing bounding, no LOD/model-based callers, no cohort ROH-island mapping); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-roh-001-evidence]].
- [[selection-scan-ihs-ehh]] ‚Äî population-genetics `POP-*` unit (POP-SELECT-001): detect **recent positive selection** from **haplotype structure** ‚Äî a selective sweep leaves an unusually long, low-diversity haplotype around the selected allele. A **haplotype-length/decay** statistic distinct from per-locus counting ([[allele-genotype-frequencies]]), within-sample diversity ([[genetic-diversity-statistics]]), between-population differentiation ([[population-differentiation-fst]]), single-locus [[hardy-weinberg-equilibrium-test]], pairwise [[linkage-disequilibrium]], and autozygosity [[runs-of-homozygosity-inbreeding]]; **consumes** derived/ancestral allele freqs from [[allele-genotype-frequencies]]. Pipeline **EHH‚ÜíiHH‚ÜíiHS‚Üíscan**: `EHH_c=Œ£C(n_h,2)/C(n_c,2)` (Sabeti 2002 / selscan Eq.3, decays 1‚Üí0 with distance), `iHH` = trapezoidal area under EHH both directions truncated at **EHH<0.05**, **unstandardized iHS = ln(iHH_A/iHH_D)** (Voight 2006, ancestral numerator), standardized to std-normal in derived-allele-freq bins, `ScanForSelection` = proportion `|iHS|>2` in ~50-SNP windows; **sign convention critical** ‚Äî Voight (A/D) is the opposite of selscan (D/A), large negative iHS ‚áí long *derived* haplotype, balanced decay ‚áí iHS‚âà0; oracles rehh F1205400‚Üí**‚àí1.978569274**, constructed panel iHH_A=10/iHH_D=40‚Üíln(0.25)=**‚àí1.386294361**; INV EHH‚àà[0,1] (1 single chromosome / 0 all-distinct), single-element bin‚Üístd iHS 0, N‚àí1 SD + 20 default 0.05 bins (overridable) affect magnitude only, throws on monomorphic core / null / empty / inconsistent length / invalid core allele / OOR coreIndex; scope = single-core iHS/EHH scan (no XP-EHH, no Fst-outlier or Tajima's-D scan, no genetic-map interpolation, no >200 kb gap masking); no deviations/contradictions; record [[pop-select-001-evidence]].
- [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] ‚Äî PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family anchor (PRIMER-TM-001): the **self-/hetero-dimer melting temperature (Tm)** of two primers via the Primer3 `ntthal` **thermodynamic alignment** over the SantaLucia & Hicks 2004 unified **DNA nearest-neighbour** model ‚Äî the **DNA** counterpart of the **RNA** Turner-2004 folding [[rna-base-pairing]] / [[pre-mirna-hairpin-detection]], distinct by modelling an intermolecular duplex at finite strand concentration. Duplex ŒîH¬∞/ŒîS¬∞ = Œ£ 10 Watson-Crick NN stacks + duplex-initiation + per-end terminal-A¬∑T-penalty + self-complementary symmetry; **bimolecular Tm** `ŒîH¬∞¬∑1000/(ŒîS¬∞+R¬∑ln(C_T/x))‚àí273.15` with **symmetry factor x=1 (reverse-complement palindrome) / x=4 (otherwise)**; **[Na‚Å∫] entropy salt correction** `0.368¬∑(N/2)¬∑ln[Na‚Å∫]` (Tm monotone in salt); the dimer DP finds the possibly-**non-contiguous** most-stable structure (internal mismatch/loop, single/multi-base bulge, `tstack2` terminal overhang), reproducing primer3-py 2.3.0 `calc_homodimer`/`calc_heterodimer` to machine precision (GCGCGCGC self x=1 Tm 40.0906 ¬∞C, TGCATGCATG/CATGCATGCA x=4 Tm 25.6596 ¬∞C, GCGCATGCGC 2√ó2 loop Tm 43.1572 ¬∞C); **no stable dimer** (poly-A) ‚Üí `structure_found=False` ‚Üí null/NaN, invalid input (null / <2 bases / non-ACGT) ‚Üí null/NaN; deviations none remaining after the 2026-06-25 full-ntthal-DP port. Also covers the **intramolecular hairpin self-folding** extension (same engine): stem NN stacks (`NnUnifiedParams`) + **Table 4 hairpin-loop ŒîG¬∞37** (loop ŒîH¬∞=0, ŒîS¬∞=‚àíŒîG¬∞37¬∑1000/310.15) + Jacobson-Stockmayer large-loop, **unimolecular hairpin Tm Eq. 11 with NO concentration term** (Vallone & Benight concentration-independent), bimolecular init & terminal-A¬∑T penalty excluded, **bundled** special tri/tetraloop hairpin bonus tables (16 triloop / 76 tetraloop rows, applied in `calc_hairpin`, key incl. closing pair; oracle tetraloop GGGGCGAAAGCCCC Tm 85.0335 ¬∞C) plus the legacy opt-in caller increment (oracle GGGCTTTTGCCC Tm 68.6404 ¬∞C, poly-A ‚Üí null/NaN); Also covers the **per-oligo (single-strand) design Tm** path (Eq. 3 applied to a primer vs its own complement; opt-in NN Tm, legacy Wallace/Marmur-Doty unchanged default) with the **Owczarzy 2004** monovalent-quadratic and **Owczarzy 2008** divalent-Mg¬≤‚Å∫/dNTP 1/Tm salt corrections (Biopython `salt_correction` methods 5‚Äì7) and the internal-mismatch/dangling-end tables (`NnInternalMismatch`/`NnDanglingEnd`); records [[primer-tm-001-dimer-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-hairpin-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-nn-evidence]], [[primer-tm-001-special-loop-evidence]].
- [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]] ‚Äî PCR primer-design `PRIMER-*` / MolTools family (PRIMER-TM-001, **base** unit): the **Primer3 weighted per-primer penalty / objective function** `p_obj_fn` ‚Äî the *only* score Primer3 sorts candidate primers by (**lower is better**), a **selection/scoring** algorithm distinct from the thermodynamic sibling [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] (Tm enters only as one input *term*). Weighted sum of **sign-gated one-sided deviations** from each parameter optimum: Tm `temp_gt¬∑(Tm‚àíopt_tm)`/`temp_lt¬∑(opt_tm‚àíTm)`, GC% (percent 0‚Äì100) `gc_content_gt/lt`, size `length_gt/lt`, plus non-thermodynamic `compl_any¬∑self_any + compl_end¬∑self_end + num_ns¬∑#N`; left/right primers identical (`p_args`). Defaults `opt_tm=60`/`opt_size=20`, weights `temp_*=length_*=1` and `gc/self/num_ns=0` (GC optimum undefined in header) ‚áí **default objective collapses to `|Tm‚àí60|+|len‚àí20|`**; sign-gated (term=0 exactly at optimum), weight-zero short-circuit, penalty ‚â• 0 with **0 iff all-optimal**; `self_any`/`self_end` are caller-supplied Primer3 `dpal` local-alignment scores (arithmetic exact, value external, vanish under default 0 weights); oracles (60,20)‚Üí0.0/(63,20)‚Üí3.0/(57,18)‚Üí5.0/combined‚Üí8.0; record [[primer-tm-001-evidence]].
- [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] ‚Äî **PROBE** family anchor (PROBE-DESIGN-001): the **TaqMan (5'-nuclease hydrolysis-probe) design rules** ‚Äî an opt-in extension over the unchanged generic hybridization-probe designer, a distinct MolTools reagent-design algorithm alongside the primer units [[primer-dimer-thermodynamics-tm]] / [[primer3-weighted-penalty-objective]]. The probe-specific hard constraints (no analogue in primer selection): **no G at the 5' end** (a 5'-G quenches the reporter dye *even after cleavage*, so it cannot be rescued ‚Äî hard rule; `SelectTaqManStrand` moves the design to the complement/antisense strand when a compliant sense probe is impossible), **more Cs than Gs**, **no run of ‚â•4 consecutive Gs** (flagged separately from the generic homopolymer cap), **G+C 30‚Äì80%**, **length 18‚Äì22 nt** (default, `minLength`/`maxLength` parameterised ‚Äî ABI/PREMIER 18‚Äì22 vs IDT/Thermo up to 30), and the **probe Tm ‚â• primer Tm + 10 ¬∞C** gate (so the probe binds before Taq reaches it) with the primer Tm caller-supplied and the probe Tm via the PRIMER-TM-001-validated salt-adjusted `81.5+16.6¬∑log‚ÇÅ‚ÇÄ[Na‚Å∫]+41¬∑GC‚àí600/N` formula (not a TaqMan-specific nearest-neighbour calc); a `NoGuanineAt5Prime`/`PassesAll`-style checker; oracles CCATCACCCTACATCACC passes-all (primerTm ‚â§ 39.35), 5'-G/GGGG-run/more-G-than-C/len<18/GC-100% each fail, sense GTTAGGGTTAGGGTTAGG ‚Üí RC CCTAACCCTAACCCTAAC strand selection; two parameterisation assumptions (18‚Äì22 default window, repository salt-adjusted Tm engine), no source contradictions; record [[probe-design-001-evidence]].
- [[probe-offtarget-specificity-scan]] ‚Äî **PROBE** family (PROBE-VALID-001): the **hybridization-probe off-target specificity scan** ‚Äî align a candidate probe against a pooled reference with a **gapped Smith‚ÄìWaterman local alignment** and report every site whose identity clears a threshold. The **specificity-checking sibling** of [[taqman-probe-design-rules]] (composition rules), a genuinely distinct algorithm. Core improvement over the earlier **ungapped Hamming scan**: SW's gap-length maxima + **zero floor** (Smith & Waterman 1981) make it *local* and **indel-aware**, so an off-target reachable only through an insertion/deletion (which frame-shifts every downstream base and hides from a fixed window) is found ‚Äî the **gapped-vs-ungapped BLAST** improvement (Altschul 1990‚Üí1997), realized as an *exact* full SW scan (not seed-and-extend). Zero-floor traceback **trims a mismatched tail** so identity is over the matched core. Off-target call at **‚â•0.75 identity** (Kane et al. 2000 microarray cross-hyb threshold; `minIdentity` caller-configurable). On/off labelling (assumption): the first perfect ungapped full-coverage exact match = intended on-target, all else off-target. Opt-in **Karlin‚ÄìAltschul** significance (`ComputeLambdaNucleotide`/`ComputeKarlinAltschul`): `E=K¬∑m¬∑n¬∑e^(‚àíŒªS)`, Œª = root of `Œ£ p_i p_j e^(Œª s_ij)=1`, bit `S'=(ŒªS‚àíln K)/ln 2`, `E=m¬∑n¬∑2^(‚àíS')`, preconditions expected-score<0 + a positive score, K caller-supplied; +1/‚àí3 uniform-0.25 ‚Üí Œª=1.3740631 (‚âà blastn 1.37), example bit 59.9627 / E 1.7802e‚àí14. Oracles: exact + indel `ACGTAC-GTACGT` 12/12=1.0 (gapped finds, ungapped misses), indel+mismatch trimmed to 10/12=0.8333 (in @0.75, out @0.90); BLAST DNA scoring +2/‚àí3 gap ‚àí2. No source contradictions; record [[probe-valid-001-evidence]].
- [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]] ‚Äî compression-based member of the sequence complexity/entropy family (SEQ-COMPLEX-COMPRESS-001): **Lempel‚ÄìZiv (LZ76) complexity** `c(S)` = number of distinct phrases in a left-to-right exhaustive-history parse, length-normalized as `c/(n/log_b n)` (b<2 clamps log base to 2, returns the normalized value). A **distinct scalar measure** from the composition Shannon-entropy [[protein-low-complexity-seg]], the fixed-k [[k-mer-statistics]] k-entropy, and the explicit-repeat [[repetitive-element-detection]] ‚Äî LZ is low exactly where those low-complexity/repeat tracts are. Records [[seq-complex-compress-001-evidence]].
- [[dust-low-complexity-score]] ‚Äî triplet-frequency member of the sequence complexity/entropy family and the DNA-sequence low-complexity **masker** (SEQ-COMPLEX-DUST-001): the **DUST** score `score = ‚àë_t c(c‚àí1)/2 / (L‚àí2)` over nucleotide triplet counts (Morgulis et al. 2006, `k=3` hardcoded), where a **HIGH score ‚áí LOW complexity**; default window 64 / mask threshold 2.0 (level 20); a **distinct scalar measure** from the compression [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]], the fixed-k [[k-mer-statistics]] k-entropy, the protein [[protein-low-complexity-seg]] (opposite direction ‚Äî Shannon entropy, low ‚áí low complexity), and the explicit-repeat [[repetitive-element-detection]]. Oracles `ATGC`‚Üí0.0 / `ACGTACGT`‚Üí0.333‚Ä¶ / `AAAAAA`‚Üí1.5 / `AAAAAAAAAA`‚Üí3.5; homopolymer max `(L‚àí3)/2`. Records [[seq-complex-dust-001-evidence]].
- [[windowed-sequence-complexity-profile]] ‚Äî the **profiling / scanning** member of the sequence complexity/entropy family (SEQ-COMPLEX-WINDOW-001): a **sliding-window** scan that emits a per-position `ComplexityPoint` *profile*, each window carrying a **Shannon entropy** of base composition (`H = ‚àíŒ£ p log‚ÇÇ p`, uniform ‚áí 2.0, homopolymer ‚áí 0) **and** a **linguistic complexity** `LC = Œ£ V·µ¢ / Œ£ Vmax,i` (`Vmax,i = min(4^i, N‚àíi+1)`, `maxWordLength = min(6, w)`; Gabrielian & Bolshoy 1999 / Troyanskaya 2002). The family's **only profile** and its first home of linguistic complexity ‚Äî distinct from the whole-sequence scalars [[sequence-complexity-compression-lempel-ziv]] / [[dust-low-complexity-score]] / [[k-mer-statistics]] k-entropy, and the DNA profiling analogue of the protein [[protein-low-complexity-seg]]. Window count `floor((L‚àíw)/s)+1` (L‚â•w else 0), only fully-contained windows emitted, Position = `WindowStart + w/2`; oracles `ACGTACGT`‚Üí2.0 / 23-29ths, poly-A‚Üí0.0 / 6-29ths, L=24/w=8/s=8‚Üí3 windows. Records [[seq-complex-window-001-evidence]]. Also hosts the **second entry point** for the same per-window Shannon scan: the standalone **Shannon entropy profile** SEQ-ENTROPY-PROFILE-001 (entropy channel only, no linguistic complexity; record [[seq-entropy-profile-001-evidence]]).
- [[restriction-enzyme-filtering]] ‚Äî **RESTR** family anchor (RESTR-FILTER-001): filtering/selecting a restriction-enzyme **library** by properties of the cut (not searching a sequence for cut sites) ‚Äî a MolTools reagent-selection algorithm alongside [[codon-optimization]] and the primer/probe units. Two filter axes: (1) **end type** ‚Äî every Type II end is either **blunt** (center cut, both strands terminate in a base pair) or **sticky** (staggered cut, 5'/3' overhang), a **total, disjoint partition** (`GetBluntCutters()` ‚à™ `GetStickyCutters()` = full library, no third category, blunt-blunt always compatible); (2) **recognition-site length** ‚Äî `GetEnzymesByCutLength(min, max)` over the **inclusive** `[min,max]` interval, undivided Type II sites canonically **4‚Äì8 nt**. Blunt: SmaI/EcoRV/AluI/HaeIII; sticky: EcoRI(5')/KpnI(3')/PstI(3')/NotI/TaqI. Invariants: partition totality+disjointness; inclusive bounds (API-shape assumption); single-length overload == range at `min==max`; `min>max`/negative/zero‚Üíempty; the **interrupted palindrome** SfiI (`GGCCNNNN^NGGCC`, 13 nt) is sticky but correctly **excluded** by `[4,8]` (undivided sites only). Sources Wikipedia sticky/blunt + restriction enzyme + cutting-site list + NEB/REBASE + PMC; record [[restr-filter-001-evidence]].
- [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] ‚Äî **splicing** family anchor (SPLICE-ACCEPTOR-001): **3' splice site / acceptor** detection ‚Äî score candidate `AG` dinucleotides for the three cis-elements of a real 3'ss under the canonical **GU-AG rule**: (1) the **branch point** (`yUnAy` adenosine ~18‚Äì50 nt upstream), (2) the **polypyrimidine tract** (C/U-rich, U2AF65), (3) the **AG + context** (`(Yn)NYAG|G`). Three scoring surfaces ‚Äî default **PWM+PPT** `FindAcceptorSites`, opt-in **branch-point** `FindAcceptorBranchPoint` (Gao 2008 `yUnAy`), opt-in **MaxEntScan score3ss** `ScoreAcceptorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004, canonical 2.89 cross-check) ‚Äî plus U12 **YCCAC** non-canonical scoring. The PWM branch is a worked biological instance of the position-weight-matrix motif family (cf. [[known-motif-search]] / [[regulatory-element-detection]]). Record [[splice-acceptor-001-evidence]].
- [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] ‚Äî **splicing** family, **donor / 5' splice site** (SPLICE-DONOR-001), the 5' partner of [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]]: score candidate `GT/GU` dinucleotides for the almost-invariant `GU` intron start under the **GU-AG rule** against a single contiguous **`MAG|GURAGU`** consensus (positions ‚àí3..+6; 0-G/+1-U ~100%, ‚àí1-G ~80% for U1 snRNP base-pairing). Unlike the acceptor there is **no branch point / polypyrimidine tract** ‚Äî two scoring surfaces only: default **IUPAC consensus match-fraction** `FindDonorSites`/`ScoreDonorSite` (plainer than the acceptor's PWM+PPT; GC donors self-penalize via the +1-U mismatch, 8/9 vs 9/9) and opt-in **MaxEntScan score5ss** `ScoreDonorMaxEnt` (Yeo & Burge 2004 9-nt window, single 16,384-entry table with no overlapping sub-windows ‚Äî the contrast with score3ss; canonical `cagGTAAGT`‚Üí**10.86**). GC-AG + U12 **AT-AC**/`ATATCC` non-canonical donors; the `MAG|GURAGU` consensus is an [[iupac-degenerate-consensus|IUPAC-degenerate]] / [[consensus-sequence|consensus]] motif (cf. [[known-motif-search]]). Record [[splice-donor-001-evidence]].
- [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] ‚Äî **germline structural-variant (SV)** family anchor (SV-BREAKPOINT-001): **breakpoint detection from split (soft-clipped) reads** ‚Äî localize an SV breakpoint to a single base at the aligned/clipped **junction** of a split read (SAM/BAM CIGAR **soft clip `S` consumes the read but not the reference**, sits only at a read end ‚Üí **leading `S` = left / trailing `S` = right breakpoint**; a no-`S` read carries no signal), then **cluster** per-read junctions into a supported call under **positional tolerance** (ClipCrop 5 b), **minimum support** (SoftSearch ‚â• x clipped reads, default 5 / configurable 2), and **same clip-side + same chromosome**, with a **min clip length** filter (‚â§ 5 clipped bases dropped) and a `RefineBreakpoint` region-consensus method. `SplitRead` record stores the junction directly (`PrimaryPosition`/`SupplementaryPosition`/`ClipLength`). One ASSUMPTION (cluster coordinate = rounded mean of member junctions, sub-tolerance only). The germline-SV anchor orthogonal to the oncology read-evidence [[gene-fusion-detection-read-evidence]] / [[chromothripsis-inference]] and distinct from the gene-order [[genome-rearrangement-breakpoint-distance]]; research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[sv-breakpoint-001-evidence]].
- [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]] ‚Äî **germline structural-variant (SV)** family, **read-depth** member (SV-CNV-001): **read-depth CNV detection** ‚Äî call copy-number deletions/duplications from **read depth of coverage** (distinct method from the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]]; aggregate depth, not per-read junctions). **read depth ‚àù copy number** (Yoon 2009) ‚Üí **windowed counting** (non-overlapping fixed-size windows, one read per start, per-window mean RD) ‚Üí optional **GC correction** `r_i'=r_i¬∑m/m_GC` ‚Üí **log2 ratio** `log2(observed/reference depth)` (reference = overall median of window means, default self-reference) ‚Üí **integer CN = round(2¬∑2^log2)** (CNVkit "round", diploid ploidy 2) ‚Üí del/dup call + segment merge (`DetectCNV`/`SegmentCopyNumber`). Anchors (verbatim CNVkit): log2(1/2)=‚àí1‚ÜíCN 1 (loss), log2(2/2)=0‚ÜíCN 2 (Neutral), log2(3/2)=+0.585‚ÜíCN 3 (gain), log2(2.0)=+1‚ÜíCN 4 (amp); CN strictly increasing in log2, clamped **‚â• 0**. Corner cases: **zero-depth window ‚Üí no-call** (log2(0) undefined), **NaN ‚Üí Neutral**. Two ASSUMPTIONs (reference = overall median of non-zero window means; diploid ploidy 2), both source-supported. Consumes **windowed depth** (cf. exact per-base [[coverage-depth-calculation]]), not raw BAM. The oncology [[copy-number-alteration-classification]] is the discrete-state classification layer built on this same log2 ratio; [[allele-specific-copy-number-ascat]] adds BAF/purity ‚Äî this germline unit is total-CN-from-depth only. Sources Yoon 2009 + CNVkit `call.py`/docs; research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[sv-cnv-001-evidence]].
- [[discordant-pair-sv-detection]] ‚Äî **germline structural-variant (SV)** family, **discordant-read-pair / paired-end-mapping (PEM)** member (SV-DETECT-001): **SV detection from PEM signatures** ‚Äî read how a mate pair's mapped **span + orientation** deviate from the concordant **FR** proper pair (SAM FLAG 0x02; RF everted/discordant) and classify the SV type. A third read-evidence channel, orthogonal to the split-read anchor [[breakpoint-detection-split-reads]] (within-read clip junction ‚Üí single-base breakpoint) and the depth-based [[read-depth-cnv-segmentation]] (aggregate dosage); integrated callers (DELLY) combine PEM + split reads. Signatures (same chr unless noted): span `> Œº+c¬∑œÉ` FR ‚Üí **Deletion**, span `< Œº‚àíc¬∑œÉ` ‚Üí **Insertion**, **FF/RR** ‚Üí **Inversion**, everted **RF** ‚Üí **tandem Duplication**, different chromosome ‚Üí **Translocation**. Span cutoff `c` s.d. of the empirical insert-size distribution (BreakDancer `-c`, default 3); **signature-then-cluster** with **min support** ‚â• `-r` (default 2). One ASSUMPTION ‚Äî inter-chromosomal (translocation) precedence over orientation. Corner cases: insertion > insert size invisible + sequence unrecoverable by span (split-read's job), below-support clusters dropped, exact cutoff bounds. Sources Medvedev 2009 + BreakDancer (Chen 2009 / Fan 2014) + SAM/BWA proper-pair + DELLY/SVXplorer; research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[sv-detect-001-evidence]].
- [[differential-expression]] ‚Äî anchor for the **Transcriptome / RNA-seq** family (first ingested unit, TRANS-DIFF-001): **two-group differential expression** `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateFoldChange` / `FindDifferentiallyExpressed`. **log2 fold change** `log2((mean(treatment)+c)/(mean(control)+c))` (pseudocount c=1, positive = up in treatment/condition 2) + **Welch unequal-variance two-sample t-test** raw p (unbiased (N‚àí1) variances, Welch-Satterthwaite df, exact Student-t tail `p=I_{ŒΩ/(ŒΩ+t¬≤)}(ŒΩ/2,¬Ω)` via regularized incomplete beta) + **Benjamini-Hochberg FDR** reproducing R `p.adjust(method="BH")`. DE ‚áî **two-criterion gate** `|log2FC| ‚â• threshold (default 1.0) AND adjusted p < alpha (default 0.05)`; fail either ‚áí not significant. Edge cases: <2 replicates ‚Üí p=1, se=0 ‚Üí p=1/0, zero mean ‚Üí pseudocount; adjusted p ‚àà [raw p, 1]. A **simple two-group** estimator, **not** the DESeq2 negative-binomial GLM. Sources DESeq2 (Love 2014, log2FC/BH) + Science Park lesson + Welch 1947 + Student-t CDF + BH 1995. `alternative_to` the non-parametric rank-sum [[significant-taxa-detection]] (which applies no built-in FDR); structurally akin to the Fisher's-exact [[differentially-methylated-regions]] gate; distinct from the single-sample z-score [[expression-outlier-zscore-signature-score]]; DE gene lists feed [[pathway-enrichment-ora]]. Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[trans-diff-001-evidence]].
- [[expression-quantification]] ‚Äî **Transcriptome / RNA-seq** family, **quantification / normalization** unit (TRANS-EXPR-001): convert raw RNA-seq **counts ‚Üí comparable expression** with `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculateTPM` / `CalculateFPKM` / `QuantileNormalize`. **TPM** `(X_i/l_i)/Œ£(X_j/l_j)¬∑10‚Å∂` ‚Äî divide by length into RPK **then** rescale so each sample **sums to exactly 10‚Å∂** (the sum-to-a-million invariant RPKM lacks; average TPM = 10‚Å∂/#transcripts = const; Wagner 2012, Zhao/Ye/Stanton 2020). **FPKM/RPKM** `X_i¬∑10‚Åπ/(l_i¬∑N)` ‚Äî per-kilobase + per-million-mapped-reads; RPKM (single-end) ‚â° FPKM (paired) formula; `TPM = FPKM/Œ£ FPKM¬∑10‚Å∂` so FPKM does **not** sum to a constant. **Quantile normalization** (Bolstad 2003) ‚Äî match all samples to one shared distribution with no reference: sort each column, set each rank to the cross-column rank mean, re-place; **ties get the mean of the rank means they span**. Oracles: TPM A(10,2000)/B(20,4000)/C(30,1000) ‚Üí (125000,125000,750000)/Œ£=10‚Å∂; FPKM X=1000,l=2000,N=10‚Å∂ ‚Üí 500; quantile C2 tied `4`s ‚Üí 5.166‚Ä¶. Edge cases: all-zero counts ‚Üí TPM 0/0 ‚Üí emit 0; non-positive length/N ‚Üí FPKM 0; empty ‚Üí empty. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (all-zero TPM ‚Üí 0; effective length = annotated length). The within-sample (TPM/FPKM) + cross-sample (quantile) normalization **upstream** of the family anchor [[differential-expression]]; TPM/RPKM are within-sample relative measures, misused across samples (Zhao 2020). Classic count-normalization, not kallisto/salmon effective-length or edgeR/DESeq2 size factors. Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[trans-expr-001-evidence]].
- [[alternative-splicing-psi]] ‚Äî **Transcriptome / RNA-seq** family, **alternative / differential splicing** unit (TRANS-SPLICE-001): quantify how a gene's exons are spliced from RNA-seq reads with `TranscriptomeAnalyzer.CalculatePSI` / `DetectAlternativeSplicing`. **Percent-Spliced-In** `Œ® = I/(I+S)` (inclusion vs exclusion read support; Wang 2008, PMC3330053, SUPPA2) with opt-in **rMATS length-normalized** `œàÃÇ = (I/l·µ¢)/(I/l·µ¢ + S/l‚Çõ)` (Shen 2014); **ŒîPSI** = splicing-level differential readout. Classifies an event between **two isoforms of one gene** into the **five canonical AS classes** (Wang 2008 = rMATS SE/RI/A5SS/A3SS/MXE): SkippedExon, RetainedIntron, AlternativeFivePrimeSS (alternative **donor**), AlternativeThreePrimeSS (alternative **acceptor**), MutuallyExclusiveExons. Oracles: (80,20)‚Üí0.80, (80,20,200,100)‚Üí0.6666‚Ä¶. Edge cases: 0/0‚ÜíNaN, S=0‚Üí1, I=0‚Üí0, `0‚â§PSI‚â§1`, <2 isoforms ‚Üí no event. The **splicing-level counterpart** to the gene-level anchor [[differential-expression]] (a gene can be differentially spliced without changing total expression); self-normalizing ratio, so unlike [[expression-quantification]] it needs no TPM/library correction. **Distinct from** the genomic splice-site *motif* predictors [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] / [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] / [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]] (which score `GT`/`AG` sequence signals) ‚Äî cross-linked only to disambiguate. Two source-backed ASSUMPTIONs (length normalization opt-in; forward strand). Read-count ratio, **not** the full rMATS/SUPPA2 replicate statistics. Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[trans-splice-001-evidence]].
- [[gene-structure-prediction-intron-exon]] ‚Äî **splicing** family **composite / umbrella** (SPLICE-PREDICT-001): **gene structure prediction (intron/exon)** ‚Äî the integrative unit that **consumes** [[splice-donor-site-prediction]] + [[splice-acceptor-site-prediction]] and adds what neither boundary unit produces: **pairs** each `GT/GU` donor with an `AG` acceptor into an **intron** under the GT-AG rule (bounded by `minIntronLength` default 60 / `maxIntronLength`, **greedy non-overlapping** selection), then builds the whole model ‚Äî **exons** = the gaps, each **typed** Initial/Internal/Terminal/Single and carrying a reading-frame **phase** = `(Œ£ preceding exon lengths) mod 3`, the **spliced (mature) sequence** (introns removed), and an **overall score** = mean of per-intron `(donor.Score+acceptor.Score)/2` in [0,1]. U2 (GT-AG) / GC-AG / U12 (AT-AC) intron types; single-exon (intronless) genes ‚Üí 1 Single exon; empty ‚Üí empty structure. Sources Breathnach & Chambon 1981 + Shapiro & Senapathy 1987 + Burge 1999 + Wikipedia Intron/Exon/Gene-structure; all 4 assumptions RESOLVED (default branch-point 0.3 constant removed). Record [[splice-predict-001-evidence]].
- [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]] ‚Äî the **interpretation / annotation** member of the variant-analysis family (VARIANT-ANNOT-001): **VEP-style variant effect annotation** ‚Äî map an already-**called** variant to its **functional consequence** + **Sequence-Ontology term/accession** + **IMPACT** (HIGH/MODERATE/LOW/MODIFIER) via the Ensembl **OverlapConsequence predicate system**. **IMPACT is a stored property of the term, not computed**; **most-severe selection returns the lowest-rank term**. The coding engine **`depends_on`** [[genetic-code-translation]] ‚Äî **translates the ref/alt codons** (NCBI Standard code table 1) and compares peptides: `synonymous` / `missense` / `stop_gained` / `stop_lost` from `ref_pep` vs `alt_pep`, **`frameshift` purely length-based `|alt‚àíref| mod 3 ‚âÝ 0`**, inframe ins/del = √ó3 indel; precedence stop_gained>missense, start_lost(rank 7)>coding-substitution. Downstream of variant calling [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]], orthogonal to pathogenicity/tier classification. Sources McLaren 2016 (VEP) + Ensembl Constants.pm/VariationEffect.pm + NCBI gc.prt + Sequence Ontology. Two assumptions (Standard code table 1 only; single-codon SNV comparison, no NMD). Research-grade, not for clinical use. Record [[variant-annot-001-evidence]].
- [[germline-variant-calling-snp-indel]] ‚Äî the **calling / detection** member of the variant-analysis family (VARIANT-CALL-001): **variant calling** ‚Äî detect **SNP / insertion / deletion** (Danecek 2011: a variant is a difference from reference) by aligning a query to a reference (`CallVariantsFromAlignment` ‚Üí `SequenceAligner.GlobalAlign`) and reading out differing columns, then classify each SNP **Transition** (A‚ÜîG, C‚ÜîT) vs **Transversion** (A‚ÜîC/A‚ÜîT/G‚ÜîC/G‚ÜîT) and report **Ti/Tv** (undefined `#Tv=0`‚Üí0). In-memory `Variant` uses a `"-"` gap sentinel + 0-based position; VCF **padding base + 1-based POS** apply only to serialized `ToVcfLines`. **Upstream of** annotation [[variant-effect-annotation-vep]] (calling produces what VEP interprets); **`alternative_to`** the oncology tumor-vs-normal caller [[somatic-variant-calling-tumor-normal]] (same goal, different evidence). Assumptions: indels **not** left-aligned/parsimony-normalized (Tan 2015 ‚Äî position-only implementation-dependence in repeats), gap-sentinel internal rep, Ti/Tv zero‚Üí0. Alignment-based single-query comparison, **not** a read-pileup genotype caller. Sources VCFv4.3 + Danecek 2011 + Tan 2015 + Collins & Jukes 1994 + Acharya 2017 (Hamming). Research-grade, not for clinical use. Records [[variant-call-001-evidence]] + [[variant-snp-001-evidence]] (SNP facet: `FindSnps`/`FindSnpsDirect`, Hamming-mismatch enumeration, equal-length/common-prefix precondition) + [[variant-indel-001-evidence]] (indel facet: `FindInsertions`/`FindDeletions`, directional length invariant, Tan 2015 normalization theory).

## Gotchas

- [[research-grade-limitations]] ‚Äî beta, not for clinical use; simplified-subset implementations; internal-only validation.
